 <hr>
 <p align="CENTER"><font size="-1" color="GREEN"><i>Calvin's Commentaries, Vol. 12: Psalms, Part V</i>, tr. by John King, [1847-50], at sacred-texts.com</font></p><hr> <a name="xxxv"></a>  		
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv-p1"></a>A NEW TRANSLATION OF</p>  		
 <p class="BOOK-CHAP-BLU-24-CEN15"><a name="xxxv-p2"></a>THE BOOK OF PSALMS.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i"></a>  		  
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i-p1"></a></p>  		  
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i-p2"></a>PSALMS 1—35</p>  		  
 <p class="3rdLevelSmallCap12Bld37"><a name="xxxv.i-p3"></a>PART FIRST.  			  <a name="fr_311"></a><a href="#fn_311"><font size="1">312</font></a>
 </p>  <a name="xxxv.i.i"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.i-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.i-p2"></a>PSALM 1</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.i-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Blessed <i>is</i> the man who walketh not in the counsel of the ungodly; And in the way of sinners doth not stand; And in the seat of scoffers doth not sit:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.i-p4"></a><b>2 </b>But in the law of the Lord <i>is</i> his delight; And in his law doth he meditate day and night.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.i-p5"></a><b>3 </b>He shall be like a tree planted near rivers of waters, Which shall yield its fruit in its season, And whose leaf shall not fade; And all that he doeth shall prosper.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.i-p6"></a><b>4 </b>Not so the ungodly: But they are like the chaff, which scatter doth the wind.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.i-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Therefore shall not stand the ungodly in the judgment, Nor sinners in the assembly of the righteous.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.i-p8"></a><b>6 </b>For know doth Jehovah the way of the righteous; But the way of the ungodly shall perish.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.ii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p2"></a>PSALM 2</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Why tumultuously rise do the Gentiles, And the peoples murmur in vain?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Confederated have the kings of the earth, And the princes have assembled together, Against Jehovah and against his Christ.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>“Let us break asunder their bonds, “And cast away from us their yoke.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>He who dwelleth in heaven shall laugh; The Lord shall deride them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Then shall he speak to them in his wrath, And in his hot displeasure he shall vex them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p8"></a><b>6 </b>“I have anointed my king, “Upon Zion, the mountain of my holiness.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>I will declare the decree: Jehovah hath said to me, “My Son art thou; I, this day, have begotten thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>“Ask of me, and I will give thee the Gentiles for thy inheritance, “And for thy possession the uttermost parts of the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p11"></a><b>9 </b>“Thou shalt break them with a rod of iron;” As the vessel of a potter thou shalt dash them in pieces.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p12"></a><b>10 </b>And now, O ye kings! understand; Be instructed, O ye judges of the earth!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p13"></a><b>11 </b>Serve Jehovah with fear, Rejoice with trembling.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ii-p14"></a><b>12 </b>Kiss the Son, lest he be angry, And ye perish from the way, When shall be kindled in a short time his wrath. Blessed are all who trust in him.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.iii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p2"></a>PSALM 3</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p3"></a>A Psalm of David, when he fled from the face of Absalom his son</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Lord! how are my oppressors multiplied! Many rise up against me,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Many say to my soul, “There is no help for him in God.” Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>And thou, O Jehovah! art a shield for me; My glory, and he that exalteth my head.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>With my voice to the Lord have I cried, And he heard me from the mountain of his holiness. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>I lay down and slept; I awaked, because the Lord sustains me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>I will not be afraid of ten thousands of people, Who on all sides have set their camps against me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Arise, O Lord l Save me, O my God! For thou hast smitten all my enemies upon the cheekbone; The teeth of the ungodly thou hast broken.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>To the Lord belongeth salvation; Upon thy people <i>is</i> thy blessing. Selah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.iv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p2"></a>PSALM 4</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>When I cry, answer me, O God of my righteousness! In distress thou hast enlarged me; Have pity upon me, and hear my prayer.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>O ye sons of men! how long my glory will ye try to put to shame? Will ye love vanity, will ye seek after lying? Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>But know that chosen hath Jehovah the merciful man for himself: Jehovah will hear when I cry unto him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Tremble and ye shall not sin; Discourse in your heart upon your bed, and be silent. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Sacrifice the sacrifices of righteousness, And trust in the Lord.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Many say, “Who will show us good?” Lift thou up on us the light of thy countenance, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Thou hast given joy to my heart More than <i>theirs</i> in the time that their corn and their wine are increased.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.iv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>In peace [<i>as if</i>] with a multitude I will sleep and take rest,   				 <a name="fr_312"></a><a href="#fn_312"><font size="1">313</font></a>
  				 For thou, O Jehovah! in safety hast placed me, [<i>though</i>] alone.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.v"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.v-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.v-p2"></a>PSALM 5</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.v-p3"></a>To the Chief. Musician upon Nehiloth. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p4"></a><b>1 </b>My words do thou give ear to, O Jehovah! Attend to my speech.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Hearken to the voice of my cry, my King and my God! For to thee will I pray.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p6"></a><b>3 </b>O Jehovah! in the morning do thou hear my voice; In the morning will I direct to thee and will watch.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For not a God taking pleasure in wickedness art thou; There shall not dwell with thee evil.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p8"></a><b>5 </b>There shall not stand the foolish before thine eyes; Thou hatest all that commit iniquity.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Thou shalt destroy them that speak falsehood: The man of bloods and the deceitful man abominate shall Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p10"></a><b>7 </b>And I, in the multitude of thy mercy, will enter into thy house; I will worship in thy holy temple in thy fear.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p11"></a><b>8 </b>O Jehovah! lead me in thy righteousness, because of my adversaries; Make straight before my face thy way.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p12"></a><b>9 </b>For there is not in their mouth uprightness; Their inward part is deep depravity; A sepulcher that is open is their throat; With their tongues they deal deceitfully.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Cause them to err, O God! Let them fall from their counsels; In the multitude of their transgressions destroy them; For they have rebelled against thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p14"></a><b>11 </b>And rejoice let all those who trust in thee, For ever let them exult; and cover thou them, And let those delight in thee that love thy name.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.v-p15"></a><b>12 </b>For thou shalt bless the righteous, O Jehovah! With thy good will as with a shield thou shalt encompass them.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.vi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p2"></a>PSALM 6</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician on Neginoth, upon the Eighth. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! do not in thy anger rebuke me, And do not in thy wrath chastise me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Have mercy upon me, O Jehovah! for I am weak; Heal me, O Jehovah! for affrighted are my bones.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>And my soul is exceedingly afraid: And thou, O Jehovah! — how long? —</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Return, O Lord! deliver my soul; Save me for the sake of thy mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>For there is not in death any remembrance of thee; In the grave who shall acknowledge thee?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>I have become wearied with my groaning; I make to swim every night my bed; With my tears my couch I water.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Waxed dim for vexation hath mine eye; It hath become old among all my persecutors.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; For heard hath the Lord the voice of my weeping.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Heard hath the Lord my supplication; The Lord my prayer will receive.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Put to shame and confounded greatly be all my enemies; Let them turn back, and be ashamed suddenly.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.vii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p2"></a>PSALM 7</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p3"></a>Shiggaion of David, which he sung to Jehovah, upon the words<br> 				of Cush the Benjamite</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah, my God! in thee do I trust: Save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Lest He seize, as a lion, upon my soul, And tear it in pieces while there is none to deliver it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>O Jehovah, my God! if I have done this, If there be iniquity in my hands,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>If I have rewarded to him that was at peace with me evil, And have not delivered him that afflicted me without cause;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Pursue let the enemy my soul and take it, And let him cast down to the earth my life, And my glory in the dust let him hold down. Selah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Arise, O Jehovah! in thy anger; Lift up thyself against the fury of my enemies; And awake thou for me to the judgment which thou hast ordained.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>And the congregation of peoples shall be round about thee: And on account of this, do thou on high return.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Jehovah shall judge the peoples: Judge me, O Jehovah! according to my righteousness, And according to the integrity which is in me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Let come to an end, I pray, the malice of the wicked; And direct thou the righteous man: For he proves the hearts and the reins, the righteous God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>My shield is in God, Who saves the upright in heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>God judgeth the righteous man, And him who despiseth God, daily.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>If he turn not, his sword he will whet; His bow he hath bent, he hath made it ready.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>And for it he hath prepared the instruments of death; He shall make fit his arrows for the persecutors.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Behold! he shall travail to bring forth iniquity, And he hath conceived wickedness, And he shall bring forth falsehood.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p18"></a><b>15 </b>A pit he hath digged, and hollowed it out; And he hath fallen into the ditch which he hath made.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Return shall his wickedness upon his own head, And upon his own crown his violence shall descend.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.vii-p20"></a><b>17 </b>I will praise Jehovah, according to his righteousness; And I will sing to the name of Jehovah, Most High.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.viii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p2"></a>PSALM 8</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p3"></a>To the chief Musician upon Hagittith. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah, our Lord! How wonderful is thy name in all the earth, To set thy glory above the heavens!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Out of the mouths of babes and sucklings Thou hast founded <i>thy</i> strength, because of thy adversaries, To put to flight the enemy and the avenger.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>When! see thy heavens, the works of thy fingers; The moon and the stars which thou hast arranged:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>What is man that thou art mindful of him? And the son of man, that thou visitest him?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>For thou hast made him lower a little than God, And with glory and honor thou hast crowned him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Thou hast set him over the works of thy hands: All things thou hast put under his feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Sheep and oxen, all of them, And also the beasts of the fields;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>The fowl of the heavens, and the fish of the sea, And whatsoever passeth through the paths of the seas.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.viii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>O Jehovah, our Lord! How wonderful is thy name in all the earth!</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.ix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p2"></a>PSALM 9</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p3"></a>To the chief Musician upon Hagittith. Almuth Laben. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I will praise Jehovah with my whole heart; will recount all thy marvelous works.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p5"></a><b>2 </b>I will rejoice and exult in thee; I will celebrate in Psalms thy name, O thou Most high!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p6"></a><b>3 </b>When turned are my enemies backward, They fall and are put to flight at thy presence.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For thou hast maintained my judgment and my cause; Thou hast sat upon the throne a righteous judge.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Thou hast rebuked the heathen; Thou hast destroyed the ungodly; Their name thou hast blotted out for ever and ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p9"></a><b>6 </b>O thou enemy! come to an end are desolations for ever; And cities thou hast destroyed; Perished has their memory with them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p10"></a><b>7 </b>And Jehovah for ever sitteth: His throne for judgment lie hath prepared.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p11"></a><b>8 </b>And he shall judge the world in righteousness; He shall judge the peoples in rectitude.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p12"></a><b>9 </b>And Jehovah will be a place of defense to the poor, And a protection in seasonable times in trouble.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p13"></a><b>10 </b>And trust in thee shall those who know thy name: For thou forsakest not those who seek thee, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Sing psalms to Jehovah, who dwelleth in Zion, Proclaim among the peoples his doings;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p15"></a><b>12 </b>For in requiring blood, it lie hath remembered: He hath not forgotten the cry of the poor.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Have mercy upon me, O Jehovah! See my affliction from those who persecute me, O thou that liftest me up from the gates of death;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p17"></a><b>14 </b>That I may recount all thy praises in the gates of the daughter of Zion; That I may exult in thy salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p18"></a><b>15 </b>Sunk are the heathen into the pit which they have made; In the net which they have hid taken are their own feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Known is Jehovah by executing judgment: In the work of his own hands the wicked is snared. Higgaion Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p20"></a><b>17 </b>Turned shall be the wicked into hell: All the nations that forget God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p21"></a><b>18 </b>For not for ever shall be forgotten the poor; The hope of the humble shall not perish for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p22"></a><b>19 </b>Arise, O Jehovah! let not man prevail: Let the heathen be judged in thy sight.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.ix-p23"></a><b>20 </b>Put, O Jehovah! fear in them, That the heathen may know that mortal men they are. Selah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.x"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.x-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.x-p2"></a>PSALM 10</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Why, O Jehovah! standest thou afar off? And winkest at seasonable times in trouble?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p4"></a><b>2 </b>In his pride the ungodly doth persecute the poor; Let them be caught in the devices which they imagine.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p5"></a><b>3 </b>For praise himself doth the ungodly on account of the desire of his own soul; And the violent man blesseth himself: He despiseth Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p6"></a><b>4 </b>The ungodly, in the pride of his countenance doth not inquire; All his devices say, “There is not a God.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Prosperous are his ways at all times; High are thy judgments before him; At all his enemies he puffeth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p8"></a><b>6 </b>He saith in his heart, “I shall not be moved from generation to generation,” Because he is not in adversity,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p9"></a><b>7 </b>Of cursing his mouth is full, and of deceit, and of malice: Under his tongue are mischief and iniquity.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p10"></a><b>8 </b>He will sit in the ensnaring places of the villages; In his lurking places will he murder the innocent: His eyes against the poor will take their aim.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p11"></a><b>9 </b>He will lie in wait in secret, as a lion in his den; He will lie in wait to catch the poor; He will catch the poor by drawing him into his net.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p12"></a><b>10 </b>He will crouch low, he will cast himself down; Then shall fall by his strengths an army of the afflicted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p13"></a><b>11 </b>He hath said in his heart, “Forgotten it hath God; “He hideth his face, that he may not see it for ever.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p14"></a><b>12 </b>Arise, O Jehovah, God! lift up thy hand: Do not forget the poor.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p15"></a><b>13 </b>Why do the wicked despise God? He saith in his heart, “Thou wilt not require it.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p16"></a><b>14 </b>Thou hast seen <i>it</i>; For mischief and oppression thou considerest, That thou mayest take them into thy own hand: Upon thee shall the poor leave; To the orphan thou wilt be an helper.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p17"></a><b>15 </b>Break thou the arm of the wicked and the evil man; Thou shalt seek his wickedness, and shalt not find it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p18"></a><b>16 </b>Jehovah is King for ever and ever; Perished are the heathen out of his land.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p19"></a><b>17 </b>The desire of the needy thou hast heard, O Jehovah! Thou wilt direct their heart; Hear shall thine car:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.x-p20"></a><b>18 </b>That thou mayest judge the fatherless and the poor, That the man <i>who</i> is of earth may terrify no more.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p2"></a>PSALM 11</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p3"></a>To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>In Jehovah do I put my trust: How then say ye to my soul, “Flee ye into your mountain as a bird?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Surely behold! the ungodly shall bend the bow, They have made ready their arrows upon the string, shoot in secret at the upright in heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Truly, the foundations are destroyed: The righteous, what hath he done?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Jehovah is in the palace of his holiness; Jehovah in heaven <i>hath</i> his throne; His eyes behold, his eyelids consider the children of men.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Jehovah will approve the righteous man; But the ungodly and him who loveth iniquity, hate doth his soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>He will rain upon the ungodly snares, Fire and brimstone, and a storm of whirlwinds: This is the portion of their cup.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>For the righteous Jehovah loveth righteousness; His countenance approveth the upright.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p2"></a>PSALM 12</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician upon the Eighth. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Save me, O Jehovah! for failed hath the merciful man, For wasted away are the faithful from among the children of men.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Deceit doth every one speak with his neighbor; With lips of flatteries, with a double heart do they speak.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Let Jehovah cut off all lips of flatteries, The tongue that great things doth speak:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Those who have said, “By our tongues we will be strengthened; “Our lips are our own; who is lord over us?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>“Because of the spoiling of the needy, “Because of the groaning of the poor, “Now will I arise,” say will Jehovah, “I will set in safety him for whom <i>the wicked man</i> layeth snares.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>The words of Jehovah are pure words; Silver melted in an excellent crucible of earth, purified seven times.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Thou, O Jehovah! wilt keep them; Thou wilt preserve him from this generation for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>On every side the ungodly walk; When they are exalted, reproach is to the children of men.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p2"></a>PSALM 13</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p3"></a>To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>How long, O Jehovah! wilt thou forget me for ever? How long wilt thou hide thy face from me?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>How long shall I take counsel in my soul? And have sorrow in my heart daily? How long exalted shall be my enemy over me?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Look upon me, answer me, O Jehovah, my God! Enlighten my eyes, lest I sleep in death;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Lest my enemy say, “I have prevailed against him;” And those who afflict me rejoice if I should fall.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>But as for me, in thy goodness I trust; Exult shall my heart in thy salvation. I will sing to the Lord because he hath dealt bountifully with me.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p2"></a>PSALM 14</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>The fool hath said in his heart, “There is no God;” They have corrupted [<i>all good order</i>,] they have done abominable work. There is none that doeth good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Jehovah from heaven looked down Upon the children of men, To see whether there were any that did understand, And seek after God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Every one of them hath gone aside, Together putrid have they become: There is none that doeth good, not even one.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Have they no knowledge all these workers of iniquity? Who eat up my people as they eat bread. Upon the Lord they do not call.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>There did they tremble with fear, For God is in the generation of the righteous.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>The counsel of the poor ye deride, Because Jehovah is his hope.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xiv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Who shall give from Zion salvation to Israel? When turn back shall Jehovah the captivity of his people, Rejoice shall Jacob, and exult shall Israel.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p2"></a>PSALM 15</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p3"></a>A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! who shall dwell in thy tabernacle? Who shall rest in the mountain of thy holiness?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>He who walketh in integrity and doeth righteousness, And who speaketh truth in his heart,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>He who detracteth not with his tongue, Who doeth not to his companion evil, And a calumnious report doth not raise up against his neighbor.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Despised in his eyes is the off cast; But those who fear the Lord he honoreth; When he hath sworn to his own hurt he doth not change.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>His money he doth not put out to usury; And a present upon the innocent he doth not accept: He who doeth these things shall not be moved for ever.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p2"></a>PSALM 16</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p3"></a>Michtam. A Psalm Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Keep me, O God! <i>For</i> in thee do I trust.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Thou shalt say to Jehovah, “My Lord thou art; “My well doing <i>extendeth</i> not to thee.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>To the saints who are on the earth, And to the excellent; all my delight is in them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Multiplied shall be their sorrows who offer to a stranger; I will not taste their libations of blood, Nor will I take their names in my lips.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Jehovah is the portion of my inheritance, and of my cup; Thou maintainest my lot.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>The lines have fallen to me in pleasant <i>places</i>; Yea, an inheritance that is goodly hath fallen to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>I will magnify Jehovah, who giveth me counsel; Even in the nights instruct me do my reins.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>I have set Jehovah before me continually; Since he is at my right hand, I shall not be moved.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Therefore glad is my heart, rejoice doth my tongue; Also my flesh dwelleth in confidence.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>For thou wilt not leave my soul in the grave; Nor wilt thou make thy Holy One to see the pit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Thou wilt make known to me the way of life; Fullness of joy <i>is</i> in thy countenance; Pleasures <i>are</i> at thy right hand for evermore.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xvii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p2"></a>PSALM 17</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p3"></a>A Prayer of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Hear, O Jehovah! my righteousness; Attend to my cry; Hearken to my prayer, which is not in lips of deceit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>From the presence of thy countenance let my judgment go forth Let thine eyes behold uprightness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Thou hast proved my heart; Thou hast visited <i>it</i> by night; Thou hast examined <i>it</i>, thou shalt not find <i>any thing in it</i>; My thought shall not pass beyond my mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>As for the works of men, by the word of thy lips I have taken heed of the ways of the destroyer.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Uphold my steps in thy paths, That my footsteps may not slide.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>I have called upon thee, surely thou wilt hear me, O God! Incline thy ear to me, and hear my speech.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Make marvelous thy mercies, O thou Preserver of those who trust [<i>in thee</i>,] From those that exalt themselves against thy right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Keep me as the apple, the daughter of the eye; In the shadow of thy wings hide me,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>From the face of the ungodly who endeavor to destroy me — Of my enemies who in my soul besiege me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>In their own fat they have enclosed themselves; With their mouth they have spoken haughtily.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>In our steps they have now encompassed me; eyes they have set to east down to the ground.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>He is like a lion, he desireth to seize his prey, And like a lion’s whelp which lurketh in secret places.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Arise, O Jehovah! confront him, lay him prostrate; Deliver my soul from the ungodly man by thy sword</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>From men by thy hand, O Jehovah! — From men who are of long duration, Whose portion is in life, Whose belly thou fillets with thy secret, goods: Filled to the full are their children with them, And their residue they leave to their babes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xvii-p18"></a><b>15 </b>As for me in righteousness I shall behold thy face; I shall be satisfied when I shall awake with thy likeness.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xviii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p2"></a>PSALM 18</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Of the servant of Jehovah, David, who spake to Jehovah the words of this song, in the day that Jehovah delivered him from the hand of all his enemies, and from the hand of Saul. And he said,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I will love thee, O Jehovah! my strength;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Jehovah my rock, my fortress, and my deliverer; My God, my rock, I will hope in him: My shield and the horn of my salvation, my refuge.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Upon the praised Jehovah will I call; And from my enemies I shall be saved.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Encompassed me had the cords of death. The torrents of ungodliness had affrighted me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>The cords of the grave had encompassed me; Prevented me had the snares of death.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>In my distress I called upon Jehovah, And to my God I cried: And he heard from his temple my voice, And my cry before him came, [<i>even</i>] into his ears.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Then shake and tremble did the earth; And the foundations of the mountains were troubled and shaken, Because he was wroth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>There ascended smoke out of his nostrils, And fire <i>proceeding</i> from his mouth consumed; Coals were kindled by it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>And he bowed the heavens and descended; And thick darkness <i>was</i> under his feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>And he rode upon a cherub and flew; And was carried upon the wings of the wind.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>He made darkness his hiding place; Round about him his pavilion was dark waters, And the clouds of the skies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>At the brightness <i>which was</i> before him his clouds passed away, [<i>There were</i>] hail-storm, and coals of fire.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>And thunder in the heavens did Jehovah, And the Most High sent forth his voice; [<i>There were</i>] hailstorm and coals of fire.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>And he sent out his army and scattered them; And lightnings he multiplied, and put them into confusion.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p18"></a><b>15 </b>And seen were the abysses of the waters, And disclosed were the foundations of the world, At thy rebuke, O Jehovah! At the blast of the breath of thy nostrils.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p19"></a><b>16 </b>He sent from on high, he took me; He drew me from waters great.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p20"></a><b>17 </b>He delivered me from my enemy [<i>that was</i>] strong, And from my adversary; Because they were stronger than I.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p21"></a><b>18 </b>They had prevented me in the day of my calamity; And Jehovah was a support for me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p22"></a><b>19 </b>And he brought me forth into a wide place; He rescued me because he wished well to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p23"></a><b>20 </b>Rewarded me hath Jehovah according to my righteousness; According to the purity of my hands he hath repaid me;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p24"></a><b>21 </b>Because I have kept the ways of Jehovah, And have not impiously departed from my God;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p25"></a><b>22 </b>Because all his judgments <i>I have had</i> before me, And his statutes I have not removed from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p26"></a><b>23 </b>And I have been upright with him, And have kept me from my iniquity.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p27"></a><b>24 </b>And repaid me hath Jehovah according to my righteousness According to the purity of my hands before his eyes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p28"></a><b>25 </b>With the merciful thou wilt deal mercifully, With a man of uprightness thou wilt show thyself upright.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p29"></a><b>26 </b>With the pure thou wilt be pure, And with the perverse thou wilt deal perversely.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p30"></a><b>27 </b>For thou the afflicted people wilt save, And the haughty eyes thou wilt east down.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p31"></a><b>28 </b>For thou shalt light my lamp, O Jehovah! My God shall enlighten my darkness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p32"></a><b>29 </b>For by thee I shall break through the wedge of a troop, And by my God I shall leap over a wall.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p33"></a><b>30 </b>As for God perfect is his way; The word of Jehovah [<i>is</i>] refined; A shield is He to all who confide in him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p34"></a><b>31 </b>For who is God besides Jehovah? And who is strong except our God?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p35"></a><b>32 </b>It is God who hath girded me with strength, And hath made perfect my way.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p36"></a><b>33 </b>He maketh my feet like <i>those</i> of hinds, And upon my high places he hath set me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p37"></a><b>34 </b>He traineth my hands to the battle, And broken will be a bow of steel by my arms.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p38"></a><b>35 </b>And thou hast given me the shield of thy salvation, And thy right hand hath sustained me, And thy clemency hath increased me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p39"></a><b>36 </b>Thou hast enlarged my steps under me, And my ankles shall not totter.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p40"></a><b>37 </b>I will pursue my enemies and will seize them; Nor will I return until I have consumed them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p41"></a><b>38 </b>I have afflicted them, and they were not able to rise; They have fallen under my feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p42"></a><b>39 </b>Thou hast girded me with might for the battle; Thou hast bowed down my enemies under me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p43"></a><b>40 </b>And of my enemies thou hast given me the neck, And [<i>as for</i>] my haters I will destroy them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p44"></a><b>41 </b>They shall cry aloud, and <i>there shall</i> <i>be</i> no Savior <i>for them</i>; To Jehovah, but he shall not answer them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p45"></a><b>42 </b>And I will bruise them to powder as dust before the wind; As the mire of the streets I will tread upon them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p46"></a><b>43 </b>Thou shalt deliver me from the contentions of the people; Thou shalt make me head of the nations; A people whom I have not known shall serve me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p47"></a><b>44 </b>At the hearing of the ear they shall obey me; The children of strangers shall lie to me;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p48"></a><b>45 </b>The children of strangers shall lose courage, And tremble from within their places of concealment.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p49"></a><b>46 </b>Let Jehovah live and blessed <i>be</i> my strength, And let the God of my salvation be exalted:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p50"></a><b>47 </b>The God who giveth vengeance for me, And subdueth peoples under me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p51"></a><b>48 </b>My deliverer from my enemies: Yea, from those who had risen up against me thou hast lifted me up: From the man of violence thou hast rescued me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p52"></a><b>49 </b>Therefore will I praise thee, O Jehovah! among the Gentiles, And to thy name will I sing.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xviii-p53"></a><b>50 </b>Who worketh great deliverances for his king, And showeth mercy to his anointed, [even to] David, And to his seed for ever.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p2"></a>PSALM 19</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p4"></a><b>1 </b>The heavens recount the glory of God; And the works of his hands proclaim doth the expanse.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Day unto day poureth forth speech; And night unto night publisheth knowledge.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p6"></a><b>3 </b>There is no speech and no language, Where is not heard their voice.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Through all the earth hath gone forth their writing, And to the extremity of the world their words: For the sun he hath set a tabernacle in them,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p8"></a><b>5 </b>And he as a bridegroom goeth forth from his chamber; He exulteth as a strong man to run <i>his</i> course.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p9"></a><b>6 </b>From <i>one</i> extremity of the heavens <i>is</i> his going forth, And his circuit to the utmost limits thereof, And no <i>person</i> is hidden from his heat.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p10"></a><b>7 </b>The law of the Lord is perfect, restoring the soul; The testimony of Jehovah is faithful, instructing in wisdom the babes;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p11"></a><b>8 </b>The statutes of Jehovah <i>are</i> right, rejoicing the heart; The commandment of the Lord <i>is</i> pure, enlightening the eyes;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p12"></a><b>9 </b>The fear of Jehovah is clean, enduring for ever; The judgments of Jehovah are truth, they are justified together.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p13"></a><b>10 </b>More desirable [<i>are they</i>] than gold, and much fine gold; And sweeter than honey, and the dropping of honeycombs.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Moreover, thy servant is made circumspect by them; And in their observance the reward <i>is</i> great.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p15"></a><b>12 </b>His errors who can understand? From my hidden <i>sins</i> cleanse thou me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Likewise from presumptuous sins restrain thou thy servant, That they may not have dominion over me; Then upright shall I be and clean from much wickedness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xix-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart be acceptable Before thee, O Jehovah! my strength and my Redeemer.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xx"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p2"></a>PSALM 20</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p4"></a><b>1 </b>May Jehovah hear thee in the day of trouble!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p5"></a><b>2 </b>May he send help to thee from the sanctuary! And out of Zion sustain thee!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p6"></a><b>3 </b>May he be mindful of all thy offerings! And thy holocaust may he make flit! Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p7"></a><b>4 </b>May he give to thee according to thy heart! And all thy counsel may he fulfill!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p8"></a><b>5 </b>That we may exult in thy salvation, And in the name of our God erect a banner, When Jehovah shall fulfill all thy petitions.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Now I have known that Jehovah hath saved his anointed; He will hear him from the heavens of his sanctuary, In the mightiness of the salvation of his right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Some <i>trust</i> in chariots, and some in horses; But the name of Jehovah our God we will remember.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p11"></a><b>8 </b>They are bowed down and fallen; But we are risen up and stand erect.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xx-p12"></a><b>9 </b>O Jehovah! do thou save; Let the King hear us in the day that we call upon him.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p2"></a>PSALM 21</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! in thy strength rejoice shall the king, And in thy salvation how greatly shall he exult!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>The desire of his heart thou hast given him, And what he uttered with his lips, thou hast not denied <i>him</i>. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For thou shalt prevent him with blessings of good; Thou shalt place upon his head a crown of gold.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Life he asked from thee; Thou hast given him length of days for ever and ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Great <i>is</i> his glory in thy salvation: Splendor and beauty thou hast put upon him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>For thou hast set him [<i>to be</i>] blessings for ever: Thou hast gladdened him with joy before thy countenance.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>For the king trusteth in Jehovah; And through the goodness of the Most High, he shall not be moved</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Find out shall thy hand all thy enemies; Thy right hand shall find out thy haters.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Thou shalt put them as in a furnace of fire in the time of thy wrath, O Jehova! In his wrath he shall overwhelm them, And consume them shall the fire.</p>  			 
 <p class="BibleVerse39"><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Their fruit from the earth thou wilt destroy, And their seed from among the sons of men.</p>  			 
 <p class="BibleVerse39"><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>For they have spread out against thee evil; They have devised against thee a stratagem which they could not accomplish.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>For thou wilt set them as a butt; On thy strings thou shalt make ready <i>thy arrows</i> against their faces.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxi-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Be thou exalted, O Jehovah! in thy strength, <i>Then</i> we will sing and celebrate in psalms thy power.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p2"></a>PSALM 22</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Upon the hind of the morning. A Psalm Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>My God! my God! why hast thou forsaken me? [<i>Why art thou</i>] far from my help, from the words of my roaring?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>O my God! I cry by day, and thou dost not hear: And in the night, and am not silent.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Yet thou art holy, Inhabiting the praises of Israel.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>In thee trust did our fathers: They trusted, and thou didst deliver them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>To thee they cried, and were saved: In thee they trusted, and were not put to shame.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>But I <i>am</i> a worm, and not a man; The reproach of men, and despised of the people.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>All who see me scoff at me: They thrust out the lip, they shake the head.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>“He hath devolved,” <i>say they</i>, “upon Jehovah, <i>his</i> cause, let him rescue him, “Let him deliver him, since he hath a favor for him.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Surely it is thou who didst take me out of the womb, Causing me to confide upon the breasts of my mother.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Upon thee I was cast from the womb: From the belly of my mother my God art thou.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Depart not far from me, for trouble is near, For there is no helper.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Encompassed me have bulls [<i>that are</i>] strong, The bulls of Bashan have beset me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>They have opened upon me their mouth, As a lion ravening and roaring.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Like water I have flowed,   				 <a name="fr_313"></a><a href="#fn_313"><font size="1">314</font></a>
  				 And disjointed have been   				 <a name="fr_314"></a><a href="#fn_314"><font size="1">315</font></a>
  				 all my bones: My heart hath been   				 <a name="fr_315"></a><a href="#fn_315"><font size="1">316</font></a>
  				 like wax, It hath been   				 <a name="fr_316"></a><a href="#fn_316"><font size="1">317</font></a>
  				 melted in the midst of my bowels.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p22"></a><b>15 </b>Dried up as a potsherd hath been   				 <a name="fr_317"></a><a href="#fn_317"><font size="1">318</font></a>
  				 my strength, And my tongue cleaveth to my jaws; And to the dust of death thou hast brought me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p24"></a><b>16 </b>For encompassed me have dogs; The assembly of the wicked have surrounded me: They have pierced my hands and my feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p25"></a><b>17 </b>I will count all my bones; As for them they look and gaze upon me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p26"></a><b>18 </b>They divide my garments among them; Upon my vesture they cast the lot.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p27"></a><b>19 </b>And thou, O Jehovah! be not far from me; <i>Thou who art</i> my strength, to my aid hasten.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p28"></a><b>20 </b>Rescue from the sword my soul; From the hand of the dog my only one.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p29"></a><b>21 </b>Save me from the mouth of the lion, And from the horns of unicorns do thou hear me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p30"></a><b>22 </b>I will declare thy name to my brethren; In the midst of the assembly will I praise thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p31"></a><b>23 </b><i>Saying</i>, “Ye who fear Jehovah praise him: “All ye the seed of Jacob glorify him: “And stand in awe of him, all ye the seed of Israel.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p32"></a><b>24 </b>“For he hath not despised nor disdained the poor; “Nor hath he hidden his face from him; “And when he cried to him, he heard him.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p33"></a><b>25 </b>From thee shall proceed my praise in the congregation great; My vows will I pay before them that fear him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p34"></a><b>26 </b>Eat shall the poor, and be satisfied; They shall praise Jehovah who seek him; Your heart shall live for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p35"></a><b>27 </b>Remember and turn to Jehovah shall all the ends of the earth; And prostrate themselves before his face shall all the tribes of the Gentiles.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p36"></a><b>28 </b>For Jehovah’s is the kingdom, That he may have dominion among the Gentiles.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p37"></a><b>29</b> Eat and worship shall all the fat ones of the earth: Before his face shall bow all who are going down to the dust; And he who his own soul doth not quicken.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p38"></a><b>30 </b><i>Their</i> seed shall serve him, It shall be registered to the Lord for a generation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxii-p39"></a><b>31 </b>They shall come and shall declare his righteousness, To a people that shall be born, because he hath done [<i>this</i>.],</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p2"></a>PSALM 23</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p3"></a>A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Jehovah is my shepherd, therefore I shall not want any thing.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>In pastures of grass he maketh me to lie down; To waters gently flowing he leadeth me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>My soul he restoreth: He leadeth me by the paths of righteousness for his name’s sake.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Though I should walk in the valley of the shadow of death, I will not fear evil, because thou art with me; Thy staff and thy crook they comfort me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Thou wilt prepare before me a table in the presence of my persecutors; Thou wilt anoint with oil my head; My cup overfloweth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life, And I shall dwell in the house of Jehovah for a length of days.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p2"></a>PSALM 24</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p3"></a>A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Jehovah’s is the earth, and the fullness thereof; The world, and those who dwell therein.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>For he upon the seas hath founded it, And upon the floods he hath arranged it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Who shall ascend into the mountain of Jehovah? Who shall stand in the place of his holiness?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>He who is clean in hands and pure in heart, Who hath not lifted up to vanity his soul, And hath not sworn deceitfully.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>He shall receive blessing from Jehovah, And righteousness from the God of his salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>This is the generation of those who seek him, Of those who seek thy face, O Jacob! Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Lift up, O ye gates! your heads, And be ye lifted up, ye doors everlasting! And enter shall the King of Glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Who is this King of Glory? Jehovah strong and mighty, Jehovah mighty in power.   				 <a name="fr_318"></a><a href="#fn_318"><font size="1">319</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p13"></a><b>9 </b>Lift up, O ye gates! your heads, Lift up, I say, ye doors everlasting! <i>And</i> enter shall the King of Glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxiv-p14"></a><b>10 </b>Who is this King of Glory? Jehovah of armies — He is the King of Glory. Selah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p2"></a>PSALM 25</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>To thee, O Jehovah! my soul have I lifted up.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>O my God! in thee have I hoped: Let me not be put to shame, Let not my enemies rejoice over me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Yea none who wait on thee shall be put to shame: They shall be ashamed who deal perfidiously without cause.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Thy ways, O Jehovah! make me to know, Thy paths teach thou me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Direct me in thy truth, and teach me; For thou art the God of my salvation; For thee I have waited all the day.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Remember thy compassions, O Jehovah! And thy loving-kindnesses; for they have been from everlasting.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>The transgressions of my youth, and my iniquities do not thou remember According to thy clemency remember thou me, For the sake of thy goodness, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Good and upright <i>is</i> Jehovah, Therefore he will teach sinners in the way.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>He will guide the poor in judgment, And will teach the poor his way.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>All the ways of Jehovah are mercy and truth, To those who keep his covenant and his testimony.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>For the sake of thy name, O Jehovah! Be merciful to my iniquity, for great is it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Who is the man that feareth Jehovah? He will teach him in the way which he should choose.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p16"></a><b>13 </b>His soul in good shall dwell, And his seed shall inherit the land.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p17"></a><b>14 </b>The counsel of Jehovah is to those who fear him, That he may make known to them his covenant.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p18"></a><b>15 </b>My eyes are continually towards Jehovah, For he will bring out of the net my feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Have respect to me, take pity upon me, For solitary and poor am I.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p20"></a><b>17 </b>The afflictions of my heart are enlarged; Out of my distresses do thou bring me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Behold my affliction and my travail, And take away all my sins.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p22"></a><b>19 </b>Behold my enemies, for they are multiplied; And with a violent hatred they hate me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p23"></a><b>20 </b>Guard my soul, and rescue me, That I may not be ashamed; For I have trusted in thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p24"></a><b>21 </b>Let integrity and rectitude preserve me; Because I have waited for thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxv-p25"></a><b>22 </b>Redeem O God! Israel from all his troubles.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p2"></a>PSALM 26</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Judge me, O Jehovah: Because in my integrity I have walked, And in Jehovah have trusted, I shall not stumble.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Prove me, O Jehovah! and try me, Examine my reins and my heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For thy goodness <i>is</i> before my eyes; Therefore I have walked in thy truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>I have not sat with men of vanity, And with crafty men I will not go in.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>I hate the assembly of transgressors, And with the wicked I will not sit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>I will wash in purity my hands, And will encompass thy altar, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>To cause to be heard the voice of praise, And to tell of all thy marvelous deeds.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>O Jehovah! I have loved the habitation of thy house, And the place of the dwelling of thy glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Gather not with ungodly men, my soul, Nor with men of bloods my life.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>For in their hands <i>is</i> maliciousness, And their right hand is full of bribes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>But as for me in my integrity I will walk: Redeem me, and have mercy upon me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>My foot hath stood in uprightness: In the congregations will I bless thee, O Jehovah!</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxvii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p2"></a>PSALM 27</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Jehovah is my light and my salvation, Whom shall I fear? Jehovah <i>is</i> the strength of my life, Of whom shall I be afraid?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>When approach against me did the wicked, To devour my flesh — My oppressors and my enemies against me — They stumbled and fell.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>If there should encamp against me a camp, My heart shall not fear: If there should rise against me war, In this shall I have confidence.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>One thing have I requested from Jehovah — This will I follow after — That I may dwell in the house of Jehovah all the days of my life, To behold the beauty of Jehovah, To survey his temple.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>For he shall hide me in his pavilion in the day of evil; He shall conceal me in the secret [<i>recess</i>] of his tent, Upon a rock he will set me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>And now he shall exalt my head Above my enemies who surround me: And I will sacrifice in his tabernacle sacrifices of triumph; I will sing and will celebrate in psalms Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Hear, O Jehovah! my voice with which I cry; Have mercy upon me and answer me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>To thee my heart hath said, “Seek ye my face;” Therefore thy face, O Jehovah! will I seek.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Hide not thy face from me; Cast not away in wrath thy servant: My strength thou hast been, do not desert me, And do not forsake me, O God of my salvation!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>When my father and my mother shall forsake me, Jehovah shall receive me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Teach me, O Jehovah! thy way, And lead me in the path of rectitude because of my enemies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Do not deliver me to the desire of my oppressors, For risen up against me have false witnesses, And he who uttereth violence.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Unless I had believed to see the goodness of Jehovah, in the land of the living —.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxvii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Wait thou on Jehovah; Be strong, and he will comfort thy heart, And wait thou on Jehovah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxviii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p2"></a>PSALM 28</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Unto thee, O Jehovah! will I cry; O my strength! hold not thy peace from me Lest if thou shouldst be silent to me, I then become like those who descend into the grave.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Hear the voice of my prayers when I cry to thee, When I lift up my hands to the sanctuary of thy holiness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Draw me not away with ungodly men, And with the workers of iniquity, Who speak peace   				 <a name="fr_319"></a><a href="#fn_319"><font size="1">320</font></a>
  				 with their neighbors, When in their hearts is malice.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p8"></a><b>4 </b>Give them according to their works, And according to the wickedness of their doings: According to the work of their hands give them, Render their reward to them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p9"></a><b>5 </b>Because they do not consider the doing of Jehovah, Nor the work of his hands, Let him destroy them and not build them up.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p10"></a><b>6 </b>Blessed <i>be</i> Jehovah! For he hath heard the voice of my supplications.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p11"></a><b>7 </b>Jehovah <i>is</i> my strength and my shield; In him trusted hath my heart, and I have been helped: Therefore exult shall my heart, And with my song will I celebrate him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Jehovah <i>is</i> strength to them, And the strength of the salvations of his Anointed <i>is</i> He.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxviii-p13"></a><b>9 </b>Save thy people, and bless thy inheritance; Feed them and exalt them for ever.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p2"></a>PSALM 29</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p3"></a>A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Ascribe to Jehovah: ye sons of the mighty — Ascribe to Jehovah glory and strength.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Ascribe to Jehovah the glory of his name; Worship before Jehovah in the brightness of his sanctuary.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p6"></a><b>3 </b>The voice of Jehovah is upon the waters; The God of glory thundereth; Jehovah is upon the waters great.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p7"></a><b>4 </b>The voice of Jehovah is in strength, The voice of Jehovah is in majesty.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p8"></a><b>5 </b>The voice of Jehovah breaketh the cedars; Break, I say, doth Jehovah the cedars of Lebanon.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p9"></a><b>6 </b>And he maketh Lebanon to leap like a calf, And Sirion like the son of the unicorns.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p10"></a><b>7 </b>The voice of Jehovah striketh out flames of fire.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p11"></a><b>8 </b>The voice of Jehovah maketh the desert to tremble. Jehovah maketh to tremble the desert of Kadesh.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p12"></a><b>9 </b>The voice of Jehovah maketh the hinds to bring forth, And discovereth the forests, And all <i>meanwhile</i> in his temple speak his praise.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Jehovah over the flood presideth, Preside, I say, doth Jehovah [<i>as</i>] King for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxix-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Jehovah strength to his people will give; Jehovah will bless his people with peace.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxx"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p2"></a>PSALM 30</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p3"></a>A Psalm of a Song at the dedication of the house of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I will exalt thee, O Jehovah! for thou hast raised me up, And hast not made glad my enemies over me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p5"></a><b>2 </b>O Jehovah, my God! I have cried to thee, And thou hast healed me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p6"></a><b>3 </b>O Jehovah! thou hast brought up from the grove my soul; Thou hast quickened me from among those who descend into the pit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Sing to Jehovah, O ye his meek ones! And acknowledge the memorial of his holiness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p8"></a><b>5 </b>For <i>there is only</i> a moment in his anger, <i>But</i> life in his favor: In the evening will lodge weeping, And in the morning shall come exultation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p9"></a><b>6 </b>But as for me I had said in my tranquillity, “I shall not be moved for ever.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p10"></a><b>7 </b>O Jehovah! in thy good pleasure Thou hast established strength to my mountain; Thou didst hide thy face, I was confounded.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p11"></a><b>8 </b>O Jehovah! to thee I cried, And to my Lord I made supplication.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p12"></a><b>9 </b>What profit shall there be in my blood, When I descend into the pit? Celebrate thee shall the dust? Shall it proclaim thy truth?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Hear, O Jehovah! and have mercy upon me; O Jehovah! be thou a helper to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Thou hast turned my mourning into dancing for me; Thou hast loosed my sackcloth, And girded me with gladness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxx-p15"></a><b>12 </b>That celebrate thee in psalms may my glory, and not be silent: O Jehovah, my God! for ever will I celebrate thee.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxxi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p2"></a>PSALM 31</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician,. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>In thee, O Jehovah! have I trusted, Let me not be put to shame for ever: In thy righteousness deliver me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Incline to me thy ear, Speedily do thou rescue me; Be to me for a rock of strength, For a house of defense to save me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For my rock, and my fortress <i>art</i> thou: And for the sake of thy name thou wilt direct and guide me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Extricate me from the net, which they have hidden for me, For thou art my strength.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Into thy hand I will commend my spirit; For thou hast redeemed me, O Jehovah! God of truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>I hate all those who regard lying vanities; But as for me in Jehovah I have trusted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>I will exult and rejoice in thy goodness; Because thou hast looked upon my affliction: Thou hast known in distresses my soul:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>And thou hast not shut me up in the hand of the enemy: <i>But</i> thou hast set at large my feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Have pity upon me, O Jehovah! for trouble is to me: My eye hath consumed away for vexation; my soul and my belly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>My life hath riffled through grid; And my years with groaning: My strength hath sunk through my sorrow, And my bones have moldered away.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>On account of all my enemies I was a reproach, Yea to my neighbors exceedingly, And a terror to my acquaintances; And those who saw me abroad fled from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>I was forgotten as a dead man from the heart; I became like a vessel [<i>that is</i>] broken.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p16"></a><b>13 </b>For I have heard the slander of many: Fear <i>hath seized</i> me on every side, While they consult together against me, And to take away my life do devise.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p17"></a><b>14 </b>But as for me, in thee have I trusted, O Jehovah! I have said, “My God art thou.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p18"></a><b>15 </b>In thy hand are my times; Rescue me from the hand of my enemies, And from those who persecute me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Cause to shine upon thy servant thy face, Save me in thy goodness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p20"></a><b>17 </b>O Jehovah! let me not be put to shame, For I have called upon thee: Let the wicked be put to shame, Let Gem be silent in the grave.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Let the lips of lying be put to shame, Which speak against the righteous a hard thing in pride and scorn.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p22"></a><b>19 </b>How great is thy goodness, Which thou hast hidden for those who fear thee! Which thou hast performed for those who confide in thee, Before the sons of men!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p23"></a><b>20 </b>Thou shalt hide them in the hidden place of thy presence, From the prides of man; Thou shalt conceal them <i>as</i> in a tent, From the strife of tongues.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p24"></a><b>21 </b>Blessed be Jehovah! For he hath made wonderful his goodness towards me, As in a city fortified.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p25"></a><b>22 </b>But as for me, I had said in my fear, “I am cast away from before thy eyes:” Yet truly thou hast heard the voice of my supplications, When I cried unto thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p26"></a><b>23 </b>Love Jehovah, all ye meek ones of his! The faithful preserve doth Jehovah, And he repayeth plentifully him who behaveth proudly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxi-p27"></a><b>24</b> Be of good courage, and he shall strengthen your heart, All ye who hope in Jehovah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxxii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p2"></a>PSALM 32</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p3"></a>Of David. Giving instruction</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Blessed are those to whom is remitted iniquity, And whose transgression is covered.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Blessed is the man to whom Jehovah doth not impute iniquity, And in whose spirit there is not guile.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>When I kept silence, waste away did my bones, And when I wailed all the day.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For by day and night heavy upon me was thy hand; Turned into the drought of summer was my greenness. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>My sin I have acknowledged to thee, And my iniquity I have not hid. I said, “I will confess against myself my wickedness to Jehovah;” And thou didst remit the guilt of my sin. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>On this account, pray to thee shall every <i>man</i>, that is meek, In the time of finding thee: So that in a flood of many waters, To him they shall not come near.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Thou art a hiding-place to me; From trouble thou shalt preserve me; With songs of deliverance thou shalt encompass me. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>I will instruct thee, And teach thee the way wherein thou shouldest walk: I will counsel thee with mine eye.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Be ye not like a horse, <i>or</i> like a mule, Which have not understanding: With bit and bridle his jaws thou shalt bind, Lest they kick against thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Many sorrows <i>shall</i> <i>be</i> to the wicked: But the man who hopeth in Jehovah goodness shall encompass.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Rejoice in Jehovah, and exult, ye righteous! Sing all ye <i>who are</i> upright in heart.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p2"></a>PSALM 33</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Exult, ye righteous! in Jehovah: For to the upright comely is praise.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Celebrate Jehovah upon the harp; Upon the nablure,   				 <a name="fr_320"></a><a href="#fn_320"><font size="1">321</font></a>
  				 and instrument of ten strings, sing psalms to him</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Sing to him a song that is new; Ardently sing with shouting.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For right <i>is</i> the word of Jehovah, And all his works are in faithfulness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>He loveth righteousness and judgment: Of the goodness of Jehovah fill is the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>By the word of Jehovah the heavens were established, And by the breath of his mouth all their host.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>He gathered together as an heap the waters of the sea; He laid up as in treasure houses the deeps.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Let all the earth fear Jehovah; Of him let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>For he spake, and it was; He commanded, and it stood.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Jehovah scattereth the counsel of the Gentiles, He rendereth fruitless the imaginations of the peoples.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>The counsel of Jehovah for ever shall stand, The thoughts of his heart from age to age.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Blessed is the people to whom Jehovah is their God, The people whom he hath chosen for: in inheritance to himself.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>From heavens looked down hath Jehovah, He hath beheld all the sons of Adam.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>From the dwelling place of His throne, He hath looked on all the inhabitants of the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p18"></a><b>15 </b>He who hath fashioned together their hearts, Who understandeth all their works.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p19"></a><b>16 </b>There is not a king saved by the multitude of an host, Nor a giant rescued by greatness of strength.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p20"></a><b>17 </b>Fallacious is a horse for safety, And by the greatness of his strength he will not deliver.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Behold! the eye of Jehovah is upon those who fear him, [<i>Upon those</i>] who hope in his mercy;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p22"></a><b>19 </b>To rescue from death their souls, To keep them alive in famine.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p23"></a><b>20 </b>Our soul waiteth for Jehovah: Our help and our shield is he.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p24"></a><b>21 </b>Surely in him rejoice shall our heart, Because in his holy name we will trust.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p25"></a><b>22 </b>Let thy mercy be upon us, O Jehovah! According as we have trusted in thee.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p2"></a>PSALM 34</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p3"></a>Of David when he changed his countenance before Abimelech, who expelled him, and he departed</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I will bless Jehovah at all times: Continually his praise <i>shall be</i> in my mouth.</p>
