 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>In Jehovah make her boast shall my soul: Hear shall the humble and be glad.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Magnify? Jehovah with me, And let us exalt his name together.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>I sought. Jehovah, and he answered me, And from all my fears he delivered me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>They shall look to him, and shall flow to him, And their faces shall not he ashamed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>This poor man cried,: and Jehovah heard him, And from all his distresses saved him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Encamp doth the angel of Jehovah about those who fear him, And will deliver them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Taste ye and see that good is Jehovah: Blessed is the man who trusteth in him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Fear Jehovah, ye saints of his; For nothing is lacking to those who fear him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>The young lions suffer want and are famished: But those who fear Jehovah shall not want any good thing.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Come ye children, hearken to me, The fear of Jehovah I will teach you.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Who is the man that desireth life, Loving days in which he may see good?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Keep thy tongue from evil, And thy lips from speaking deceit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Depart from evil, and do good; Seek peace, and pursue it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p18"></a><b>15 </b>The eyes of Jehovah <i>are</i> upon the righteous, And his ears [<i>are open</i>] to their cry.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p19"></a><b>16 </b>The face of Jehovah is upon those who do evil, To blot out from the earth their remembrance.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p20"></a><b>17 </b>They cried, and Jehovah heard <i>them</i>, And from all their distresses he delivered them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Near is Jehovah to the broken in heart; The contrite in spirit he will save.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p22"></a><b>19 </b>Many <i>are</i> the afflictions of the righteous; But from them all deliver him will Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p23"></a><b>20 </b>He keepeth all his bones: One of them is not broken.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p24"></a><b>21 </b>That malice shall slay the wicked, And those who hate the righteous shall be destroyed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p25"></a><b>22 </b>Redeem doth, Jehovah the soul of his servants, And they shall not perish who confide in him.</p>  <a name="xxxv.i.xxxv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p2"></a>PSALM 35</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Plead, O Jehovah! with those who plead with me, Fight against those who fight against me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Lay hold on shield and buckler, And rise up to my aid.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Draw out the spear, and stop my ears against my persecutors: Say to my soul, “Thy salvation am I.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Let those be confounded and put to shame Who seek my soul, Let those be turned back and be abashed Who devise my hurt.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Let them be as chaff before the wind? And let the angel of Jehovah drive them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Let their way be darkness and slipperiness; And let the angel of Jehovah pursue them:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>For without a cause they have hid for me the pitfall of their net,   				 <a name="fr_321"></a><a href="#fn_321"><font size="1">322</font></a>
  				 Without a cause they have digged a pit for my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Let there come upon him confusion of which he is not aware; And let the net which he hath hidden catch him; With confusion let him fall into it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p13"></a><b>9 </b>And my soul hath exulted in Jehovah, It shall rejoice in his salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p14"></a><b>10 </b>All my bones shall say, “O Jehovah! who is like to thee, “Rescuing the poor from him who is too strong for him, “The poor and wretched from his spoiler?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p15"></a><b>11 </b>Rise up do witnesses [<i>that are</i>] violent; Things which I have not known they ask me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p16"></a><b>12 </b>They repay me evil for good, To the bereaving of my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p17"></a><b>13 </b>But as for me, in their sickness my clothing was sackcloth: I afflicted by fasting my soul; And my prayer upon my own bosom was turned.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p18"></a><b>14 </b>As if he had been a friend, as if a brother to me, I behaved myself <i>towards him</i>: As he who mourneth heavily for his mother I humbled myself.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p19"></a><b>15 </b>But they at my halting rejoiced, they were assembled together: Assembled together, I say, against me, were the abjects whom I had not known: They have torn with their lips and have not been silent.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p20"></a><b>16 </b>Among perfidious jesters at feasts, They gnash upon me with their teeth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p21"></a><b>17 </b>O Lord! how long wilt thou behold it? Rescue my soul from their violence, From the lions my only one.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p22"></a><b>18 </b>I will celebrate thee in the congregation great: Among people many I will praise thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p23"></a><b>19 </b>Let not those rejoice over me, who unjustly are my enemies; Nor let those who hate me without a cause wink with the eye.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p24"></a><b>20 </b>For peace they speak not;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p25"></a><b>21 </b>They have opened against me their mouth; They have said, “Aha! aha! seen <i>it</i> hath our eye.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p26"></a><b>22 </b>Thou hast seen <i>it</i> <i>also</i>, O Jehovah: Be not silent, O Lord! be not far from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p27"></a><b>23 </b>Arouse thyself, and awake for my judgment, My God! and my Lord! to my cause.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p28"></a><b>24 </b>Judge me according to thy righteousness, O Jehovah, my God! And let them not rejoice over me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p29"></a><b>25 </b>Let them not say in their heart, “Aha! our soul!” Let them not say “We have destroyed him.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p30"></a><b>26 </b>Let those be ashamed and confounded together, Who rejoice at my calamity; Let those be clothed with shame and ignominy, Who magnify themselves against me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p31"></a><b>27 </b><i>But</i> let those shout and rejoice, who favor my righteousness: And let them say continually, “Magnified be Jehovah! “Who loveth the peace of his servant.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.i.xxxv-p32"></a><b>28 </b>And my tongue shall speak of thy righteousness; All the day of thy praise.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii"></a>  		  
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii-p1"></a></p>  		  
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii-p2"></a>PSALMS 36—66</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.i"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p2"></a>PSALM 36</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Of the servant of Jehovah, [even] of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Ungodliness saith to the wicked man in the midst of my heart, There is no fear of God before his eyes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p5"></a><b>2 </b>For he flattereth himself in his own eyes, Until his iniquity be found to be hateful.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p6"></a><b>3 </b>The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit, He teaseth to understand that he may do good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Iniquity he meditates upon his bed; He setteth himself in a way not good; Evil he doth not abhor.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p8"></a><b>5 </b>O Jehovah! unto the heavens is thy mercy, Thy truth even unto the clouds.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Thy justice is like the great mountains, Thy judgments are a great deep. Man and beast, thou preservest, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p10"></a><b>7 </b>How precious is thy loving-kindness, O God! Therefore the sons of men in the shadow of thy wings shall trust.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p11"></a><b>8 </b>They shall be fully satisfied with the fatness of thy house; And of the river of thy pleasures thou shalt cause them to drink.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p12"></a><b>9 </b>For with thee is the fountain of life, And in thy light shall we see light.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Extend thy mercy to those who know thee, And thy righteousness to the upright in heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Let not the foot of pride come upon me; And the hand of the ungodly let it not remove me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.i-p15"></a><b>12 </b>There fallen are the workers of iniquity; They are thrust down and shall not be able to stand.   				 <a name="fr_322"></a><a href="#fn_322"><font size="1">323</font></a>
 </p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.ii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p2"></a>PSALM 37</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Vex not thyself because of the wicked, Nor be envious on account of the workers of iniquity.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>For like the grass quickly shall they be cut down; And as the green herb they shall wither.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Trust thou in Jehovah, and do good; Dwell in the land, and be fed in truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>And delight in Jehovah, And he will grant thee the request of thy heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Devolve upon Jehovah thy ways, And trust in him, and he will bring it to pass.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>And he will bring forth as the light thy righteousness, And thy judgments as the noonday.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Be silent to Jehovah, and wait for him; Vex not thyself at him who prospereth in his way, At the man who committeth wickedness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Cease from anger, forsake wrath, Vex not thyself so as to commit sin.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>For the wicked shall be cut off; But those who wait for Jehovah shall inherit the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Yet a little while, and the ungodly shall not be; And thou shalt give attention to his place, and shalt not find <i>him</i></p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>But the meek ones shall inherit the earth, And shall be delighted in the abundance of peace.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Plot doth the ungodly against the righteous, And gnasheth against him with his teeth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>The Lord shall laugh at him, For he seeth that coming is his day.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p17"></a><b>14 </b><i>Their</i> sword draw do the ungodly, And their bow they bend, To lay prostrate the poor and needy, To slay those who are upright in the way.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p18"></a><b>15 </b><i>But</i> their sword shall enter into their own heart, And their bow shall be broken.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Better is a little to the righteous man, Than the wealth of the ungodly who are great.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p20"></a><b>17 </b>For the arms of the ungodly shall be broken; But Jehovah sustaineth the righteous.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Know doth Jehovah the days of the upright, And their inheritance for ever shall be.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p22"></a><b>19 </b>They shall not be put to shame in the time of adversity; And in the days of famine they shall be satisfied.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p23"></a><b>20 </b>For the ungodly shall perish, And the enemies of Jehovah like the fattest of lambs shall be consumed; Into smoke they shall be consumed.;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p24"></a><b>21 </b>Borrow doth the ungodly man, and doth not repay; But the righteous man is compassionate and giveth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p25"></a><b>22 </b>For those who are blessed of him shall inherit the earth, And those who are cursed of him shall be cut off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p26"></a><b>23 </b>By Jehovah the steps of a man are directed, And his way he will love.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p27"></a><b>24 </b>When he shall fall he shall not be bruised, For Jehovah putteth under [<i>him</i>] his hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p28"></a><b>25 </b>Young I have been, I have also grown old; And yet I have not seen the righteous man forsaken, Nor his seed begging for bread.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p29"></a><b>26 </b>Daily he is compassionate and lendeth, And his seed is for blessing.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p30"></a><b>27 </b>Depart from evil and do good, And dwell for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p31"></a><b>28 </b>For Jehovah loveth judgment, And doth not forsake his meek ones; For ever shall they be preserved: And the seed of the ungodly shall be cut off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p32"></a><b>29 </b>The righteous shall inherit the earth, And shall dwell for ever upon it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p33"></a><b>30 </b>The mouth of the righteous shall speak wisdom;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p34"></a><b>31 </b>The law of his God is in his heart; Slide not shall his steps.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p35"></a><b>32 </b>Watch doth the ungodly the righteous man, And seeketh to put him to death.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p36"></a><b>33 </b>Jehovah will not leave him in his hand, Nor condemn him when he is judged.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p37"></a><b>34 </b>Wait for Jehovah, and keep his way, And he shall exalt thee to inherit the earth: When the ungodly shall be cut off thou shalt see it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p38"></a><b>35 </b>I have seen the ungodly man robust,   				 <a name="fr_323"></a><a href="#fn_323"><font size="1">324</font></a>
  				 And spreading himself like a green bay tree;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p40"></a><b>36 </b>And he passed away, and to I he was not; And I sought for his place, and he was not found.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p41"></a><b>37 </b>Mark the perfect man, and consider the upright; For the end of such a man is peace.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p42"></a><b>38 </b>But transgressors shall be destroyed together: The end of the ungodly shall be cut off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p43"></a><b>39 </b>But the salvation of the righteous is from Jehovah: <i>He will</i> be their strength in the time of trouble.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ii-p44"></a><b>40 </b>And help them shall Jehovah, and deliver them: He shall deliver them from the wicked: He shall save them, because they trust in him.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.iii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p2"></a>PSALM 38</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p3"></a>A Psalm of David: to bring to remembrance</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! do not in thy fury rebuke me, And in thy wrath do not chasten me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>For thy arrows go down in me, And descend upon me doth thy hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>There is no soundness in my flesh, because of thy wrath, Nor peace in my bones because of my sin.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For my iniquities have passed over my head, Like a burden that is weighty, they are too heavy for me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Putrid [<i>and</i>] corrupt have my wounds become, Because of my foolishness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>I am bowed down, I am brought low exceedingly; Day by day a mourner I do walk:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>For my reins are filled with a burning heat; Nor is there soundness in my flesh.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>I am enfeebled and broken exceedingly: I have roared through the disquietude of my heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>O Lord! before thee is all my desire, And my groaning from thee is not hidden,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>My heart hath throbbed, forsaken me hath my strength; And the light of my eyes, it also is gone from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>My friends and my companions aloof from my stroke have stood, And my kinsmen afar off have stood.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>And they have laid snares who sought for my soul; Arid those who sought my hurt have threatened mischiefs; And deceits daily do they meditate.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>But as for me, like a deaf man I hear not; And <i>I am</i> like a dumb man who openeth not his mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>And I was as a man who doth not hear, And in whose mouth there are no reproofs.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p18"></a><b>15 </b>For on thee, O Jehovah! do I wait: Thou wilt answer <i>me</i>, O Lord, my God!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p19"></a><b>16 </b>For I said, “Lest they should rejoice over me:” At the slipping of my foot against me they magnified themselves,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p20"></a><b>17 </b>Surely as for me I am ready to halt; And my sorrow is before me continually.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Surely my iniquity I declare; I am in consternation because of my sin.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p22"></a><b>19 </b>But my enemies are living;   				 <a name="fr_324"></a><a href="#fn_324"><font size="1">325</font></a>
  				 they are strong; And those are become mighty who hate me wrongfully.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p24"></a><b>20 </b>And they who requite me evil for good are against me, Because I follow [<i>what is</i>] good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p25"></a><b>21 </b>Forsake me not, O Jehovah, my God! Be not far from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iii-p26"></a><b>22 </b>Hasten to my help, O Lord, my salvation!</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.iv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p2"></a>PSALM 39</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician, Jeduthun. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I said “I will take heed to my ways, “That I sin not with my tongue: “I will keep my mouth with a muzzle, “While the ungodly man standeth before me.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>I was dumb not uttering a word; I held my peace [<i>even</i>] from good; And my sorrow was stirred.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>My heart became hot within me; In my musing a fire did burn; I spake with my tongue.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Cause me to know, O Jehovah! my end, And the number of my days, That I may know of what duration I am.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Behold! as an handbreadth thou hast made my days, And my duration is as nothing before thee: Surely altogether vanity is every mart while he standeth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Surely in a shadow man walketh; [Selah. Surely in vain is he disquieted: They heap together, and know not who shall gather.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>And now what do I wait for, O Lord? My hope is towards thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>From all my sins deliver thou me: The reproach of the foolish make me not.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>I was dumb; I will not open my mouth, Because thou hast done it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Remove from me thy stroke: By the blow of thy hand I have failed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>With rebukes for iniquity thou chastisest man; And causest to waste away as a moth his beauty: Surely vanity <i>is</i> every man. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Hear my prayer, O Jehovah! And to my cry give ear; At my tears be not silent; For a stranger am I before thee, A sojourner like all my fathers.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.iv-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Let me alone, that I may recover strength, Before I depart and be no more.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.v"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p2"></a>PSALM 40</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I have patiently waited for Jehovah, And he inclined to me, and heard my cry.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p5"></a><b>2 </b>And he drew me out of the roaring pit, Out of the mire of clay, And set upon a rock my feet; He hath established my steps.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p6"></a><b>3 </b>And he hath put in my mouth a song [that is] new, <i>Even</i> praise to our God: See shall many and shall fear, And shall trust in Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Blessed is the man who maketh Jehovah his confidence, And hath not respected the proud, Nor those who turn aside to lying.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Many, O Jehovah, my God! are thy wonderful works which thou hast done; And thy thoughts towards us it is impossible to reckon up in order to thee: I will declare and speak [<i>of them;</i>] [But] they are more than can be told.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Sacrifice and oblation thou hast not taken pleasure in: <i>But</i> my ears hast thou made fit:   				 <a name="fr_325"></a><a href="#fn_325"><font size="1">326</font></a>
  				 Burnt-offering and sin-offering thou hast not required.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p11"></a><b>7 </b>Then I said, “Behold! I come; “In the volume of the book it is written of me,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p12"></a><b>8 </b>“That I may do thy pleasure, O my God! “I have desired <i>to do it</i>, “And thy law is in the midst of my bowels.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p13"></a><b>9 </b>I have proclaimed thy righteousness in the assembly great: Behold my lips I will not restrain; O Jehovah! thou knowest it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p14"></a><b>10 </b>Thy righteousness I have not hidden within my heart; Thy truth and thy salvation I have declared: I have not concealed thy goodness and thy truth in the assembly great.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p15"></a><b>11 </b>O thou, Jehovah! withhold not thy compassions from me; Let thy goodness and thy truth continually preserve me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p16"></a><b>12 </b>For encompassed me have evils innumerable; Laid hold upon me have my iniquities, <i>yea in so great number</i> that I cannot see them: They are more in number than the hairs of my head; <i>And</i> my heart hath failed me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p17"></a><b>13 </b>Let it please thee, O Jehovah! to deliver me; O Jehovah! to my aid make haste.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p18"></a><b>14 </b>Let them be put to shame and confounded together Who seek after my soul to destroy it; Let them be turned backward and put to shame Who seek after my hurt.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p19"></a><b>15 </b>Let them be destroyed for a reward of their shame, Who have said to me, “Aha! aha!”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p20"></a><b>16 </b>Let all those exult and rejoice in thee who seek thee; And let those say continually, “May Jehovah be magnified” — “Those who love thy salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.v-p21"></a><b>17 </b>But as for me <i>I am</i> poor and needy. Jehovah hath regarded me; My help and my deliverer <i>art thou</i>: O thou, my God! delay not.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.vi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p2"></a>PSALM 41</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Blessed is he who judgeth wisely of the poor: In the day of evil Jehovah will deliver him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Jehovah will keep him, and preserve him alive: He shall be blessed upon the earth: And thou will not give him up to the desire of his enemies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Jehovah will support him upon the bed of sorrow: All his bed thou hast turned in his sickness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>I have said, “O Jehovah! have mercy upon me;  				”  				 “Heal my soul, for I have sinned against thee.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>My enemies have spoken evil of me, “When will he die, and perish shall his name?“</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>And if he come to see me falsely doth he speak; His heart gathereth iniquity to itself’: When he goeth abroad he speaketh [<i>it</i>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Together against me do all my haters whisper; Against me do they devise evil for me, [<i>saying</i>,]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>“An evil deed of Belial cleaveth fast to him; “And he who lieth shall not rise again.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Even the man of my peace in whom I trusted, Who eateth of my bread, hath lifted up against me the heel.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Do thou <i>then</i>, O Jehovah! have mercy upon me; Raise me up, and I will recompense them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>By this I have known that I have been acceptable to thee, Because my enemy shall not triumph over me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>And as for me, in my integrity thou wilt uphold me, And wilt establish me before thy face for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vi-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Blessed <i>be</i> Jehovah, the God of Israel, For ever and ever. Amen and Amen.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.vii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="3rdLevelAllCap12Bld40"><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p2"></a>PART SECOND.  				 <a name="fr_326"></a><a href="#fn_326"><font size="1">327</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p4"></a>PSALM 42</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p5"></a>To the Chief Musician. A lesson of instruction to the Sons of Korah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p6"></a><b>1 </b>As the hart crieth for the fountains of waters, So my soul crieth for thee, O God!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p7"></a><b>2 </b>Thirsted hath my soul for God, for the living God: When shall I come to appear before the face of God?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p8"></a><b>3 </b>To me have my tears been <i>for</i> bread, by day and night, While it is said to me daily, “Where is thy God?“</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p9"></a><b>4 </b>When these things I remember, I pour out within me my soul, Because I had gone with the procession, Leading them even to the house of God, With the voice of exultation and praise, — The multitude dancing for joy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p10"></a><b>5 </b>‘Why art thou cast down, O my soul! And why art thou disquieted within me? Wait thou for God; for I shall yet give him thanks, [<i>For</i>] the salvations of his countenance.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p11"></a><b>6 </b>O my God! my soul within me is cast down, When I remember thee from the land of Jordan and of Hermonim, From the mountain Mizar.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p12"></a><b>7 </b>Deep unto deep calleth at the noise of thy waterspouts: All thy waves and all thy billows over me have gone.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p13"></a><b>8 </b>By day command will Jehovah his loving-kindness, And by night his song <i>shall be</i> with me, And prayer to the God of my life.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p14"></a><b>9 </b>I will say to God, my Rock, “Why hast thou forgotten me? “Why mourning do I go because of the oppression of <i>my</i> enemy?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p15"></a><b>10 </b>[<i>It is as</i>] a wound in my bones when my enemies reproach me, Saying to me daily, “Where is thy God?“</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.vii-p16"></a><b>11 </b>Why art thou cast down, O my soul? And why art thou disquieted within me? Hope in God; for I shall yet give thanks to him, The salvations of my countenance, and my God.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.viii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.viii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.viii-p2"></a>PSALM 43</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.viii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Judge me, O God! and plead my cause: From a people without mercy, from a man deceitful and wicked deliver me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.viii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>For thou <i>art</i> the God of my strength; Why art thou estranged from me? Why mourning do I go because of the oppression of the enemy?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.viii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Send forth thy light and thy truth; Let them direct me, let them conduct me, To the mountain of thy holiness, and to thy tabernacles.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.viii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>And I will go to the altar of God, To the God of the joy of my rejoicing; And I will celebrate thee upon the harp, O God, my God!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.viii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Why art thou cast down, O my soul! And why art thou disquieted within me? Hope in God, for I shall yet celebrate him, <i>Who is </i>the salvation of my countenance and my God.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.ix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p2"></a>PSALM 44</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. Giving instruction</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O God! with our ears we have heard, Our fathers have told us, The work which thou hast done in their days, In the days of old.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Thou with thy hand hast expelled the heathen, and planted them: Thou hast wasted the peoples and multiplied them:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For not by their own sword acquired they the land, And their own arm did not save them; But thy right hand and thy arm, and the light of thy countenance, Because thou wast favorable to them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p7"></a><b>4</b> Thou, even thou, <i>art</i> my King; O God! command salvations for Jacob.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Through thee our adversaries with the horn we have pushed; In thy name we have trampled under foot those who rise up against us.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p9"></a><b>6 </b>For not in my bow will I trust, And my sword will not save me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Surely thou hast saved us from our enemies, And our haters thou hast put to shame.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p11"></a><b>8 </b>In God we will boast all the day, And thy name for ever shall we praise. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Nevertheless thou hast abhorred us and put us to shame, And thou goest not forth <i>any more</i> with our armies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Thou hast made us to turn back from him that afflicteth us, And our haters have spoiled <i>us</i> for themselves.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Thou hast given us as sheep for food; And among the heathen thou hast scattered us.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Thou hast sold thy people, and not become rich, And thou hast not increased the price of them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Thou hast made us a reproach to our neighbors, A scorn and derision to those who are round about us.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Thou hast made us a byword among the heathen, A shaking of the head among the peoples.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p18"></a><b>15 </b>Daily <i>is</i> my reproach before me, And the shame of my face hath <i>quite</i> covered me,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Because of the voice of him who reproacheth and revileth, Because of the face of the adversary and avenger.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p20"></a><b>17 </b>All this is come upon us, and we have not forgotten thee, Nor dealt perfidiously in thy covenant;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Not turned back hath our heart, Nor declined have our steps from thy path.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p22"></a><b>19 </b>Although thou hast crushed us in the place of dragons, And covered us with the shadow of death.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p23"></a><b>20 </b>If we have forgotten the name of our God, And have spread forth our hands to a God that is strange;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p24"></a><b>21 </b>Shall not God search out this? For he knoweth the secrets of the heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p25"></a><b>22 </b>Surely for thy sake we are killed daily; We are accounted as sheep [<i>appointed</i>] for slaughter.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p26"></a><b>23 </b>Arise, why sleepest thou, O Lord? Awake, do not forget <i>us</i> for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p27"></a><b>24 </b>Wherefore thy face dost thou hide? Wilt thou forget our misery and our affliction?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p28"></a><b>25 </b>For humbled to the dust is our soul; Cleave to the earth doth our belly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.ix-p29"></a><b>26 </b>Arise for our help, And redeem us for the sake of thy loving-kindness.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.x"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p2"></a>PSALM 45</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Upon the lilies. Of the sons of Korah. Giving instruction. A Song of loves</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Boiling over is my heart to speak a goodly theme, Speak shall I myself of my works concerning the King: My tongue is as the pen of a swift writer.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Thou art fair above the sons of men; Diffused is grace on thy lips; Because God hath blessed thee for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O mighty one! With majesty and glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p7"></a><b>4 </b>And in thy majesty prosper thou; Ride forth upon the word of truth, and meekness and righteousness; And thy right hand shall teach thee terrible things:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Thy arrows <i>are</i> sharp (so that the people fall under thee) In the hearts of the enemies of the king.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Thy throne, O God! <i>is</i> for ever and ever; The scepter of rectitude <i>is</i> the scepter of thy kingdom.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Thou lovest righteousness and hatest impiety; Because anointed thee hath God, thy God, With the oil of gladness above thy fellows.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Myrrh, and aloes and cassia [<i>are</i>] <i>in</i> all thy garments, Out of the ivory palaces, whence they have made thee glad.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p12"></a><b>9 </b>The daughters of kings [<i>were</i>] among thy maids of honor; Stand did thy consort at thy right hand in gold of Ophir.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Hearken, O daughter! and consider and incline thy ear; And forget thy people, and the house of thy father.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p14"></a><b>11 </b>And enamored shall be the King with thy beauty; For he <i>is</i> thy Lord, and thou shalt worship him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p15"></a><b>12 </b>And the daughter of Tyre [<i>shall come</i>] with a present; Thy favor entreat shall the rich among the people.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p16"></a><b>13 </b>All glorious is the daughter of the King within; Of garments embroidered with gold <i>is</i> her clothing.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p17"></a><b>14 </b>In raiment of needle-work she shall be brought to the King; Her virgins that follow her, her companions shall be brought to thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p18"></a><b>15 </b>They shall be brought with joy and exultation; They shall enter into the palace of the King.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Instead of thy fathers shall be thy children; Thou shalt make them princes in all the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.x-p20"></a><b>17 </b>I will make thy name to be remembered throughout all generation; Therefore celebrate thee shall the peoples for ever and ever.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p2"></a>PSALM 46</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. Upon Alamoth. A Song</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>God is to us a protection and strength; A help in troubles he is found exceedingly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Therefore we will not fear when moved shall be the earth, And fall shall the mountains into the heart of the sea.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>[<i>When</i>] roar and rage tempestuously shall the waters thereof; [<i>When</i>] shake shall the mountains with the swelling thereof. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>The streams of her river shall make glad the city of God, The Sanctuary of the tabernacles of the Most High.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>God <i>is</i> in the midst of her; she shall not be moved: Help her will God at the dawn of the morning.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Rage did the peoples, moved were the kingdoms: He uttered his voice, melt did the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Jehovah of armies <i>is</i> with us; A fortress for us <i>is</i> the God of Jacob. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Come ye, consider the works of Jehovah, What desolations he hath wrought in the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>He maketh to cease battles, even to the ends of the earth; He breaketh the bow, he shattereth in pieces the arms; The chariot he burneth with fire.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Be still and know that I am God: I will be exalted among the heathen; I will be exalted in the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Jehovah of armies is with us; A fortress for us <i>is</i> the God of Jacob. Selah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p2"></a>PSALM 47</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. Upon Alamoth. A Song</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O all ye peoples! clap the hand; Shout unto God with the voice of exultation;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>For Jehovah <i>is</i> high, terrible, A great king over all the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>He hath put in order the people under us, And the nations under our feet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>He hath chosen for us our inheritance, The glory of Jacob, whom he hath loved. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Gone up is God with a shout, Jehovah with the sound of a trumpet.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Sing psalms to God, sing psalms; Sing psalms to our King, sing psalms;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>For king of all the earth is God; Sing praises, all ye who understand!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>The kingdom he hath obtained over the heathen; God sitteth upon the throne of his holiness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>The princes of the peoples are assembled together To the people of the God of Abraham: For to God belong the shields of the earth: He is greatly exalted.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p2"></a>PSALM 48</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p3"></a>A Song of a Psalm. Of the sons of Korah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Great is Jehovah and to be praised greatly In the city of our God, in the mountain of his holiness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Beautiful for situation, the joy of the whole earth, The mountain of Zion, on the sides of the north, The city of the great King.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>God in her palaces is known for a defense.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For behold! the kings assembled, They passed away together.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>They themselves saw, so they marveled; They were frightened, they fled precipitately,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Fear seized upon them there, Pain as of one in travail.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>By the east wind thou breakest in pieces the ships of Tarshish.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>As we have heard, so have we seen In the city of Jehovah of Hosts, In the city of our God: God will establish it for ever. Selah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>We have waited, O God! for thy mercy In the midst of thy temple,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>As <i>is</i> thy name, O God! So <i>is</i> thy praise unto the ends of the earth: Of righteousness full is thy right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Rejoice shall Mount Zion, Exult shall the daughters of Judah, Because of thy judgments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Encompass Zion, and walk round about her. Number the towers thereof,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Set your heart to her walls, Exalt her towers, That ye may make report to the generations to come.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>For this God is our God for ever and ever: He will be our guide even unto death.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p2"></a>PSALM 49</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. A Psalm</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Hear this all ye peoples; Give ear all ye inhabitants of the world:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Both ye sons of Adam, and ye sons of men, Rich and poor together.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>My mouth shall speak of wisdoms, And the meditation of my heart is of understanding.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>I will incline to a parable my ear: I will open upon the harp my enigma.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Wherefore should I fear in the days of evil? The iniquity of my heel shall compass me about.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>They trust in their wealth, And in the multitude of their riches do glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>The brother shall not be able to redeem; None shall give to God the price of his redemption.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>And precious shall be the redemption of their soul, And <i>their</i> continuance for ever:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>That he should still live for ever, And not see the grave.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>For he shall see that wise men die, Together the fool and the brutish person shall perish, And leave to strangers their wealth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Their inward thought is [<i>how to make</i>] their houses [<i>to continue</i>] for ever, Their dwelling-places from generation to generation: They have called out their names upon the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>And man in honor shall not abide; He hath become like the beasts: they perish.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p16"></a><b>13 </b>This their way <i>is</i> foolishness in them, And their posterity in their saying will acquiesce. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Like sleep in the grave they are laid; Death shall feed them; And have dominion over them shall the upright in the morning, And their strength shall wax old; The grave <i>shall receive</i> them from their dwelling.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p18"></a><b>15 </b>But God shall redeem my soul from the hand of the grave; For he hath taken me up. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p19"></a><b>16 </b>Be not thou afraid when a man shall become rich, When increased shall be the glory of his house;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p20"></a><b>17 </b>For he shall not at his death carry all away: Descend not after him shall his glory:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p21"></a><b>18 </b>For his soul in his lifetime he will bless, And they shall praise thee when thou doest well to thyself.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p22"></a><b>19 </b>He shall come to the age of his fathers, Even for ever he shall not see the light.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xiv-p23"></a><b>20 </b>Man <i>is</i> in honor, and will not understand: He hath become like the beasts: they shall perish.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p2"></a>PSALM 50</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p3"></a>A Song, of Asaph</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>The God of gods, Jehovah hath spoken, And called the earth From the rising of the sun unto the going down thereof.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Out of Zion, the Perfection of beauty, God hath shined.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Come shall our God, and shall not keep silence; A fire before him shall devour, And round about him a tempest shall rage exceedingly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>He shall call to the heavens from above, And to the earth, to judge his people.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>“Gather together to me my meek ones, (<i>will he say</i>), “Those who strike a covenant with me over sacrifices.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>And declare shall the heavens his righteousness: For God is judge himself. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>“Hear, O my people! and I will speak; “O Israel! and I will announce to thee: “God, [<i>even</i>] thy God am I.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>“Not for thy sacrifices will I reprove thee; “And thy burnt-offerings <i>are</i> before me continually.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>“I will not take out of thy house a calf, “<i>Nor</i> out of thy folds he-goats:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>“For mine are all the beasts of the forest, “The cattle upon a thousand hills.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>“I know all the birds of the mountains; “And the wild beasts of the field are at my command.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>“If I am hungry, I will not tell thee: “For mine is the world and the fullness thereof.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p16"></a><b>13 </b>“Will I eat the flesh of bulls, “And the blood of goats will I drink?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p17"></a><b>14 </b>“Sacrifice unto God praise, “And pay unto the Most High thy vows.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p18"></a><b>15 </b>“Call upon me in the day of trouble; “I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p19"></a><b>16 </b>“But unto the wicked said hath God, “What hast thou to do to declare my statutes, “[<i>Or</i>] that thou shouldest take my covenant into thy lips?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p20"></a><b>17 </b>“Also thou hatest correction, “And castest my words behind thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p21"></a><b>18 </b>“If thou seest a thief, thou wilt run with him, “And with adulterers is thy portion.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p22"></a><b>19 </b>“Thy mouth thou puttest forth to evil, “And thy tongue frameth deceit,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p23"></a><b>20 </b>“Thou wilt sit against thy brother; “Thou wilt speak against the sons of thy mother; “Thou wilt set forth slander.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p24"></a><b>21 </b>“These things thou hast done, and I kept silence; “Thou thoughtest that I would be like thyself’: “I will reprove thee, and set them in order before thine eyes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p25"></a><b>22 </b>“Now consider this, ye who forget God, “Lest I seize upon you and there be none to deliver.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xv-p26"></a><b>23 </b>“He who sacrificeth praise will glorify me: “And he who ordereth his way to him will I show the salvation of God.”</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p2"></a>PSALM 51</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David, when Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had gone in to Bathsheba</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Have pity upon me, O God! according to thy mercy; According to the multitude of thy compassions blot out my iniquities.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p5"></a><b>2</b> Multiply to wash me from my sin, And from my wickedness do thou cleanse me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For my sins I know, And my wickedness is before me continually.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Against thee, against thee only, have I sinned, And that which was displeasing in thy sight have I done; That thou mayest be justified when thou speakest, And be pure in giving judgment.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Behold in iniquity I was born, And in sin conceive me did my mother.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Behold, truth thou hast loved in the inmost parts, And in secret, wisdom thou hast made me know.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Thou shalt purge me with hyssop, and I shall be clean; Thou shalt wash me, and I shall be whiter than snow.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Make me to hear joy and gladness; And exult shall the bones which thou hast broken.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Hide thy face from my sins, And all my iniquities blot out.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>A heart [<i>that is</i>] clean create in me, O God! And a spirit [<i>that is</i>] right renew in my inward parts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Cast me not away from thy face, And the Spirit of thy holiness take not from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Restore to me the joy of thy salvation, And with a free spirit uphold me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p16"></a><b>13 </b>I will teach transgressors thy ways, the ungodly to time shall be converted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Deliver me from bloods, O God! O God of my salvation! And sing aloud shall my tongue of thy righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p18"></a><b>15 </b>O Lord! my lips do thou open, And my mouth shall show forth thy praise.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p19"></a><b>16 </b>For thou wilt not accept a sacrifice; Though I should give a burnt-offering, it would not please thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p20"></a><b>17 </b>The sacrifices of God are an afflicted spirit: A heart afflicted and contrite, O God! thou wilt not despise.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p21"></a><b>18 </b>Do good in thy good pleasure to Zion; Build thou the walls of Jerusalem.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvi-p22"></a><b>19 </b>Then shalt thou accept the sacrifices of righteousness, The burnt-offering and oblation;   				 <a name="fr_327"></a><a href="#fn_327"><font size="1">328</font></a>
  				 Then shall come upon thy altar calves.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xvii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p2"></a>PSALM 52</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A lesson of instruction of David: when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, and said to him, that David had come into the house of Abimelech</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Why dost thou glory in thy wickedness, O mighty man? The goodness of God <i>continueth</i> daily.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Thy tongue reckoneth up mischiefs, Like a razor [<i>that is</i>] sharp working deceitfully.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Thou lovest wickedness more than goodness; Falsehood more than to speak righteousness. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Thou lovest all words of deceit, O thou tongue of guilefulness!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Likewise God shall destroy thee for ever: He shall lay hold on thee and pluck thee out of thy tabernacle, And root thee out of the land of the living. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>See it also shall the righteous ones, and shall fear, And at him they shall laugh.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Behold! the man who made not God his strength; And trusted in the abundance of his riches, And was strong in his wickedness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>But as for me <i>I shall be</i> like an olive-tree [<i>that is</i>] green in the house of God: I have trusted in the goodness of God for ever and ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xvii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>I will celebrate thee for ever, because thou hast done [<i>it</i>:]   				 <a name="fr_328"></a><a href="#fn_328"><font size="1">329</font></a>
  				 I will wait on thy name, For it is good in the presence of thy meek ones.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xviii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p2"></a>PSALM 53</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician, upon Mahalath. A lesson of instruction ofDavid</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>The fool hath said in his heart, “There is not a God:” They have corrupted [<i>all good order</i>,] they have done abominable work: There is none who doeth good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>God from heaven looked down upon the sons of men, To see if there was any who did understand, Who did seek after God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Every one of them hath gone back; They have all together become corrupt: There is none that doeth good, not even one.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Have they no knowledge, all <i>these</i> workers of iniquity? Eating my people [<i>as</i>] they eat bread: Upon Jehovah they have not called.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>There were they afraid with fear, where there was not fear; For scattered hath Jehovah the bones of him that encampeth against thee: Thou hast put them to shame because God hath despised them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xviii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Who shall give out of Zion deliverance to Israel? When bring back shall God the captivity of his people, Rejoice shall Jacob, exult shall Israel.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p2"></a>PSALM 54</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician, on Neginoth. A lesson of instruction of David. When the Ziphims came and said to Saul, “Doth not David hide himself with us?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O God! by thy name save me, And by thy strength judge me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p5"></a><b>2 </b>O God! hear my prayer, Give ear to the words of my mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For strangers have risen up against me, And terrible ones have sought after my soul: They have not set God before them. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Behold! God is a helper to me; The Lord is with those who uphold my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p8"></a><b>5 </b>He shall repay evil to my adversaries: In thy truth cut them off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Willingly will I sacrifice to thee; I will celebrate thy name, O Jehovah! for it is good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xix-p10"></a><b>7 </b>For out of all trouble he hath delivered me; And [<i>punishment</i>] upon my adversaries mine eye hath seen.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xx"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p2"></a>PSALM 55</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A lesson of instruction of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Give ear, O God! to my prayer, And hide not thyself from my supplication.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Attend to me, and answer me: I will wail in my address, and will become tumultuous.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p6"></a><b>3 </b>By reason of the voice of the enemy — Under the oppression of the ungodly; For they cast upon me iniquity, In wrath they set themselves against me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p7"></a><b>4 </b>My heart trembleth within me, And the terrors of death have fallen upon me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Fear and trembling are come upon me, And horror hath overwhelmed me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p9"></a><b>6 </b>And I said, “Who will give me wings like a dove? “I will fly away and be at rest.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p10"></a><b>7 </b>“Lo! I will flee far away, “I will repose in the desert. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p11"></a><b>8 </b>“I will hasten my escape from the tempestuous whirlwind.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Destroy, O Lord! divide their tongue: For I have seen oppression and strife in the city.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p13"></a><b>10 </b>By day and night they go round it upon the walls thereof: And labor and sorrow are in the midst of it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Wickedness   				 <a name="fr_329"></a><a href="#fn_329"><font size="1">330</font></a>
  				 is in the midst of it; And fraud and deceit depart not from the streets thereof.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p16"></a><b>12 </b>Truly it was not an enemy who reproached me, For [<i>then</i>] I could have borne [<i>it</i>:] <i>It was</i> not an adversary who magnified himself against me, For [<i>then</i>] I would have hid himself from him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p17"></a><b>13 </b>But thou, a man according to my own rank, My guide, and my familiar friend.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p18"></a><b>14 </b>We sweetly exchanged our secret thoughts; Into the house of God we walked in company.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p19"></a><b>15 </b>Let death seize upon them, Let them descend into the grave alive; For wickedness   				 <a name="fr_330"></a><a href="#fn_330"><font size="1">331</font></a>
  				 <i>is</i> I, their dwelling, in the midst of them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p21"></a><b>16 </b>As for me, to God; will I cry, And Jehovah shall save me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p22"></a><b>17 </b>In the evening, and the morning, and at noonday Will I pray, and cry aloud; And he shall hear my voice.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p23"></a><b>18 </b>He hath redeemed into peace my soul From the battle which was against me: For many were with me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p24"></a><b>19 </b>Hear shall God, and shall afflict them, Even he who sitteth from ancient time. Selah. Because they have no changes, And fear not God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p25"></a><b>20 </b>He hath set his hands against those who were at peace with him: He hath broken his covenant.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p26"></a><b>21 </b>Smoother than butter are the words of his mouth, And<i> in</i> his heart <i>is</i> war; Softer are his words than oil, And [<i>yet</i>] they <i>are</i> darts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p27"></a><b>22 </b>Cast upon Jehovah whatever blessings thou askest from him,   				 <a name="fr_331"></a><a href="#fn_331"><font size="1">332</font></a>
  				 And he shall feed thee; He shall not suffer for ever the righteous man to stagger.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xx-p29"></a><b>23 </b>Thou, O God! shalt cast them into the pit of corruption: The men of blood and deceit shall not live out half their days: But as for me, I will hope in thee.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p2"></a>PSALM 56</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician upon, the silent dove in distant places. Michtam of David, when the Philistines took him in Gath</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Have mercy upon me, O God, For swallow me up doth man; He daily assaulting doth oppress me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Swallow me up do <i>my</i> enemies daily: Truly many <i>strive</i> to oppress me, <i>O Jehovah</i>, Most High!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>In the day when I was afraid, I in thee did trust.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>In God I will praise his word; In God have I trusted; I will not fear what flesh can do to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Every day my words disquiet me; Against me <i>are</i> all their thoughts for evil.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>They assemble together, they hide themselves, My heels they watch, Because they desire my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>In <i>their</i> iniquity <i>they think</i> there is escape for them: In <i>thy</i> wrath the peoples thou wilt cast down, O God!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>My wanderings thou numbereth, even thou: Put my tears into thy bottle; Are they not in thy register?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Then my enemies shall be turned back in the day when I cry: This I know, because God is with me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>In God will I praise [<i>his</i>] word; In Jehovah will I praise [<i>his</i>] word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>In God have I trusted; I will not fear what man can do to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Upon me, O God! are thy vows, I will render praises to thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxi-p16"></a><b>13 </b>For thou hast delivered my soul from death: Hast thou not <i>also delivered</i> my feet from falling? That I may walk before God in the light of the living.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p2"></a>PSALM 57</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Destroy not. Michtam of David. When he fled from the face of Saul in the cave</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Have mercy upon me, O God! have mercy upon me; For in thee my soul doth trust; And in the shadow of thy wings will I hope, Until iniquity pass away.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>I will cry to God Most High, Who perfecteth [<i>his work</i>] towards me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>He shall send from Heaven, And shall save me from the reproach of him who swalloweth me up: Send forth shall God his mercy and his truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>My soul is in the midst of lions; I lie among those who are set on fire, — Among the sons of men, whose teeth are spears and arrows, And their tongue a sword [<i>that is</i>] sharp.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Be thou exalted above the heavens, O God! Above all the earth thy glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>A net they have prepared for my steps: Bowed down is my soul: They have digged before me a pit, <i>But</i> they have fallen into it. Selah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Prepared <i>is</i> my heart, O God! prepared <i>is</i> my heart: I will sing, and chant psalms.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Awake my tongue, awake nablum   				 <a name="fr_332"></a><a href="#fn_332"><font size="1">333</font></a>
  				 and harp: I will awake at dawn of day.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p13"></a><b>9 </b>I will celebrate thee, among the peoples, O Lord! I will sing psalms to thee among the nation:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p14"></a><b>10 </b>For great unto the heavens is thy goodness, And unto the clouds thy truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxii-p15"></a><b>11 </b>Be thou exalted, above the heavens, O God! Above all the earth thy glory.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p2"></a>PSALM 58</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Destroy not. Michtam of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Do ye indeed, O ye congregation! speak righteousness? Uprightly do ye judge? O ye sons of men!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Yea rather in <i>your</i> heart wickedness ye plot, On the earth violence your hands weigh out.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Estranged are the ungodly from the womb, They have gone astray from their birth speaking falsehood.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>They have poison like the poison of a serpent, [<i>They are</i>] like the deaf adder which stoppeth her ear;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Which listeneth not to the voice of the enchanter, — Of him who exerciseth enchantment skillfully.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>O God! break their teeth in their mouth: The jawbones of the lions break, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Let them melt away like water, let them be gone: Let them bend their bow, and let their arrows be as if broken.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Like a snail which melteth away let them vanish; Like the untimely birth of a woman which doth not see the sun.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Before your pots can feel the fire of the bramble, <i>Like</i> flesh yet raw as a whirlwind he shall carry him away.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Rejoice shall the righteous when he seeth the vengeance; His hands he shall wash in the blood of the ungodly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>And men   				 <a name="fr_333"></a><a href="#fn_333"><font size="1">334</font></a>
  				 shall say, “Truly there is fruit for the righteous, “Truly there is a God who judgeth in the earth.”</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p2"></a>PSALM 59</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. Destroy not. Michtam of David. When Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Deliver me from my enemies, O my God! from those who rise up against me set me on high.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Deliver me from the workers of iniquity, And from men of bloods save me:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For lo! they have laid snares for my soul; Gathered together against me have the strong men; Not [<i>for</i>] my sin, nor [<i>for</i>] my wickedness, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Without <i>any</i> iniquity <i>of mine</i> they have run and prepared themselves. Awake and come to meet me, and behold.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>And thou, O Jehovah, God of armies! the God of Israel! Awake to visit all the nations; Do not have compassion upon any who transgress wickedly. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>They will return at evening; They will make a noise like a dog, And go round about the city.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Behold they will prate with their mouth; Swords are in their lips; “For who,” <i>say they</i>, “will hear?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>But thou, O Jehovah! shalt laugh at them; Thou shalt hold in derision all the nations.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>His strength with thee I will put in trust; For God is my fortress.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>The God of my mercy shall prevent me; God will make me see my desire upon my enemies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Slay them not, lest my people should forget; Make them to wander by thy power; And bring them down, O Lord, our shield!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>The sin of their mouth, the words of their lips: Let them be taken in their pride: of cursing and lying let them speak.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Consume, in thy fury consume them, that they may be no more; And let men know that God ruleth in Jacob, Even to the ends of the earth. Selah.   				 <a name="fr_334"></a><a href="#fn_334"><font size="1">335</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p19"></a><b>14 </b>And they will return at evening; They will bark like a dog, And go round about the city.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p20"></a><b>15 </b>They will wander up and down for food; If they be not satisfied they will even stay all night.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p21"></a><b>16 </b>But as for me, I will sing of thy strength, I will praise in the morning thy mercy; For thou hast been a fortress to me, And a refuge in the day of my trouble.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p22"></a><b>17 </b>My strength is with thee, I will sing psalms; For God <i>is</i> my fortress, the God of my mercy.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p2"></a>PSALM 60</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician upon Shushan Eduth. Michtam of David to teach. When he fought against the Syrians of Mesopotamia and against the Syrians of Zobah; and when Joab, having returned, smote of the Edomites in the Valley of Salt twelve thousand</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O God! thou hast cast us off, thou hast scattered us; Thou hast been angry, O return to us!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>To tremble thou hast made the earth; Thou hast caused it to open wide; Heal the breaches thereof for it shaketh.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Thou hast showed to thy people a hard thing, Thou hast made us drunk with the wine of stupefaction.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Thou hast given to those who fear thee a banner, That it may be displayed before <i>thy</i> truth. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>That thy beloved ones may be delivered, Save with thy right hand and hear me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice: I will divide Shechem, And the valley of Succoth I will measure.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Mine <i>shall be</i> Gilead, and mine <i>shall be</i> Manasseh; And Ephraim <i>shall be</i> the strength of my head; Judah, my lawgiver.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Moab <i>shall be</i> the pot for my washing; Over Edom will I cast my shoe; O Palestina! triumph thou over me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Who will bring me into the city fortified? Who will lead me into Edom?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Wilt not thou, O God! who hadst cast us off? [<i>thou</i>] O God! [<i>who</i>] didst not go forth with our armies?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Grant us relief from trouble, For vain <i>is</i> the help of man.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Through God we shall do valiantly: And he it is who shall tread down our adversaries.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p2"></a>PSALM 61</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician upon Neginoth. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Hear, O God! my cry, Attend to my prayer.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>From the end of the earth to thee will I cry, when vexed is my heart: To the rock which is higher than I thou shalt lead me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For thou hast been a hope to me, A tower of strength from the face of the enemy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>I will dwell in thy tabernacle for ever; I will be safe under the covert of thy wings. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>For thou, O God! hast heard my vows: Thou hast given an inheritance to those who fear thy name.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Days upon days to the king thou shalt add, His years <i>shall be</i> as many generations.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>He shall dwell for ever in the presence of God: Mercy and truth do thou prepare: thou shalt preserve him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>So will I sing unto thy name for ever, That I may perform my vows every day.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p2"></a>PSALM 62</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician upon Jeduthun. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Nevertheless towards God silent is my soul: From him is my salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Nevertheless he is my reek and my salvation, My fortress: <i>therefore</i> I shall not be moved greatly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>How long will ye continue to lay snares against a man? Ye shall be slain all of you: As an inclining wall shall ye be, and a fence that is shaken.</p>  			 
 <p class="BibleVerse39"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Yet from his elevation they consult to east him down: They delight in falsehood: With their mouth they bless, And in their hearts they curse. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p class="BibleVerse39"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Nevertheless towards God be thou silent O my soul: For from him <i>is</i> my expectation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Nevertheless he <i>only is</i> my rock, and my salvation: My fortress; I shall not fall.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>In God <i>is</i> my salvation and my glory; The rock of my strength; my hope <i>is</i> in God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Hope in him at all times, O ye people! Pour out before his face your hearts: God <i>is</i> our hope. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Nevertheless vanity are the sons of Adam; A lie the sons of men: When put all together in a balance they are found lighter than vanity itself.   				 <a name="fr_335"></a><a href="#fn_335"><font size="1">336</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p14"></a><b>10 </b>Trust not in oppression and robbery; be not vain: [<i>Upon</i>] riches if they abound set not your heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p15"></a><b>11 </b>Once God hath spoken; Twice this I have heard, “That power belongeth to God;” And to thee, O Lord! <i>belongeth</i> mercy; Truly thou wilt render to every man according to his work.</p>  <a name="xxxv.ii.xxviii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p2"></a>PSALM 63</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p3"></a>A Psalm of David, when he was in the wilderness of Judea</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O God! my God art thou; Early will I seek thee: Thirsted for thee hath my soul, Longed for thee hath my flesh, In this land [<i>that is</i>] inhospitable and dry, without water.</p>
