 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p8"></a><b>4 </b>I am counted with those who go down to the sepulcher,   				 <a name="fr_354"></a><a href="#fn_354"><font size="1">355</font></a>
  				 I have been as a man who hath no strength:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p10"></a><b>5 </b>Free among the dead, As the slain lying in the grave, Whom thou rememberest no more, And who from thy hand are cut off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p11"></a><b>6 </b>Thou hast laid me in the lowest pit, In thick darkness, in the deeps.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p12"></a><b>7 </b>Upon me lieth heavy thy indignation; And with all thy waves thou hast afflicted me. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p13"></a><b>8 </b>Thou hast removed my acquaintances from me: Thou hast made me abominations to them: I am shut up that I cannot go forth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p14"></a><b>9 </b>My eye mourneth because of my affliction; I invoke thee, O Jehovah! daily: I stretch out to thee my hands.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p15"></a><b>10 </b>Wilt thou for the dead do a miracle? Shall the dead rising up praise thee? Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p16"></a><b>11 </b>Shall thy loving-kindness be declared in the grave? Thy truth in destruction?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p17"></a><b>12 </b>Shall thy wonders be known in darkness? And thy righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p18"></a><b>13 </b>But as for me to thee, O Jehovah! have I cried, And in the morning my prayer shall prevent thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p19"></a><b>14 </b>Wherefore, O Jehovah! wilt thou reject my soul? [<i>Wherefore</i>] wilt thou hide thy face from me?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p20"></a><b>15 </b>Afflicted am I, and ready to die from my youth; I have suffered thy terrors by doubting.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p21"></a><b>16 </b>Passed over me hath thy fierce wrath: Thy terrors have cut me off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p22"></a><b>17 </b>They have encompassed me as waters daily; They have surrounded me together.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxii-p23"></a><b>18 </b>Thou hast removed from me lover and companion; And my acquaintances are darkness.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p2"></a>PSALM 89</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p3"></a>An Instruction of Ethan, the Ezrahite</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>The mercies of Jehovah for ever will I sing: From generation to generation will I celebrate thy truth with my mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>For I have said, For ever Mercy shall be built up: The heavens thou shalt establish; thy truth [<i>is</i>] in them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>“I have made a covenant with my chosen: “I have sworn to David my servant:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>“For ever will I establish thy seed, “And I will build up from age to age thy throne.” Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>And celebrate shall the heavens thy wondrous work, O Jehovah! Also thy truth in the congregation of the saints.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>For who in the clouds can be compared to Jehovah? Who is like unto Jehovah among the sons of the gods?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>God is terrible exceedingly in the assembly of the saints, And to be feared above all who are around him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>O Jehovah, God of armies! who <i>is</i> a strong God like thee? And thy truth is round about thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Thou governest the pride of the sea: When rise up do the waves thereof, thou restrainest them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Thou hast overthrown Egypt as a wounded mail; With the arm of thy strength thou hast scattered thy enemies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Thine are the heavens, thine also is the earth: The world, and the fullness thereof thou hast formed.   				 <a name="fr_355"></a><a href="#fn_355"><font size="1">356</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p16"></a><b>12 </b>The north and the south thou hast created: Tabor and Hermon in thy name shall exult.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p17"></a><b>13 </b>Thou hast an arm of might: Thou wilt strengthen thy hand, Thou wilt exalt thy right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p18"></a><b>14 </b>Righteousness and judgment <i>are</i> the seat of thy throne: Mercy and truth shall go before thy face.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p19"></a><b>15 </b>Blessed is the people that know the joyful sound! O Jehovah! in the brightness of thy countenance they shall walk.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p20"></a><b>16 </b>In thy name shall they exult daily; And in thy righteousness shall they glory:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p21"></a><b>17 </b>For the glory of their strength art thou; And in thy favor exalted shall be our horn.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p22"></a><b>18 </b>For to Jehovah <i>is</i> our buckler; And to. the Holy One of Israel <i>is</i> our King.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p23"></a><b>19 </b>Then thou spakest in vision to thy meek ones, And saidst, “I have laid help upon a Mighty One; “I have exalted one chosen from among the people.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p24"></a><b>20 </b>“I have found David my servant; “With the oil of my holiness have I anointed him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p25"></a><b>21 </b>“Therefore, my hand shall be established with him: “Yea, my arm shall strengthen him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p26"></a><b>22 </b>“The enemy shall not exact upon him, “Nor shall the son of iniquity afflict him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p27"></a><b>23 </b>“And I will break in pieces before his face his oppressors; “And those who hate him I will smite.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p28"></a><b>24 </b>“And my truth and my mercy <i>shall be</i> with him: “And in my name exalted shall be his horn.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p29"></a><b>25 </b>“And I will set in the sea his hand, “And in the rivers his right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p30"></a><b>26 </b>“He shall cry to me, ‘My Father art thou, “‘My God, the Rock of my salvation.’</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p31"></a><b>27 </b>“Also I myself my firstborn will make him, “Higher than the kings of the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p32"></a><b>28 </b>“And for ever will I keep for him my mercy, “And my covenant shall stand firm with him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p33"></a><b>29 </b>“And I will establish for ever his seed, “And his throne as the days of heaven.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p34"></a><b>30 </b>“If forsake shall his children my law, “And in my judgments shall not walk;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p35"></a><b>31 </b>“If my ordinances they shall profane, “And my statutes they shall not keep;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p36"></a><b>32 </b>“Then will I visit with my rod their transgressions, “And with stripes their iniquity.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p37"></a><b>33 </b>“But my mercy will I not withdraw from him; “Nor will I be false in my truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p38"></a><b>34 </b>“I will not profane my covenant, “And that which is gone forth from my lips I will not alter.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p39"></a><b>35 </b>“Once have I sworn by my holiness, “If to David I lie —</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p40"></a><b>36 </b>“His seed for ever shall endure; “And his throne as the sun before me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p41"></a><b>37 </b>“As the moon it shall be established for ever, “And [<i>as</i>] a faithful witness in the heaven.” Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p42"></a><b>38 </b>But thou, even thou, hast abhorred and rejected <i>him</i>; Thou hast been wroth with thy anointed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p43"></a><b>39 </b>Thou hast made to cease the covenant of thy servant; Thou hast profaned to the earth his crown.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p44"></a><b>40 </b>Thou hast broken down all his walls; Thou hast made his fortresses a ruin.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p45"></a><b>41 </b>Plundered him have all who pass by the way: He hath been a reproach to his neighbors.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p46"></a><b>42 </b>Thou hast exalted the right hand of his oppressors; Thou hast made glad all his adversaries.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p47"></a><b>43 </b>Also thou hast blunted the edge of his sword, And hast not made him to stand in battle.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p48"></a><b>44 </b>Thou hast effaced his splendor, And his throne to the ground thou hast east down.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p49"></a><b>45 </b>Thou hast shortened the days of his youth; Thou hast covered him with disgrace. Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p50"></a><b>46 </b>How long, O Jehovah! wilt thou hide thyself for ever? Burn like fire shall thy indignation?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p51"></a><b>47 </b>Remember how short-lived I am!   				 <a name="fr_356"></a><a href="#fn_356"><font size="1">357</font></a>
  				 Wherefore in vain shouldst thou have created all the sons of men?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p53"></a><b>48 </b>What man shall live, and shall not see death? <i>And</i> shall deliver his soul from the hand of the grave? Selah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p54"></a><b>49 </b>Where <i>are</i> thy former compassions, O Lord? Thou hast sworn to David in thy truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p55"></a><b>50 </b>Remember, O Lord! the reproach of thy servants: I have sustained in my bosom all <i>those</i> [<i>reproaches</i>] of the mighty peoples,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p56"></a><b>51 </b>With which thy enemies have reproached thee, O Jehovah! With which they have reproached the footsteps of thy Messiah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p57"></a><b>52 </b>Blessed <i>be</i> Jehovah for evermore. Amen and Amen!</p>  <a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="3rdLevelAllCap12Bld40"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p2"></a>PART FOURTH.  				 <a name="fr_357"></a><a href="#fn_357"><font size="1">358</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p4"></a>PSALM 90</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p5"></a>A Psalm of Moses, the man of God</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p6"></a><b>1 </b>O Lord! a dwelling-place thou hast been to us from generation to generation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p7"></a><b>2 </b>Before the mountains were brought forth, And [<i>before</i>] thou hadst formed the earth and the world, Even from everlasting to everlasting, thou art God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p8"></a><b>3 </b>Thou shalt turn man to destruction, And shalt say, “Return ye sons of Adam.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p9"></a><b>4 </b>For a thousand years in thy sight <i>are</i> as yesterday when it is past, And <i>as</i> a watch in the night.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p10"></a><b>5 </b>Thou overflowest them;   				 <a name="fr_358"></a><a href="#fn_358"><font size="1">359</font></a>
  				 they will be a sleep: In the morning as grass he shall grow.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p12"></a><b>6 </b>In the morning he (<i>or</i> it) shall flourish and grow: At the evening he (<i>or</i> it) shall be cut down, and shall wither.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p13"></a><b>7 </b>For we fail by thy anger, And by thy indignation are we affrighted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p14"></a><b>8 </b>Thou hast set our iniquities before thee, Our secret sins in the light of thy countenance.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p15"></a><b>9 </b>For all our days are passed away in thy indignation: We have spent our years as if a thought.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p16"></a><b>10 </b>In the days of our years <i>there are</i> seventy years; And if through strength, eighty years, Yet is their pride [<i>but</i>] grief and labor; For it passeth by quickly, and we fly away.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p17"></a><b>11 </b>Who knoweth the power of thy anger? And according to thy fear is thy wrath.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p18"></a><b>12 </b>Teach us so to number our days, And we shall apply our heart to wisdom.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p19"></a><b>13 </b>Return, O Jehovah! how long? Be pacified towards thy servants.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p20"></a><b>14 </b>Satiate us early with thy goodness, And we will exult and rejoice all our days.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p21"></a><b>15 </b>Make us joyful according to the days of our affliction; <i>According</i> to the years in which we have seen evil.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p22"></a><b>16 </b>Let thy work appear towards thy servants, And thy glory upon their children.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p23"></a><b>17 </b>And let there be the beauty of the Lord our God upon us; And the work of our hands direct thou upon us; Yea, the work of our hands direct thou.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iii.xxv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p2"></a>PSALM 91</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p3"></a><b>1 </b>He who dwelleth in the secret place of the Most High, Under the shadow of the Almighty shall abide.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p4"></a><b>2 </b>I will say to Jehovah, “<i>Thou art</i> my hope and my fortress:” <i>He is</i> my God; I will hope in him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Surely he shall deliver thee from the snare of the fowler, From the noxious pestilence:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p6"></a><b>4 </b>With his wings he shall protect thee; And under his feathers thou shalt be safe; <i>Thy</i> shield and <i>thy</i> buckler<i> shall be</i> his truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Thou shalt not be afraid at the terror of the night; At the arrow which flieth by day;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p8"></a><b>6 </b>At the destruction which in darkness walketh: At the pestilence which wasteth at noon-day.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p9"></a><b>7 </b>There shall fall at thy side a thousand, And ten thousand at thy right hand: To thee it shall not come nigh.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p10"></a><b>8 </b>Only with thine eyes shalt thou behold, And the reward of the ungodly thou shalt see.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p11"></a><b>9 </b>Because thou, O Jehovah! <i>art</i> my protection; The Most High thou hast made thy refuge.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p12"></a><b>10 </b>There shall not befall thee [<i>any</i>] evil, And the plague shall not come nigh thy tabernacle:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p13"></a><b>11 </b>For to his angels he hath given charge concerning thee, To keep thee in all thy ways.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p14"></a><b>12 </b>Upon their hands they shall bear thee, Lest thou dash against a stone thy foot.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p15"></a><b>13 </b>Over the lion and asp thou shalt walk; Thou shalt tread upon the young lion and dragon.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p16"></a><b>14 </b>Because on me he hath reposed, I will deliver him; I will exalt him because he hath known my name.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p17"></a><b>15 </b>He will call upon me, and I will answer him: With him will I be in trouble; I will deliver him, and will glorify him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxv-p18"></a><b>16 </b>With length of days will I satisfy him, And will show him my salvation.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p2"></a>PSALM 92</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p3"></a><b>1 </b>It is good to give thanks to Jehovah, To sing psalms to thy name, O Most High!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p4"></a><b>2 </b>To proclaim in the morning thy goodness, And thy truth in the night.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Upon the psaltery, and upon the nablum,   				 <a name="fr_359"></a><a href="#fn_359"><font size="1">360</font></a>
  				 Upon higgaion with the harp.   				 <a name="fr_360"></a><a href="#fn_360"><font size="1">361</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p8"></a><b>4 </b>For thou hast made me glad, O Jehovah! in thy works; In the works of thy hands I will exult.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p9"></a><b>5 </b>How magnificent are thy works, O Jehovah! Exceeding deep are thy thoughts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p10"></a><b>6 </b>The man that is foolish shall not know them, Neither shall he who is void of wisdom understand them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p11"></a><b>7 </b>When the wicked flourish as the grass, And all the workers of iniquity spring up, [<i>It is</i>] that they may perish for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p12"></a><b>8 </b>But thou <i>art</i> exalted for evermore, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p13"></a><b>9 </b>For lo! thine enemies, O Jehovah! For lo! thine enemies shall perish; Scattered shall be all the workers of iniquity:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p14"></a><b>10 </b>But thou shalt exalt my horn like <i>that</i> of the unicorn. I am anointed with fresh oil.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p15"></a><b>11 </b>And mine eye shall see [<i>ruin</i>] on my oppressors: [<i>Of destruction</i>,] on those who rise up against me — On those who trouble me hear shall my ears.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p16"></a><b>12 </b>The righteous as the palm tree shall flourish, As the cedar in Lebanon he shall be multiplied.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p17"></a><b>13 </b>Planted in the house of Jehovah, In the courts of our God, they shall flourish.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p18"></a><b>14 </b>Still shall they bud forth in old age; Fat and green shall they be;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p19"></a><b>15 </b>That they may proclaim that upright is Jehovah, my Rock, And <i>that</i> there is no iniquity in him.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv"></a>  		  
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv-p1"></a></p>  		  
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv-p2"></a>PSALMS 93—118</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.i"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.i-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.i-p2"></a>PSALM 93</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.i-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Jehovah hath reigned, He hath put on glory, Put on hath Jehovah strength; He hath girded himself: Also he hath established the world, It shall not be moved.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.i-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Fixed is thy throne; [<i>Even as</i>] from that time   				 <a name="fr_361"></a><a href="#fn_361"><font size="1">362</font></a>
  				 thou art, and from eternity.   				 <a name="fr_362"></a><a href="#fn_362"><font size="1">363</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.i-p8"></a><b>3 </b>Raised have the floods, O Jehovah! Raised have the floods their voice; Raise shall the floods their waves.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.i-p9"></a><b>4 </b>By reason of the voices   				 <a name="fr_363"></a><a href="#fn_363"><font size="1">364</font></a>
  				 of the great waters Terrible are the waves of the sea: Terrible on high is Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.i-p11"></a><b>5 </b>Thy testimonies are verified exceedingly; To thy house <i>is</i> glory; The holiness of Jehovah <i>is</i> for length of days.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.ii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p2"></a>PSALM 94</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! God of vengeances! O God of vengeances! shine forth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Lift up thyself; O judge of the earth! Render a reward to the proud.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>How long shall the ungodly, O Jehovah! How long shall the ungodly triumph?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>They pour forth, they speak hard things, Extol themselves do all the workers of iniquity.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Thy people, O Jehovah! they break in pieces; And thy inheritance they afflict:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p8"></a><b>6 </b>The widow, and the stranger they slay, And the orphans they put to death.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>And they have said, “God shall not see, “The God of Jacob shall not know..”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>Understand, ye stupid among the people! And ye fools! when will ye be wise?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p11"></a><b>9 </b>He who planted the ear shall not He hear? He who formed the eye, shall not He see?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p12"></a><b>10 </b>He who chastiseth the nations, shall not He correct? He who teacheth man knowledge?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p13"></a><b>11 </b>Jehovah knoweth the thoughts of men that they are vain.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p14"></a><b>12 </b>Blessed <i>is</i> the man whom thou hast instructed, O God! And out of thy law hast taught;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p15"></a><b>13 </b>To give him rest from days of evil, Whilst there is digged for the ungodly [<i>man</i>] a pit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p16"></a><b>14 </b>Surely Jehovah will not cast off his people, And his inheritance he will not forsake.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p17"></a><b>15 </b>For return shall judgment unto righteousness, And [<i>follow</i>] after him shall all the upright in heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p18"></a><b>16 </b>Who will rise up for me against my adversaries? Who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p19"></a><b>17 </b>Unless Jehovah had been a help to me, My soul had well-nigh dwelt in silence.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p20"></a><b>18 </b>If I said, “Slidden hath my foot,” Thy goodness, O Jehovah! hath sustained me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p21"></a><b>19 </b>In the multitude of my thoughts, Within me thy comforts cheer my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p22"></a><b>20 </b>Shall the throne of iniquities have fellowship with thee, Framing molestation for law?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p23"></a><b>21 </b>They will gather together against the soul of the righteous, And the blood of the innocent they will condemn.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p24"></a><b>22 </b>But Jehovah hath been to me for a fortress; And my God for the rock of my confidence:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ii-p25"></a><b>23 </b>And he shall retribute upon them their own iniquity, And in their wickedness he shall destroy them; Destroy them shall Jehovah our God.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.iii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p2"></a>PSALM 95</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Come let us exult to Jehovah; Let us shout for joy to the Rock of our salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Let us come before his face with praise, In psalms let us shout for joy unto him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>For a great God <i>is</i> Jehovah, And a great King, above all gods.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>For in his hand <i>are</i> the deep places of the earth; And the heights of the mountains are his.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>For his is the sea, and he made it; And the dry land his hands formed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p8"></a><b>6 </b>Come ye, let us worship, and fall down; Let us kneel before the face of Jehovah, our Maker.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>For he <i>is</i> our God, And we [<i>are</i>] the people of his pastures, And the flock of his hand; To-day, if his voice ye will hear,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>Harden not your heart, as in Meribah; As in the day of Massah in the desert,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p11"></a><b>9 </b>When tempt me did your fathers; They proved me, though they had seen my work.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p12"></a><b>10 </b>Forty years I strove with this generation, And said, “They are a people erring in heart, “And they have not known my ways.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iii-p13"></a><b>11 </b>Wherefore I swear in my wrath, “If they shall enter into my rest —”</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.iv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p2"></a>PSALM 96</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Sing ye to Jehovah a song that is new, Sing to Jehovah all the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Sing to Jehovah, bless his name; Publish from day to day his salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Tell among the heathen his glory; Among all the peoples his wonders.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p6"></a><b>4 </b>For great <i>is</i> Jehovah, and to be praised highly; Terrible [<i>is</i>] he above all gods.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p7"></a><b>5 </b>For all the gods of the nations are vanities; But Jehovah made the heavens.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p8"></a><b>6 </b>Strength and majesty <i>go</i> before him; Power and glory <i>are</i> in his sanctuary.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p9"></a><b>7 </b>Ascribe to Jehovah, O ye congregations of peoples! Ascribe to Jehovah glory and strength.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p10"></a><b>8 </b>Ascribe to Jehovah the glory of his name; Bring an offering, and enter into his courts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p11"></a><b>9 </b>Worship before Jehovah in the beauty of the sanctuary; Tremble before his face let the whole earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p12"></a><b>10 </b>Say ye among the heathen, “Jehovah reigneth; “Truly established shall be the world, it shall not be moved: “He shall judge the peoples in righteousness.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p13"></a><b>11 </b>Rejoice let the heavens, and exult let the earth; Thunder let the sea, and the fullness thereof.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p14"></a><b>12 </b>Exult let the field, and all that is in it; Shout for joy together let all the trees of the wood</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.iv-p15"></a><b>13 </b>Before Jehovah; for he cometh, For he cometh to judge the earth: He shall judge the world in righteousness, And the peoples in his truth.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.v"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p2"></a>PSALM 97</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Jehovah reigneth: Exult let the earth, Rejoice let the great islands.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Clouds and darkness <i>are</i> round about him; Righteousness and judgment <i>are</i> the seat of his throne.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p5"></a><b>3 </b>A fire before his face shall go, And shall burn up round about his enemies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p6"></a><b>4 </b>Enlighten did his lightnings the world; See and tremble shall the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p7"></a><b>5 </b>The mountains like wax melted at the presence of Jehovah, At the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p8"></a><b>6 </b>Declared have the heavens his righteousness, And seen have all the peoples his glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p9"></a><b>7 </b>Confounded be all those who serve graven images, Who glory in <i>their</i> inventions: Worship before him let all the gods.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p10"></a><b>8 </b>Heard and rejoiced hath Zion; Exulted have the daughters of Judah, Because of thy judgments, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p11"></a><b>9 </b>For thou, O Jehovah! <i>art</i> high above all the earth: Exceedingly exalted art thou above all gods.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p12"></a><b>10 </b>Ye who love Jehovah, hate evil: He preserveth the souls of his meek ones; From the hand of the ungodly he will deliver them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p13"></a><b>11 </b>Light is sown for the righteous, And for the upright in heart joy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.v-p14"></a><b>12 </b>Rejoice, O ye righteous! in Jehovah, And celebrate the memory of his holiness.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.vi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p2"></a>PSALM 98</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p3"></a>A Psalm</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Sing ye to Jehovah a song that is new, For marvels he hath done: Salvation wrought for him hath his own right hand, And the arm of his holiness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Made known hath Jehovah his salvation: In the sight of the heathen he hath revealed his righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>He hath remembered his goodness and <i>his</i> truth towards the house of Israel: Seen have all the ends of the earth the salvation of our God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Exult to Jehovah all the earth; Make a loud noise, and exult, and sing psalms.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Sing psalms to Jehovah upon the harp, Upon the harp, and with the voice of song:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>With trumpets, and the voice of the cornet, Sing psalms before the King, Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Roar let the sea, and the fullness thereof; The world, and those who dwell therein.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Let the floods clap the hand: Together let the mountains exult</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Before Jehovah: for he cometh to judge the earth; He shall judge the world in righteousness, And the peoples with rectitude.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.vii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p2"></a>PSALM 99</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Jehovah reigneth; tremble let the people: He dwelleth <i>between</i> the cherubim; moved let be the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Jehovah in Zion is great; And exalted is he above all nations.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>They shall acknowledge thy great and terrible name: It is holy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>And the strength of the king loveth judgment; Thou hast established rectitude; Judgement and righteousness in Jacob thou hast done.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Exalt ye Jehovah our God, And worship at his footstool: He is holy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p8"></a><b>6 </b>Moses and Aaron among his priests, And Samuel among those who call upon his name; They cried to Jehovah and he answered them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>In the pillar of the cloud he spake to them: They kept his testimonies And his statutes which he gave them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>O Jehovah, our God! thou didst answer them: A God propitious thou wast to them, And [<i>yet</i>] taking vengeance upon their works.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.vii-p11"></a><b>9 </b>Exalt ye Jehovah our God, And worship at the mountain of his holiness; For holy <i>is</i> Jehovah our God.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.viii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p2"></a>PSALM 100</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p3"></a>A Psalm for praising</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Sing aloud to Jehovah,   				 <a name="fr_364"></a><a href="#fn_364"><font size="1">365</font></a>
  				 all ye <i>inhabitants</i> of the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p6"></a><b>2 </b>Serve Jehovah with gladness; Come into his presence with exultation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p7"></a><b>3 </b>Know that Jehovah He is God; He made us, and not we ourselves: <i>We are</i> his people, and the flock of his pasture.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p8"></a><b>4 </b>Enter his gates with praise, his courts with exultation; Celebrate him,   				 <a name="fr_365"></a><a href="#fn_365"><font size="1">366</font></a>
  				 bless his name:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.viii-p10"></a><b>5 </b>For good is Jehovah, For ever <i>endureth</i> his mercy, And from generation to generation his truth.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.ix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p2"></a>PSALM 101</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p3"></a>A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Of mercy and judgment I will sing; To thee, O Jehovah, will I sing psalms.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p5"></a><b>2 </b>I will act wisely in a perfect way, Until thou comest to me; I will walk in the integrity of my heart in the midst of my house.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p6"></a><b>3 </b>I will not set before my eyes a wicked thing; The work of those who turn aside I hate; It shall not adhere to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p7"></a><b>4 </b>A heart perverse shall depart from me; Evil I will not know.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p8"></a><b>5 </b>He who slandereth in secret his neighbor, him will I destroy: The lofty in look and the wide in heart him I will not suffer.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p9"></a><b>6 </b>My eyes <i>shall be</i> upon the faithful of the land, That they may dwell with me: He who walketh in an upright way, [<i>Even</i>] he shall minister to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p10"></a><b>7 </b>He shall not dwell in the midst of my house, he who worketh deceit; He who speaketh lies shall not be established before my eyes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.ix-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Early will I destroy all the ungodly of the land; That I may cut off from the city of Jehovah all the workers of iniquity.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.x"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p2"></a>PSALM 102</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p3"></a>A Prayer for the afflicted when he shall be shut up, and shall pour out his meditation before Jehovah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! hear my prayer, And let my cry to thee come.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Hide not thy face from me in the day of my afflictions; Incline to me thy ear; In the day when I cry, make haste, answer me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For consumed like smoke are   				 <a name="fr_366"></a><a href="#fn_366"><font size="1">367</font></a>
  				 my days, And my bones as a hearth are burnt up.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p8"></a><b>4 </b>Smitten like grass, and withered is my heart, Because I have forgotten to eat my bread.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p9"></a><b>5 </b>By reason of the voice of my groaning, Cleave do my bones to my flesh.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p10"></a><b>6 </b>I am become like a pelican of the desert, I am become as an owl of the solitudes;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p11"></a><b>7 </b>I have watched and am as the sparrow <i>Which is</i> solitary upon the roof of the house.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Daily reproach me do my enemies; And those who are mad against me, by me have sworn.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p13"></a><b>9 </b>For ashes as bread I have eaten, And my drink with weeping   				 <a name="fr_367"></a><a href="#fn_367"><font size="1">368</font></a>
  				 I have mingled.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p15"></a><b>10 </b>Because of thy indignation and thy wrath; For thou hast lifted me up and cast me down.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p16"></a><b>11 </b>My days <i>are</i> as a shadow which declineth; And as grass I am dried up.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p17"></a><b>12 </b>And thou, O Jehovah! for ever shalt dwell, And thy memorial from generation to generation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p18"></a><b>13 </b>Thou thyself shalt arise, thou shalt have mercy upon Zion; For it is time to compassionate her, For come is the appointed time.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p19"></a><b>14 </b>For take pleasure do thy servants in her stones, And upon her dust they will have compassion.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p20"></a><b>15 </b>And fear shall the Gentiles the name of Jehovah, And all the kings of the earth thy glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p21"></a><b>16 </b>For Jehovah hath builded Zion, He hath appeared in his glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p22"></a><b>17 </b>He hath regarded the prayer of the solitary, And hath not despised their prayer.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p23"></a><b>18 </b>This shall be written for the generation to come, And the people [<i>to be</i>] created shall praise him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p24"></a><b>19 </b>For he hath looked from the high <i>place</i> of his holiness, Jehovah from the heavens upon the earth hath looked,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p25"></a><b>20 </b>To hear the groaning of the prisoners To release the sons of death;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p26"></a><b>21 </b>That declared in Zion may be the name of Jehovah, And his praise in Jerusalem;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p27"></a><b>22 </b>When gathered shall be the peoples together, And the kingdoms to serve Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p28"></a><b>23 </b>He hath afflicted in the way my strength, He hath shortened my days.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p29"></a><b>24 </b>I said, O my God! take me not away in the midst of my days; <i>For</i> throughout generations of generations <i>are</i> thy years.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p30"></a><b>25 </b>Aforetime the earth thou hast founded; And the work of thy hands serve the heavens.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p31"></a><b>26 </b>They shall perish but thou shalt endure; And they all as a garment shall grow old; As a vesture thou shalt change them, and they shall be changed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p32"></a><b>27 </b>But thou <i>art always</i> the same, And thy years shall not fail.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.x-p33"></a><b>28 </b>The children of thy servants shall dwell, And their seed before thee shall be established.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p2"></a>PSALM 103</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Bless, O my soul! Jehovah, And all my inward parts <i>bless</i> his holy name.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Bless, O my soul! Jehovah, And forget not all his bounties.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Who forgiveth all thy iniquities; Who healeth all thy infirmities;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Who redeemeth from the grave thy life; Who crowneth thee with mercy and compassions;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Who satisfieth with good thy mouth: Renewed as <i>that</i> of the eagle shall be thy youth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Execute doth Jehovah righteousness And judgments for all who are oppressed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>He made known his ways to Moses, To the children of Israel his doings.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Compassionate and merciful <i>is</i> Jehovah, Slow to anger and abundant in goodness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>He will not always chide; Neither for ever will he keep [<i>his anger</i>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Not according to our sins hath he dealt with us, Nor according to our iniquities hath he recompensed us.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>For in proportion to the height of the heavens above the earth, Hath been the greatness of his goodness upon those who fear him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>As far distant as is the east from the west, So far hath he removed from us our sills.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p16"></a><b>13 </b>As a father is compassionate towards his children, So is Jehovah compassionate towards those who fear him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p17"></a><b>14 </b>For he knoweth of what we are made; He hath remembered that dust are we.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p18"></a><b>15 </b>Man... as grass <i>are</i> his days: As a flower of the field, so he flourisheth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p19"></a><b>16 </b>As soon as the wind passeth over it, it is not; And know it no more shall the place thereof.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p20"></a><b>17 </b>But the goodness of Jehovah <i>is</i> from everlasting to everlasting upon those who fear him, And his righteousness upon the children’s children;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p21"></a><b>18 </b>To those who keep his covenant, And are mindful of his statutes to do them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p22"></a><b>19 </b>Jehovah in the heavens hath established his throne; And his kingdom over all hath dominion.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p23"></a><b>20 </b>Bless Jehovah, <i>ye</i> his angels mighty in strength! Who do his commandment, in hearing the voice of his word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p24"></a><b>21 </b>Bless Jehovah, all <i>ye</i> his armies! Ye ministers of his, who do his pleasure.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xi-p25"></a><b>22 </b>Bless Jehovah, all ye his works! In all places of his dominion: Bless, O my soul! Jehovah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p2"></a>PSALM 104</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Bless, O my soul! Jehovah: O Jehovah, my God! thou art great exceedingly; With praise and honor thou hast clothed thyself.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Being arrayed with light as with a garment; Spreading out the heavens as a curtain;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Flooring in the waters his upper rooms; Making the clouds his chariot; Walking upon the wings of the wind:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>Making the winds his messengers; His ministers a fire that flameth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>He hath founded the earth upon its foundations, So that it shall not be moved for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p8"></a><b>6 </b>With the deep as with a garment he hath covered it: Above the mountains stand shall the waters.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>At thy rebuke they shall flee; At the voice of thy thunder they shall suddenly pass away.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>Ascend shall the mountains and descend shall the valleys To the place which thou hast founded for them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p11"></a><b>9 </b>A boundary thou hast set, they shall not pass over <i>it</i>: They shall not return to cover the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p12"></a><b>10 </b>Sending out springs by the valleys, <i>Which</i> between the hills shall run.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p13"></a><b>11 </b>Drink <i>thereof</i> shall all the beasts of the field: Quench shall the wild asses their thirst.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p14"></a><b>12 </b>Nigh time the fowl of the heaven shall dwell, From the midst of the branches they shall send out their voice.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p15"></a><b>13 </b>Watering the mountains from his chambers: From the fruit of thy works satisfied shall be the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p16"></a><b>14 </b>Making grass to grow for cattle, And herb for the service of mm: That he may bring forth bread out of the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p17"></a><b>15 </b>And wine cheereth the heart of man, To make <i>his</i> face to shine with oil, And bread sustaineth the heart of man.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p18"></a><b>16 </b>Satiated shall be the trees of Jehovah; The cedars of Lebanon which he hath planted:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p19"></a><b>17 </b>For there the birds build their nests: [<i>As for</i>] the stork, the fir trees are her dwelling.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p20"></a><b>18 </b>The high mountains <i>are</i> for the deer; The rocks a place of shelter for the hedgehogs.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p21"></a><b>19 </b>He hath made the moon for set times: The sun knoweth his going down.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p22"></a><b>20 </b>Thou makest darkness, and it is night; Wherein do creep forth all the beasts of the forest.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p23"></a><b>21 </b>The lions roar after their prey, And in seeking from God their food.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p24"></a><b>22 </b>Rise shall the sun, and they shall gather themselves together, And in their dens shall lie down.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p25"></a><b>23 </b>Go forth shall man to his work, And to his labor, until the evening.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p26"></a><b>24 </b>How magnificent are thy works! O Jehovah! All things in wisdom thou hast made: Filled is the earth with thy riches.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p27"></a><b>25 </b>This sea great, and wide in extent; Therein are creeping things inntanerable, Beasts both small and great.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p28"></a><b>26 </b>There the ships go, And the leviathan, which thou hast formed to sport in it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p29"></a><b>27 </b>All things on thee do wait, That thou mayest give <i>them</i> their food in its season.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p30"></a><b>28 </b>Thou shalt give it them, they shall gather [<i>it</i>:] Thou shalt open thy hand, they shall be satisfied with good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p31"></a><b>29 </b>Thou shalt hide thy face, they shall be afraid: Thou shalt take away their spirit, they shall die, and to their dust shall return.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p32"></a><b>30 </b>Thou shalt send forth thy Spirit, they shall be created: And thou shalt renew the face of the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p33"></a><b>31 </b>Glory be to Jehovah for ever: Rejoice let Jehovah in his works.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p34"></a><b>32 </b>He looketh upon the earth, and it trembleth: If he touch the mountains, they shall smoke.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p35"></a><b>33 </b>I will sing to Jehovah whilst I live: I will sing psalms to my God as long as I have my being.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p36"></a><b>34 </b>Let my speech be acceptable to him: I will rejoice in Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xii-p37"></a><b>35 </b>Perish let sinners from the earth, And the ungodly till they cease to be any more. Bless, O my soul! Jehovah. Hallelujah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p2"></a>PSALM 105</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Celebrate ye Jehovah; invoke his name: Announce among the peoples his works.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Sing ye to him: sing psalms to him: Speak of all his wonders.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Rejoice ye in his holy name: Rejoice let the heart of those who seek Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>Seek ye Jehovah, and his strength; Seek his face continually.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Remember the marvelous works which he hath done; His wonders, and the judgments of his mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p8"></a><b>6 </b><i>Ye</i> seed of Abraham, his servant, The sons of Jacob his chosen one:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>He <i>is</i> Jehovah our God; Through all the earth are his judgments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>He hath remembered for ever his covenant, The word <i>which</i> he commanded to a thousand generations:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p11"></a><b>9 </b>Which he made with Abraham, And his oath <i>which he swore</i> to Isaac;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p12"></a><b>10 </b>And established it to Jacob for a law, To Israel for an everlasting covenant:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p13"></a><b>11 </b>Saying, “To thee will I give the land of Canaan, “The cord of your inheritance.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p14"></a><b>12 </b>When they were very few in number; And strangers in it;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p15"></a><b>13 </b>And walked about from nation to nation, From <i>one</i> kingdom to another people,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p16"></a><b>14 </b>He did not suffer men to hurt them; And rebuked for their sake kings;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p17"></a><b>15 </b><i>Saying</i>, “Touch not my anointed ones, “And to my prophets do no harm.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p18"></a><b>16 </b>And he called a famine upon the land; All the stall of bread he broke.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p19"></a><b>17 </b>He sent before them a man, For a slave sold was Joseph.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p20"></a><b>18 </b>They afflicted in the fetters his feet: The iron entered into his soul:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p21"></a><b>19 </b>Until the time that his word came: The word of Jehovah tried him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p22"></a><b>20 </b>Send did the king and loosed him; Even the ruler of the peoples, and freed him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p23"></a><b>21 </b>He made him lord over his house; And ruler over all his substance:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p24"></a><b>22 </b>To bind his princes at his pleasure; And to teach his elders wisdom.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p25"></a><b>23 </b>And come did Israel into Egypt; And Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p26"></a><b>24 </b>And he increased his people exceedingly, He multiplied them above their oppressors.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p27"></a><b>25 </b>He turned their heart so that they hated his people, And dealt craftily with his servants.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p28"></a><b>26 </b>He sent Moses, his servant; Aaron, whom he chose.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p29"></a><b>27 </b>They set among them the words of his signs, And <i>his</i> miracles in the land of Ham.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p30"></a><b>28 </b>He sent darkness, and made it dark; And they were not rebellious against his words.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p31"></a><b>29 </b>He turned their waters into blood, And killed their fish.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p32"></a><b>30 </b>Their land brought forth frogs, <i>Yea even</i> within the chambers of their kings.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p33"></a><b>31 </b>He spake and there came a swarm of flies, Lice in all their borders.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p34"></a><b>32 </b>He gave them for rain, hail, Flaming fire upon their land.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p35"></a><b>33 </b>And he smote their vines and their fig-trees; And destroyed <i>every</i> tree of their border.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p36"></a><b>34 </b>He spake, and there came the locust, And the caterpillar without number;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p37"></a><b>35 </b>And they devoured all the herbage in their land, And consumed the fruit of their ground.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p38"></a><b>36 </b>And he smote all the firstborn in their land, The beginning of all their strength.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p39"></a><b>37 </b>And he brought them forth with silver and gold: And not one among their tribes was a feeble person.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p40"></a><b>38 </b>Glad was Egypt at their departure; For fallen upon them had their terror.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p41"></a><b>39 </b>He spread out a cloud for a covering; And fire to give light by the night.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p42"></a><b>40 </b>He   				 <a name="fr_368"></a><a href="#fn_368"><font size="1">369</font></a>
  				 asked, and brought quails, And with the bread of heaven he filled them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p44"></a><b>41 </b>He opened the rock, and there gushed out waters; They ran in the dry <i>places like</i> a river.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p45"></a><b>42 </b>For he remembered the word of his holiness, <i>Which he had spoken</i> to Abraham his servant.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p46"></a><b>43 </b>And he brought forth his people with joy, With exultation his chosen ones.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p47"></a><b>44 </b>And he gave them the lands of the nations: And the labor of the peoples they inherited.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiii-p48"></a><b>45 </b>That they might keep his ordinances, And that his law they might observe. Hallelujah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p2"></a>PSALM 106</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p3"></a>Hallelujah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Celebrate Jehovah, for he is good; For to everlasting <i>is</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Who shall express the mighty acts of Jehovah? Who shall declare all his praise?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Blessed are they who keep judgment, <i>Blessed</i> is he who doeth righteousness at all times.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Remember me, O Jehovah! with the good will [<i>which thou</i> <i>bearest towards</i>] thy people. Visit me with thy salvation;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>That I may see the good of thy chosen ones, That I may rejoice in the joy of thy nation, That I may glory with thy heritage.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>We have sinned with our fathers, We have acted iniquitously, we have done wickedly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Our fathers in Egypt understood not thy wonders; They remembered not the multitude of thy kindnesses; And they rebelled at the sea, at the Red Sea.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Yet he saved them for the sake of his own name, That. he might cause to be known his power.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p12"></a><b>9 </b>And he rebuked the Red Sea, and it was dried up; And he made them walk in the deeps as in a desert.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p13"></a><b>10 </b>And he saved them from the hand of the enemy, And redeemed them from the hand of the adversary.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p14"></a><b>11 </b>And cover did the waters their oppressors: One of them was not left.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Then they believed his words; They sang his praise.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p16"></a><b>13 </b>They made haste, they forgat his works; They did not wait for his counsel;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p17"></a><b>14 </b>And they lusted greatly in the desert, And tempted God in the wilderness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p18"></a><b>15 </b>And he gave them their request; But sent leanness into their souls.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p19"></a><b>16 </b>And they envied Moses in the camp, And Aaron, the saint of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p20"></a><b>17 </b>Open did the earth and swallowed up Dathan, And covered over the tent of Abiram.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p21"></a><b>18 </b>And kindled was a fire in their company, The flame burned up the ungodly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p22"></a><b>19 </b>They made a calf in Horeb, And worshipped before the molten image.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p23"></a><b>20 </b>And they changed their glory Into the likeness of an ox that eateth hay.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p24"></a><b>21 </b>They forgat God their Savior, Who had done great things in Egypt;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p25"></a><b>22 </b>Miracles in the land of Ham, Terrible things at the Red Sea.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p26"></a><b>23 </b>And he said that he would destroy them, Unless Moses his chosen had stood in the breach before his face, To turn away his wrath, that he might not destroy <i>them</i></p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p27"></a><b>24 </b>And they despised the land of pleasantness; They believed not his word;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p28"></a><b>25 </b>And they mutinied in their tents, They hearkened not to the voice of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p29"></a><b>26 </b>And he lifted tip his hand against them, To destroy them in the desert:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p30"></a><b>27 </b>And to scatter their seed among the heathen, And to disperse them throughout the lands.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p31"></a><b>28 </b>And they joined themselves to Baal-peor, And ate the sacrifices of <i>things</i> dead.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p32"></a><b>29 </b>And they provoked <i>God</i> to anger by their works: And break in upon them did the plague.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p33"></a><b>30 </b>Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: And stayed was the plague.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p34"></a><b>31 </b>And <i>that</i> was imputed to him for righteousness From generation to generation, even for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p35"></a><b>32 </b>And they provoked <i>him</i> to anger at the waters of strife, And it turned out in to Moses on their account:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p36"></a><b>33 </b>For they embittered his spirit, And he spake [<i>rashly</i>] with his lips.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p37"></a><b>34 </b>They did not destroy the nations, As Jehovah had commanded them:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p38"></a><b>35 </b>And they were mingled with the heathen, And learned their works:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p39"></a><b>36 </b>And they served their idols; Which were to them for ruin.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p40"></a><b>37 </b>And they sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p41"></a><b>38 </b>And they shed innocent blood, The blood of their sons and of their daughters, Whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan; And polluted was the land with bloods.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p42"></a><b>39 </b>And they were defiled in their own works, And were adulterous in their own inventions.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p43"></a><b>40 </b>Then   				 <a name="fr_369"></a><a href="#fn_369"><font size="1">370</font></a>
  				 burn did the wrath of Jehovah against his people, And he abhorred his inheritance;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p45"></a><b>41 </b>And he delivered them into the hands of the heathen; And those had dominion over them who hated them:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p46"></a><b>42 </b>And subdue them did their enemies, And they were afflicted under their hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p47"></a><b>43 </b>Many times did he deliver them; But they provoked <i>him</i> with their counsels, And were oppressed in their iniquity.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p48"></a><b>44 </b>Yet he saw when they were in distress, And heard their cry:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p49"></a><b>45 </b>And he remembered towards them his covenant; And it repented him according to the greatness of his mercies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p50"></a><b>46 </b>And he made them to find pity Before all who had led them captive.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p51"></a><b>47 </b>Save us, O Jehovah, our God! And gather us from among the heathen, That we may celebrate thy holy name, That we may glory in thy praise.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xiv-p52"></a><b>48 </b>Blessed <i>be</i> Jehovah, the God of Israel, From everlasting to everlasting; And say let all the people, Amen. Praise ye Jehovah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="3rdLevelAllCap12Bld40"><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p2"></a>PART FIFTH.  				 <a name="fr_370"></a><a href="#fn_370"><font size="1">371</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p4"></a>PSALM 107</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p5"></a><b>1 </b>“Celebrate Jehovah, for he is good, “For to everlasting is his mercy.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p6"></a><b>2 </b>Say <i>this</i> let the redeemed of Jehovah, Whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the afflicter.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p7"></a><b>3 </b>Whom he hath gathered from the lands, From the east, and from the west, From the north, and from the south.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p8"></a><b>4 </b>They wandered from the way in the solitary desert; A city of habitation they found not:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p9"></a><b>5 </b>Hungry, also thirsty, <i>So that</i> their soul within them fainted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p10"></a><b>6 </b>Then they cried to Jehovah in their distress, And from their troubles he delivered them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p11"></a><b>7 </b>And he directed them by a right way, That they might come to a city of habitation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Let them celebrate before Jehovah his mercy, His marvelous works before the sons of men.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p13"></a><b>9 </b>For he hath satisfied the soul that longeth, And the soul that is famished he hath filled with good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p14"></a><b>10 </b>Those who dwell in darkness, and in the shadow of death, Bound in affliction and iron;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p15"></a><b>11 </b>Because they rebelled against the words of God, And the counsel of the Most High they despised:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p16"></a><b>12 </b>And he humbled with trouble their heart; They were afflicted and <i>there was</i> none to help <i>them</i></p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p17"></a><b>13 </b>They cried to Jehovah in their distress: From their troubles he delivered them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p18"></a><b>14 </b>He rescued them from darkness and the shadow of death, And their chains he broke asunder.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p19"></a><b>15 </b>Let them celebrate before Jehovah his mercy, And his marvelous works before the sons of men.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p20"></a><b>16 </b>For he hath broken the gates of brass, And the bars of iron he hath shivered.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p21"></a><b>17 </b>Fools on account of the way of their transgression; And on account of their iniquities are afflicted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p22"></a><b>18 </b>All food loathe doth their soul; And they approach the gates of death.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p23"></a><b>19 </b>Then they cry to Jehovah in their trouble: From their straits he sayeth them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p24"></a><b>20 </b>He sendeth his word, and healeth them, And rescueth them from all their corruptions.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p25"></a><b>21 </b>Let them celebrate before Jehovah his mercy, And his marvelous works before the sons of men.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p26"></a><b>22 </b>And let them sacrifice sacrifices of praise, And announce his works with exultation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p27"></a><b>23 </b>Those who go down to the sea in ships, Trading in the great waters,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p28"></a><b>24 </b>These men see the works of Jehovah, His wonders in the deep.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p29"></a><b>25 </b>He speaketh and raiseth the wind of storm, And lifteth high the waves thereof.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p30"></a><b>26 </b>They mount up to the heavens, They descend into the deeps; Their soul in   				 <a name="fr_371"></a><a href="#fn_371"><font size="1">372</font></a>
  				 <i>their</i> distress is melted away.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p32"></a><b>27 </b>They are tossed and stagger as a drunken man, And all their skill is swallowed up.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p33"></a><b>28 </b>And they cry to Jehovah in their distress, And from their troubles he bringeth them out.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p34"></a><b>29 </b>He maketh the storm a calm, So that quiet are the waves thereof.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p35"></a><b>30 </b>And they rejoice because they are stilled; And he leadeth them unto the haven of their desire.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p36"></a><b>31 </b>Let them celebrate before Jehovah his mercy, And his wonders before the sons of men;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p37"></a><b>32 </b>And let them exalt him in the congregation of the people, And in the assembly of the elders let them praise him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p38"></a><b>33 </b>He turneth rivers into a desert, And springs of water into dryness;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p39"></a><b>34 </b>A land that is fruitful into saltness, For the wickedness of those who dwell therein.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p40"></a><b>35 </b>He turneth the desert into a pool of water, And the land of barrenness into springs of water.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p41"></a><b>36 </b>And there he causeth to dwell the famished, That they may prepare a city of habitation;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p42"></a><b>37 </b>And sow fields, and plant vineyards, And eat the fruit of increase.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p43"></a><b>38 </b>And he blesseth them, and they multiply exceedingly; And their cattle he doth not diminish,.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p44"></a><b>39 </b>Afterwards they are diminished and brought low, By reason of anguish, affliction, and sorrow.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p45"></a><b>40 </b>He poureth contempt upon princes, And maketh them to wander in the waste where there is no path.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p46"></a><b>41 </b>And he raiseth the afflicted from <i>his</i> misery, And maketh like a flock [<i>his</i>] families.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p47"></a><b>42 </b>See shall the upright ones and shall rejoice: And all iniquity shall stop her mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xv-p48"></a><b>43 </b>Who is wise, and he will observe these things, And they shall understand the loving-kindness of Jehovah?</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p2"></a>PSALM 108</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p3"></a>A Song of a Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Prepared <i>is</i> my heart, O God! prepared is my heart, I will chant and will sing psalms, even with my glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Awake, psaltery and harp: I will arise at the dawn of day.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>I will celebrate thee, among the peoples, O Jehovah! And will sing psalms to thee among the nations:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For great above the heavens, is thy goodness; And unto the clouds is thy truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Be thou exalted above the heavens, O God! And above all the earth thy glory:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>That thy beloved ones may be delivered: Save by thy right hand, and hear me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice: I will divide Shechem, And the valley of Succoth I will measure.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Mine <i>is</i> Gilead, mine is Manasseh; And Ephraim <i>is</i> the strength of my head; Judah my lawgiver.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Moab the pot for my washing; Over Edom will I cast my shoe; Over Palestina will I triumph.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>Who will lead me into the city fortified? Who will lead me even into Edom?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Wilt not thou, O God! who hadst cast us off? And [<i>thou</i>] O God! [<i>who</i>] didst not go forth with our armies?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Grant us relief from   				 <a name="fr_372"></a><a href="#fn_372"><font size="1">373</font></a>
  				 trouble; For vain is the help of man.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvi-p17"></a><b>13 </b>Through God we shall do valiantly, And he shall tread down our adversaries.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xvii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p2"></a>PSALM 109</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O God of my praise! be not silent;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>For the mouth of the ungodly man, and the mouth of deceit upon me are opened; They have talked with me with a tongue of guile:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>And with words of hatred they have encompassed me, And have fought against me without a cause.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>[<i>In return</i>] for my love they have been my adversaries; But I <i>set myself</i> to prayer.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>And they have requited me evil for good, And hatred for my love.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Set thou over him an ungodly man; And let the adversary stand at his right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>When he is judged let him go forth condemned,   				 <a name="fr_373"></a><a href="#fn_373"><font size="1">374</font></a>
  				 And let his prayer be turned into sin.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Let his days be few; His office let another receive.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p13"></a><b>9 </b>Let his children be fatherless, And his wife a widow.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p14"></a><b>10 </b>And in wandering let his children wander and beg,   				 <a name="fr_374"></a><a href="#fn_374"><font size="1">375</font></a>
  				 And seek [<i>for bread</i>] out of their waste places.   				 <a name="fr_375"></a><a href="#fn_375"><font size="1">376</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p17"></a><b>11 </b>Catch let the extortioner all which he hath, And let strangers plunder his labor.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p18"></a><b>12 </b>Let there be none prolonging mercy to him; And let there be none to have compassion upon his orphans.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p19"></a><b>13 </b>Let his posterity be destroyed;   				 <a name="fr_376"></a><a href="#fn_376"><font size="1">377</font></a>
  				 In the generation following let their name be blotted out.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p21"></a><b>14 </b>Remembered let be the iniquity of his fathers before Jehovah; And the wickedness   				 <a name="fr_377"></a><a href="#fn_377"><font size="1">378</font></a>
  				 of his mother let it not be blotted out.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p23"></a><b>15 </b>Let them be before Jehovah continually, And let him blot out from the earth their memorial;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p24"></a><b>16 </b>Because he remembered not to do mercy, And persecuted the man [<i>that was</i>] wretched and poor, And afflicted in heart, to put <i>him</i> to death.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p25"></a><b>17 </b>He loved cursing, and let it come upon him: He delighted not in blessing, and let it be far from him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p26"></a><b>18 </b>And let him be clothed with cursing as with a garment; And let it come as water into his entrails, And as oil into his bones.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p27"></a><b>19 </b>Let it be to him as a mantle to cover him, And as a girdle with which continually he may gird himself</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p28"></a><b>20 </b>Let this be the recompense   				 <a name="fr_378"></a><a href="#fn_378"><font size="1">379</font></a>
  				 of my adversaries from Jehovah, And of those who speak evil against my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p30"></a><b>21 </b>But thou, O Jehovah, my Lord! deal thou with me for the sake of thy name: Because good <i>is</i> thy mercy, deliver me;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p31"></a><b>22 </b>For poor and needy I am, And my heart is wounded within me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p32"></a><b>23 </b>As a shadow when it declineth, I walk about; I am shaken off as the locust.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p33"></a><b>24 </b>My knees are become feeble through fasting; And my flesh hath fallen away from <i>its</i> fatness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p34"></a><b>25 </b>But I am become a reproach to them; When they see me they shake their head.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p35"></a><b>26 </b>Help me, O Jehovah, my God! Save me according to thy mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p36"></a><b>27 </b>And they shall know that this is thy hand, <i>That</i> thou, O Jehovah! hast done it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p37"></a><b>28 </b>They shall curse, but thou shalt bless; When they rise up they shall be put to shame; But thy servant shall rejoice.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p38"></a><b>29 </b>Clothed shall be my adversaries with disgrace, And they shall be covered as with a garment with their own shame.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p39"></a><b>30 </b>I will praise Jehovah greatly with my mouth; And in the midst of the great I will celebrate him:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xvii-p40"></a><b>31 </b>Because he standeth at the right hand of the poor one, To save from condemnations his soul.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xviii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p2"></a>PSALM 110</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p3"></a>A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Jehovah said to my Lord, “Sit thou at my right hand, “Until I make thy enemies thy footstool.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>The scepter of thy power send shall Jehovah out of Zion: Rule thou in the midst of thy enemies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Thy people <i>shall come</i> with voluntary offerings, On the day <i>of the assembling</i> of thy army, In beauty of holiness: From the womb as from the morning dawn To thee <i>has been</i> the dew of thy youth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Sworn hath Jehovah, and he will not repent: “Thou art a priest for ever “According to the manner of Melchisedek.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>The Lord at thy right hand Hath crushed in the day of his wrath kings.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>He shall judge among the heathen, He shall fill <i>all</i> with ruins; He shall crush the head over a great country.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xviii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Of the torrent in the way he shall drink, Therefore shall he lift up the head.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p2"></a>PSALM 111</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p3"></a>Hallelujah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p4"></a><b>1 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p4.1"></a>א I will celebrate Jehovah with <i>my</i> whole heart, <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p4.2"></a>ב In the congregation of the just, and in the assembly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p5"></a><b>2 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p5.1"></a>ג Great are the works of Jehovah, <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p5.2"></a>ד Sought out of all who have pleasure in them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p6"></a><b>3 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p6.1"></a>ה Beautiful and honorable   				 <a name="fr_379"></a><a href="#fn_379"><font size="1">380</font></a>
  				 <i>is</i> his work; <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p7.1"></a>ו And his righteousness endureth for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p8"></a><b>4 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p8.1"></a>ז He hath made a memorial by his wonderful works: <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p8.2"></a>ח Merciful and compassionate <i>is</i> Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p9"></a><b>5 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p9.1"></a>ט A portion he hath given to those who fear him: <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p9.2"></a>י He will remember for ever his covenant.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p10"></a><b>6 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p10.1"></a>כ The might of his works he hath proclaimed to his people, <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p10.2"></a>ל To give them the heritage of the heathen.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p11"></a><b>7 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p11.1"></a>מ The works of his hands <i>are</i> truth and judgment: <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p11.2"></a>נ True <i>are</i> all his statutes,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p12"></a><b>8 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p12.1"></a>ס And established for ever — <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p12.2"></a>ע Made in truth and rectitude.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p13"></a><b>9 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p13.1"></a>פ Redemption he hath sent to his people; <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p13.2"></a>ץ He hath commanded for ever his covenant: <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p13.3"></a>ק 				Holy and terrible <i>is</i> his name.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p14"></a><b>10 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p14.1"></a>ר The beginning of wisdom is the fear of Jehovah; <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p14.2"></a>ש A good understanding <i>have</i> all those who do them: <a name="xxxv.iv.xix-p14.3"></a>ת His praise endureth for ever.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xx"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p2"></a>PSALM 112</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p3"></a>Hallelujah</p>
