 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p4"></a><b>1 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p4.1"></a>א Blessed is the man who feareth Jehovah; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p4.2"></a>ב In his commandments he will delight greatly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p5"></a><b>2 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p5.1"></a>ג Mighty on the earth shall be his seed: <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p5.2"></a>ד The generation of the upright ones shall be blessed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p6"></a><b>3 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p6.1"></a>ה Wealth and riches <i>shall be</i> in his house; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p6.2"></a>ו And his righteousness endureth for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p7"></a><b>4 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p7.1"></a>ז There ariseth in darkness light to the upright ones: <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p7.2"></a>ח <i>He is</i> merciful and compassionate and righteous.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p8"></a><b>5 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p8.1"></a>ט A good man showeth pity and lendeth; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p8.2"></a>י He manageth his affairs   				 <a name="fr_380"></a><a href="#fn_380"><font size="1">381</font></a>
  				 in uprightness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p10"></a><b>6 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p10.1"></a>כ Truly he shall not for ever be moved; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p10.2"></a>ל In everlasting remembrance shall be the righteous one.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p11"></a><b>7 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p11.1"></a>מ Of evil tidings he shall not be afraid; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p11.2"></a>נ Established is his heart, because he trusteth in Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p12"></a><b>8 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p12.1"></a>ס Sustained <i>is</i> his heart, he shall not be afraid, <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p12.2"></a>ע Until he see <i>his</i> <i>desire</i> upon his adversaries.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p13"></a><b>9 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p13.1"></a>פ He hath dispersed; he hath given to the poor ones; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p13.2"></a>ץ His righteousness continueth for ever; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p13.3"></a>ק His horn shall be exalted with glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p14"></a><b>10 </b><a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p14.1"></a>ר The ungodly one shall see <i>it</i>, and be incensed; <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p14.2"></a>ש With his teeth he shall gnash and waste away: <a name="xxxv.iv.xx-p14.3"></a>ת The desire of the ungodly ones shall perish.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xxi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p2"></a>PSALM 113</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p3"></a>Hallelujah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Praise ye, O ye servants of Jehovah! Praise ye the name of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Let the name of Jehovah be blessed, From henceforth and for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>From the rising of the sun even to his going down, Worthy to be praised <i>is</i> the name of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>High above all nations <i>is</i> Jehovah, Above the heavens is his glory.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Who <i>is</i> like Jehovah our God,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Who hath his dwelling on high,   				 <a name="fr_381"></a><a href="#fn_381"><font size="1">382</font></a>
  				 Who humbleth himself to behold <i>that which</i> is done in heaven and on earth?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p11"></a><b>7 </b>Who raiseth from the dust the needy one; From the dunghill he lifteth up the wretched one;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p12"></a><b>8 </b>To make him sit with princes, With the princes of his people.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxi-p13"></a><b>9 </b>Who causeth the barren woman to dwell with a family, Rejoicing that <i>she is</i> a mother of children. Hallelujah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xxii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p2"></a>PSALM 114</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>When Israel went forth from Egypt, The house of Jacob from a people barbarous;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>[<i>Then</i>] was Judah for his holiness, Israel, his dominions.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>The sea saw, and fled, Jordan was turned backward.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>The mountains leaped as rams, The hills as the lambs of the flock.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>What ailed thee, O sea! that thou fleddest? <i>And thou</i>, O Jordan! <i>that</i> thou wast turned back?</p>  			 
 <p class="BibleVerse39"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p8"></a><b>6 </b>Ye mountains, <i>that</i> ye leaped like rams; Ye hills, as the lambs of the flock?</p>  			 
 <p class="BibleVerse39"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>At the presence of the Lord, tremble, O earth! At the presence of the God of Jacob;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>Who turned the rock into pools of water, The flinty rock into a fountain of waters.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p2"></a>PSALM 115</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Not to us, O Jehovah! not to us, But to thy name give glory, On account of thy mercy, on account of thy truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Why should the heathen say, “Where <i>is</i> now their God?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>But our God <i>is</i> in the heaven: Whatever pleased him he hath done.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>Their idols <i>are</i> silver and gold, The work of the hands of men.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>A mouth have they,   				 <a name="fr_382"></a><a href="#fn_382"><font size="1">383</font></a>
  				 and they do not speak: Eyes have they, and they do not see:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Ears have they, and they do not hear: Noses have they, and they do not smell:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Hands have they, and they do not feel: Feet have they, and they do not walk: They do not speak through their throat.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Like to them shall be those who make them, And every one who trusteth in them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>O Israel! trust thou in Jehovah: Their help and their shield is He:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>O house of Aaron! trust in Jehovah: Their help and their shield is he:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Ye who fear Jehovah! trust in Jehovah: Their help and their shield <i>is</i> He.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>Jehovah hath remembered us; he will bless us; He will bless the house of Israel; He will bless the house of Aaron.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>He will bless those who fear Jehovah, The small together with the great.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>Jehovah will add to you, To you and to your children.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p18"></a><b>15 </b>Blessed are ye of Jehovah, Who made heaven and earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p19"></a><b>16 </b>The heavens, the heavens <i>are</i> Jehovah’s: But the earth he hath given to the sons of men.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p20"></a><b>17 </b>The dead shall not praise <i>thee</i>, O God! Nor any who go down into silence.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p21"></a><b>18 </b>But as for us we will bless God, From this time, and even for evermore. Hallelujah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p2"></a>PSALM 116</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p3"></a><b>1 </b>I have loved, because heard hath Jehovah the voice of my prayer;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Because he hath inclined his ear to me, When in my straits I called upon him.   				 <a name="fr_383"></a><a href="#fn_383"><font size="1">384</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>They encompassed me, the snares of death, And the sorrows of the grave found me: Trouble and grief I found.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>And on the name of Jehovah I will call: “I beseech thee, O Jehovah! deliver my soul.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Merciful <i>is</i> Jehovah and righteous; And our God <i>is</i> compassionate.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Guard doth Jehovah the simple: I was brought low and he saved me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Return, O my soul! to thy rest; For Jehovah hath dealt kindly with thee.   				 <a name="fr_384"></a><a href="#fn_384"><font size="1">385</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Because thou hast rescued my soul from death My eye from tears, My foot from falling.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p13"></a><b>9 </b>I will walk before Jehovah in the land of the living.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p14"></a><b>10 </b>I have believed, for I will speak: “I am afflicted greatly.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p15"></a><b>11 </b>I said in my fear, “Every man is a liar.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p16"></a><b>12 </b>What shall I render to Jehovah? All his benefits <i>are</i> upon me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p17"></a><b>13 </b>The cup of salvation I will take, And upon the name of Jehovah I will call.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p18"></a><b>14 </b>My vows to, Jehovah I will perform Now in the presence of all his people.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p19"></a><b>15 </b>Precious in the eyes of Jehovah is the death of his meek ones.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p20"></a><b>16 </b>Come! O Jehovah! for I, <i>am</i> thy servant; I <i>am</i> thy servant, the son of thy handmaid; Thou hast broken my fetters.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p21"></a><b>17 </b>To thee will I sacrifice the sacrifice of praise, And upon the name of Jehovah will I call.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p22"></a><b>18 </b>My vows to Jehovah will I perform Now in the presence of all his people,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p23"></a><b>19 </b>In the courts of the house of Jehovah In the midst of thee, O Jerusalem! Hallelujah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xxv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxv-p2"></a>PSALM 117</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxv-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Praise ye Jehovah, all ye nations! Celebrate him all ye peoples!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxv-p4"></a><b>2 </b>For great towards us is his mercy, And the truth of Jehovah <i>continueth</i> for ever. Hallelujah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p2"></a>PSALM 118</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Celebrate ye Jehovah! for <i>he is</i> good: For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Let now Israel say: “For   				 <a name="fr_385"></a><a href="#fn_385"><font size="1">386</font></a>
  				 to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Let now the house of Aaron say: “For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Let now those who fear Jehovah say: “For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>In my distress I called upon God; God answered me <i>by setting me</i> at large.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Jehovah <i>is</i> with me: I will not fear what man can do to me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Jehovah <i>is</i> with me among those who help me, And I shall see <i>my desire</i> upon my adversaries.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>It is better to hope in Jehovah Than to place confidence in man:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p12"></a><b>9 </b>It is better to hope in Jehovah Than to place confidence in princes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p13"></a><b>10 </b>All the nations encompassed me: <i>But</i> in the name of Jehovah I will surely cut them off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p14"></a><b>11 </b>They encompassed me, yea they encompassed me, <i>But</i> in the name of Jehovah I will surely cut them off’.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p15"></a><b>12 </b>They encompassed me as bees: They were extinguished as a fire of thorns: In the name of Jehovah I will surely cut them off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p16"></a><b>13 </b>Thou hast thrust and   				 <a name="fr_386"></a><a href="#fn_386"><font size="1">387</font></a>
  				 thrust at me, that I might fall: But Jehovah helped me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p18"></a><b>14 </b>My strength and <i>my</i> song is God, And he hath become to me salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p19"></a><b>15 </b>The voice of exultation and salvation is in the tabernacles of the righteous: The right hand of Jehovah hath done valiantly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p20"></a><b>16 </b>The right hand of Jehovah is exalted, The right hand of Jehovah hath done valiantly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p21"></a><b>17 </b>I shall not die, yea, I shall live, And recount the works of God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p22"></a><b>18 </b>Chastised me sorely hath   				 <a name="fr_387"></a><a href="#fn_387"><font size="1">388</font></a>
  				 God; But he hath not delivered me up unto death.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p24"></a><b>19 </b>Open to me the gates of righteousness; <i>And</i> having entered into them, I will celebrate God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p25"></a><b>20 </b>This is the gate of Jehovah, The just ones shall enter into it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p26"></a><b>21 </b>I will celebrate thee because thou hast heard me, And hast been my salvation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p27"></a><b>22 </b>The stone which the builders rejected Is become the head [<i>stone</i>] of the corner.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p28"></a><b>23 </b>By Jehovah hath this been done: It is marvelous in our eyes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p29"></a><b>24 </b>This <i>is</i> the day which Jehovah hath made; Let us exult and rejoice in it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p30"></a><b>25 </b>I beseech thee, O Jehovah! save me; I beseech thee, I beseech thee, O Jehovah! give prosperity I beseech thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p31"></a><b>26 </b>Blessed is he who cometh in the name of Jehovah: We bless you from the house of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p32"></a><b>27 </b>God <i>is</i> Jehovah, and he hath given light to us: Bind ye the lamb with cords, even to the horns of the altar.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p33"></a><b>28 </b>My God art thou, and I will celebrate thee: My God, I will exalt thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p34"></a><b>29 </b>Celebrate ye Jehovah; for <i>he</i> <i>is</i> good: For to everlasting <i>is</i> his mercy.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v"></a>  		  
 <p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v-p1"></a>PSALMS 119—150</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.i"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p2"></a>PSALM 119</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p3"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p3.1"></a>א [<b>Aleph</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p4"></a><b>1 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p4.1"></a>א Blessed <i>are</i> those who are upright in <i>their</i> way, Walking in the law of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p5"></a><b>2 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p5.1"></a>א Blessed <i>are</i> those who keep his testimonies, <i>Who</i> with <i>their</i> whole heart seek him.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p6"></a><b>3 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p6.1"></a>א, Surely they do not work iniquity, <i>Who</i> in his ways do walk.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p7"></a><b>4 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p7.1"></a>א Thou hast commanded That thy statutes be kept carefully.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p8"></a><b>5 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p8.1"></a>א O that my ways may be directed To the keeping of thy statutes!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p9"></a><b>6 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p9.1"></a>א Then shall I not be ashamed, When I shall have been attentive to all thy commandments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p10"></a><b>7 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p10.1"></a>א I will celebrate thee with uprightness of heart, When I shall have learned the judgments of thy righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p11"></a><b>8 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p11.1"></a>א, Thy statutes I will keep: Do not thou forsake me very far.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p12"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p12.1"></a>ב [<b>Beth</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p13"></a><b>9 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p13.1"></a>ב By what [<i>means</i>] shall a young man cleanse his way? By taking heed according to thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p14"></a><b>10 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p14.1"></a>ב With my whole heart have I sought thee; Let me not go astray from thy commandments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p15"></a><b>11 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p15.1"></a>ב In my heart I have hidden thy word, That I might not sin against thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p16"></a><b>12 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p16.1"></a>ב Blessed <i>art</i> thou, O Jehovah! Teach me thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p17"></a><b>13 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p17.1"></a>ב With my lips have I declared All the judgments of thy mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p18"></a><b>14 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p18.1"></a>ב In the way of thy testimonies I have taken delight, As much as in all riches.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p19"></a><b>15 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p19.1"></a>ב Upon thy statutes will I meditate, And I will consider thy paths.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p20"></a><b>16 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p20.1"></a>ב In thy commandments will I delight myself; I will not forget thy words.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p21"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p21.1"></a>ג [<b>Gimel</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p22"></a><b>17 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p22.1"></a>ג Do good to thy servant, And I shall live and keep thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p23"></a><b>18 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p23.1"></a>ג Open mine eyes, And I shall behold the wonders of thy law.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p24"></a><b>19 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p24.1"></a>ג I am a stranger on the earth: Hide not from me thy commandments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p25"></a><b>20 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p25.1"></a>ג Broken is my soul with the desire <i>it hath </i>To thy judgments at all times.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p26"></a><b>21 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p26.1"></a>ג Thou hast destroyed the proud ones; Cursed are those who decline from thy commandments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p27"></a><b>22 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p27.1"></a>ג Remove from me reproach and contempt; For thy testimonies I have kept.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p28"></a><b>23 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p28.1"></a>ג Princes also have sat, against me they have spoken: Thy servant meditated upon thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p29"></a><b>24 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p29.1"></a>ג Also thy testimonies <i>are</i> my delights, The men of my counsel.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p30"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p30.1"></a>ד [<b>Daleth</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p31"></a><b>25 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p31.1"></a>ד Cleave to the dust doth my soul: Quicken me according to thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p32"></a><b>26 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p32.1"></a>ד I have declared my ways, and thou hast answered me: Teach me thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p33"></a><b>27 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p33.1"></a>ד The way of thy commandments make me to understand, And I will meditate upon thy wonders.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p34"></a><b>28 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p34.1"></a>ד Drop away doth my soul for grief: Raise me up according to thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p35"></a><b>29 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p35.1"></a>ד The way of falsehood remove from me, And thy law grant me graciously.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p36"></a><b>30 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p36.1"></a>ד The way of truth I have chosen; Thy judgments I have set before me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p37"></a><b>31 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p37.1"></a>ד I have cleaved to thy testimonies, O Jehovah Let me not be put to shame.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p38"></a><b>32 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p38.1"></a>ד The way of thy statutes I will run, When thou shalt have enlarged my heart.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p39"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p39.1"></a>ה [<b>He</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p40"></a><b>33 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p40.1"></a>ה Teach me, O Jehovah! the way of thy statutes, And I will keep it unto the end.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p41"></a><b>34 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p41.1"></a>ה Make me to understand, and I will observe thy law, And keep it with my whole heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p42"></a><b>35 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p42.1"></a>ה Direct me in the way of thy statutes; For in it is my delight.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p43"></a><b>36 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p43.1"></a>ה Incline my heart to thy testimonies, And not to covetousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p44"></a><b>37 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p44.1"></a>ה Turn away my eyes from seeing vanity; In thy way quicken me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p45"></a><b>38 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p45.1"></a>ה Confirm to thy servant thy word, Who to thy fear <i>is devoted</i></p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p46"></a><b>39 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p46.1"></a>ה Remove my reproach which I have dreaded, For thy judgments are good.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p47"></a><b>40 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p47.1"></a>ה Behold! I have longed after thy commandments: In thy righteousness quicken me.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p48"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p48.1"></a>ו [<b>Vau</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p49"></a><b>41 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p49.1"></a>ו And let come to me thy mercies, O Jehovah! Thy salvation according to thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p50"></a><b>42 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p50.1"></a>ו And I will answer a word to him who reproacheth me; For I have trusted in thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p51"></a><b>43 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p51.1"></a>ו And take not from my mouth the word of truth utterly: Because for thy judgments I wait.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p52"></a><b>44 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p52.1"></a>ו And I will keep thy law continually, For ever and ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p53"></a><b>45 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p53.1"></a>ו And I will walk at large; For thy statutes I have sought.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p54"></a><b>46 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p54.1"></a>ו And I will speak of thy testimonies before kings, And will not be ashamed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p55"></a><b>47 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p55.1"></a>ו And I will delight myself in thy commandments Which I have loved.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p56"></a><b>48 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p56.1"></a>ו And I will lift up my hands to thy commandments Which I have loved; And I will meditate upon thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p57"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p57.1"></a>ז [<b>Zain</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p58"></a><b>49 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p58.1"></a>ז Remember thy word to thy servant, Upon which thou hast caused me to hope.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p59"></a><b>50 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p59.1"></a>ז This is my consolation in my affliction; For thy word revives me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p60"></a><b>51 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p60.1"></a>ז The proud ones have derided me exceedingly: From thy law I have not declined.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p61"></a><b>52 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p61.1"></a>ז I remembered thy judgments of old, O Jehovah! And comforted myself.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p62"></a><b>53 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p62.1"></a>ז Terror hath seized upon me, Because of the ungodly who forsake thy law.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p63"></a><b>54 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p63.1"></a>ז Thy statutes have been songs to me In the house of my pilgrimage.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p64"></a><b>55 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p64.1"></a>ז I remembered in the night thy name, O Jehovah! And I will keep thy law.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p65"></a><b>56 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p65.1"></a>ז This is done to me, Because thy statutes I have observed.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p66"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p66.1"></a>ח [<b>Cheth</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p67"></a><b>57 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p67.1"></a>ח <i>Thou art</i> my portion, O Jehovah! I have said that I will keep thy words.   				 <a name="fr_388"></a><a href="#fn_388"><font size="1">389</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p69"></a><b>58 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p69.1"></a>ח I have sought thy face with my whole heart; Have mercy upon me according to thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p70"></a><b>59 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p70.1"></a>ח I thought upon my ways, And turned my feet to thy testimonies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p71"></a><b>60 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p71.1"></a>ח I made haste and delayed not To keep thy commandments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p72"></a><b>61 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p72.1"></a>ח The cords of the ungodly have caught hold of me; Thy law I have not forgotten.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p73"></a><b>62 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p73.1"></a>ח At midnight I will rise to praise thee, Because of the judgments of thy righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p74"></a><b>63 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p74.1"></a>ח A companion am I to all who fear thee, And who keep thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p75"></a><b>64 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p75.1"></a>ח Of thy mercy, O Jehovah! the earth is full: Thy statutes teach thou me.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p76"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p76.1"></a>ת [<b>Teth</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p77"></a><b>65 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p77.1"></a>ת Kindly hast thou dealt with thy servant, O Jehovah! According to thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p78"></a><b>66 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p78.1"></a>ת Goodness of taste and knowledge teach me; For thy commandments I have believed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p79"></a><b>67 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p79.1"></a>ת Before I was brought low I went astray; But now thy word I keep.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p80"></a><b>68 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p80.1"></a>ת Good <i>art</i> thou, and beneficent: Teach me thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p81"></a><b>69 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p81.1"></a>ת Weaved a lie   				 <a name="fr_389"></a><a href="#fn_389"><font size="1">390</font></a>
  				 against me have the proud ones; <i>But as for me</i> I with my whole heart will keep statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p83"></a><b>70 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p83.1"></a>ת Fat as grease is their heart; <i>But as for me</i> I in thy law do delight.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p84"></a><b>71 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p84.1"></a>ת <i>It hath been</i> good for me that I have been afflicted, That I might learn thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p85"></a><b>72 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p85.1"></a>ת Better to me is the law of thy mouth Than thousands of gold and silver.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p86"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p86.1"></a>י [<b>Yod</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p87"></a><b>73 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p87.1"></a>י Thy hands have made and formed me; Make me to understand, and I shall learn thy commandments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p88"></a><b>74 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p88.1"></a>י Those who fear thee shall see me and rejoice; Because for thy word I have waited.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p89"></a><b>75 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p89.1"></a>י I have known, O Jehovah! that righteousness are thy judgments; And in truth thou hast humbled me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p90"></a><b>76 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p90.1"></a>י To thy word to thy servant.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p91"></a><b>77 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p91.1"></a>י Let come to me thy compassions, and I shall live; For thy law is my delight.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p92"></a><b>78 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p92.1"></a>י Ashamed let be the proud, for they have falsely wronged me: As for me I will meditate upon thy precepts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p93"></a><b>79 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p93.1"></a>י Let those turn unto me who fear thee, And have known thy testimonies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p94"></a><b>80 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p94.1"></a>י Let my heart be sound in thy statutes, That I may not be put to shame.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p95"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p95.1"></a>כ [<b>Caph</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p96"></a><b>81 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p96.1"></a>כ Fainted for thy salvation hath my soul: For thy word I wait.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p97"></a><b>82 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p97.1"></a>כ Failed have my eyes [<i>in looking</i>] for thy word, While I say, “When wilt thou comfort me?”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p98"></a><b>83 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p98.1"></a>כ For I have been as a bottle in the smoke; <i>And yet</i> thy statutes I have not forgotten.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p99"></a><b>84 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p99.1"></a>כ How many are the days of thy servant? When wilt thou execute judgment on my persecutors?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p100"></a><b>85 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p100.1"></a>כ The proud have digged pits for me, Which is not according to thy law.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p101"></a><b>86 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p101.1"></a>כ All thy commandments are truth: Deceitfully do they persecute me; <i>therefore</i> help thou me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p102"></a><b>87 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p102.1"></a>כ Almost have they consumed me upon the earth; Yet I have not forsaken thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p103"></a><b>88 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p103.1"></a>כ According to thy goodness quicken me; And I will keep the testimony of thy mouth.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p104"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p104.1"></a>ל [<b>Lamed</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p105"></a><b>89 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p105.1"></a>ל For ever, O Jehovah! Thy word endureth in the heavens.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p106"></a><b>90 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p106.1"></a>ל From generation to generation <i>is</i> thy truth: Thou hast established the earth, and it abideth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p107"></a><b>91 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p107.1"></a>ל By thy judgments they continue to this day; For all are thy servants.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p108"></a><b>92 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p108.1"></a>ל Unless thy law <i>had been</i> my delight, Then should I have perished in my affliction.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p109"></a><b>93 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p109.1"></a>ל Never will I forget thy statutes, For in them thou hast quickened me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p110"></a><b>94 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p110.1"></a>ל Thine I am; O save me! For thy statutes I have sought.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p111"></a><b>95 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p111.1"></a>ל For me wait do the ungodly to destroy me: <i>But</i> I consider thy testimonies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p112"></a><b>96 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p112.1"></a>ל In all perfection I have seen an end: Broad is thy commandment exceedingly.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p113"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p113.1"></a>מ [<b>Mem</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p114"></a><b>97 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p114.1"></a>מ O how have I loved thy law! All the day it is my meditation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p115"></a><b>98 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p115.1"></a>מ Than my adversaries thou hast made me wiser by thy commandments; Because for ever they are with me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p116"></a><b>99 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p116.1"></a>מ Than all my teachers thou hast made me wiser; Because thy testimonies are my meditation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p117"></a><b>100 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p117.1"></a>מ Than the aged I have more understanding; Because thy statutes I have observed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p118"></a><b>101 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p118.1"></a>מ From every evil path I have restrained my feet, That I may keep thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p119"></a><b>102 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p119.1"></a>מ From thy judgments I have not declined; For thou thyself hast taught me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p120"></a><b>103 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p120.1"></a>מ How sweet to my palate have been thy words! More [<i>sweet</i>] than honey to my mouth!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p121"></a><b>104 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p121.1"></a>מ By thy statutes I have gotten understanding; Therefore I have hated every path of falsehood.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p122"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p122.1"></a>נ [<b>Nun</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p123"></a><b>105 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p123.1"></a>נ A lamp to my feet is thy word, And a light to my path.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p124"></a><b>106 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p124.1"></a>נ I have sworn and will make sure, To observe the judgments of thy righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p125"></a><b>107 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p125.1"></a>נ I am afflicted exceedingly, O Jehovah! Quicken me according to thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p126"></a><b>108 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p126.1"></a>נ I Let the freewill <i>offerings</i> of my mouth, I pray thee, be pleasing to thee, O Jehovah! And thy judgments teach me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p127"></a><b>109 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p127.1"></a>נ My soul <i>is</i> in my hand continually; And thy law I have not forgotten.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p128"></a><b>110 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p128.1"></a>נ Laid have the ungodly a snare for me: Yet from thy statutes I have not erred.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p129"></a><b>111 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p129.1"></a>נ I have as [<i>my</i>] inheritance thy testimonies for ever; For the joy of my heart are they.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p130"></a><b>112 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p130.1"></a>נ I have inclined my heart to perform thy statutes For ever, and even to the end.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p131"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p131.1"></a>ס [<b>Samech</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p132"></a><b>113 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p132.1"></a>ס <i>Crooked</i> thoughts I have hated; But thy law I have loved.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p133"></a><b>114 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p133.1"></a>ס My hiding-place and my shield art thou: In thy word I have trusted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p134"></a><b>115 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p134.1"></a>ס Depart from me, ye wicked men! And I will keep the commandments of my God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p135"></a><b>116 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p135.1"></a>ס Sustain me by thy word, and I shall live: And make me not ashamed of my expectation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p136"></a><b>117 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p136.1"></a>ס Establish me, and I shall be safe, And I will consider thy statutes continually.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p137"></a><b>118 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p137.1"></a>ס Thou hast trodden down all who go astray from thy statutes; For falsehood is their deceit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p138"></a><b>119 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p138.1"></a>ס <i>As</i> dross thou hast made to cease all the ungodly of the earth; Therefore I have loved thy testimonies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p139"></a><b>120 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p139.1"></a>ס Tremble   				 <a name="fr_390"></a><a href="#fn_390"><font size="1">391</font></a>
  				 for fear of thee did my flesh, And of thy judgments I was afraid.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p141"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p141.1"></a>ע [<b>Ain</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p142"></a><b>121 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p142.1"></a>ע I have done judgment and righteousness: Give me not up to my oppressors.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p143"></a><b>122 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p143.1"></a>ע Become surety for thy servant for good, That the proud may not oppress me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p144"></a><b>123 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p144.1"></a>ע My eyes have failed for thy salvation, And for the word of thy righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p145"></a><b>124 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p145.1"></a>ע Deal with thy servant according to thy goodness, And thy statutes teach thou me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p146"></a><b>125 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p146.1"></a>ע Thy servant am I, give me understanding, That I may learn thy testimonies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p147"></a><b>126 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p147.1"></a>ע <i>It is</i> time [<i>for thee</i>] to work, O Jehovah! <i>For they</i> have destroyed thy law.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p148"></a><b>127 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p148.1"></a>ע Therefore I have loved thy statutes Mere than gold and fine gold.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p149"></a><b>128 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p149.1"></a>ע Therefore all <i>thy</i> commandments I have esteemed <i>to be</i> altogether right: Every way of falsehood I have hated:</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p150"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p150.1"></a>פ [<b>Phe</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p151"></a><b>129 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p151.1"></a>פ Marvelous things <i>are</i> thy testimonies; Therefore observed them hath my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p152"></a><b>130 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p152.1"></a>פ The entrance of thy words is light, Giving understanding to the little ones.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p153"></a><b>131 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p153.1"></a>פ My mouth I opened and panted, Because thy commandments I loved.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p154"></a><b>132 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p154.1"></a>פ Look upon me and have pity upon me, According to <i>thy</i> judgment towards those who love thy name.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p155"></a><b>133 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p155.1"></a>פ My steps direct thou according to thy word, And let not any iniquity have dominion in me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p156"></a><b>134 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p156.1"></a>פ Redeem me from the oppression of men, And I will keep thy precepts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p157"></a><b>135 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p157.1"></a>פ Thy face cause thou to shine upon thy servant, And teach me thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p158"></a><b>136 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p158.1"></a>פ Rivers of waters run from my eyes, Because they have not kept thy law.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p159"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p159.1"></a>ץ [<b>Tsadde</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p160"></a><b>137 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p160.1"></a>ץ Righteous art thou, O Jehovah! And right <i>are</i> thy judgments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p161"></a><b>138 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p161.1"></a>ץ Thou hast commanded righteousness <i>in</i> thy testimonies, And truth exceedingly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p162"></a><b>139 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p162.1"></a>ץ Consumed me hath my zeal, Because forgotten thy words have my adversaries.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p163"></a><b>140 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p163.1"></a>ץ Refined <i>is</i> thy word exceedingly: And thy servant hath loved it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p164"></a><b>141 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p164.1"></a>ץ Small <i>am</i> I, and despised; [<i>Yet</i>] thy precepts I have not forgotten.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p165"></a><b>142 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p165.1"></a>ץ Thy righteousness <i>is</i> righteousness for ever, And thy law is truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p166"></a><b>143 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p166.1"></a>ץ Trouble and anguish have come upon me; <i>But</i> thy commandments <i>have been</i> my delights.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p167"></a><b>144 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p167.1"></a>ץ The righteousness of thy testimonies <i>endureth</i> for ever; Make me to understand, and I shall live.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p168"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p168.1"></a>ק [<b>Koph</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p169"></a><b>145 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p169.1"></a>ק I have cried with my whole heart; Answer me, O Jehovah! <i>And</i> thy statutes I will keep.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p170"></a><b>146 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p170.1"></a>ק I have called upon thee, save me, And I will keep thy testimonies.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p171"></a><b>147 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p171.1"></a>ק I have prevented the dawn of the morning,   				 <a name="fr_391"></a><a href="#fn_391"><font size="1">392</font></a>
  				 and have cried: To thy word I have looked up.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p173"></a><b>148 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p173.1"></a>ק Prevented have my eyes the watches <i>of the night</i>, To meditate upon thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p174"></a><b>149 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p174.1"></a>ק My voice hear thou, according to thy mercy, O Jehovah According to thy judgment quicken me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p175"></a><b>150 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p175.1"></a>ק Drawn near have the pursuers of malice; From thy law they have departed.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p176"></a><b>151 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p176.1"></a>ק Near art thou, O Jehovah! And all thy commandments <i>are</i> truth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p177"></a><b>152 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p177.1"></a>ק From the beginning I have known from thy testimonies, That for ever thou hast founded them.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p178"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p178.1"></a>ר [<b>Resh</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p179"></a><b>153 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p179.1"></a>ר Behold my affliction, and rescue me; For thy law I have not forgotten.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p180"></a><b>154 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p180.1"></a>ר Debate my cause, and redeem me; According to thy word quicken me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p181"></a><b>155 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p181.1"></a>ר Far from the ungodly is safety; Because thy statutes they have not sought.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p182"></a><b>156 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p182.1"></a>ר Thy compassions <i>are</i> great, O Jehovah! According to thy judgments quicken me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p183"></a><b>157 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p183.1"></a>ר Many <i>are</i> my persecutors and my oppressors: From thy testimonies I have not declined.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p184"></a><b>158 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p184.1"></a>ר I saw the perfidious, and chid them; Because thy word they have not kept.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p185"></a><b>159 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p185.1"></a>ר Behold how thy commandments I have loved: According to thy clemency quicken me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p186"></a><b>160 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p186.1"></a>ר The beginning of thy word <i>is</i> truth; And to everlasting <i>is</i> all the judgment of thy righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p187"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p187.1"></a>ש [<b>Shin</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p188"></a><b>161 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p188.1"></a>ש Princes have persecuted me without a cause Yet at thy word afraid hath been my heart.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p189"></a><b>162 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p189.1"></a>ש Joyful am I over thy word, As he who hath found much spoil.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p190"></a><b>163 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p190.1"></a>ש Deceit I <i>have</i> hated and abhorred; Thy law I <i>have</i> loved.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p191"></a><b>164 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p191.1"></a>ש Seven times a day have I praised thee, Because of the judgments of thy righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p192"></a><b>165 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p192.1"></a>ש Much peace have those who love thy law, And they have no stumbling-block.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p193"></a><b>166 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p193.1"></a>ש I have waited for thy salvation, O Jehovah! And thy commandments I have done.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p194"></a><b>167 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p194.1"></a>ש Kept hath my soul thy testimonies, And I have loved them exceedingly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p195"></a><b>168 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p195.1"></a>ש I have kept thy commandments and thy testimonies; For all my ways <i>are</i> before thee.</p>  			 
 <p class="Center"><a name="xxxv.v.i-p196"></a><a name="xxxv.v.i-p196.1"></a>ת [<b>Thau</b>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p197"></a><b>169 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p197.1"></a>ת Come let my cry into thy presence, O Jehovah! According to thy word give me understanding.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p198"></a><b>170 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p198.1"></a>ת Come let my prayer into thy presence: According to thy word deliver me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p199"></a><b>171 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p199.1"></a>ת Speak shall my lips praise, When thou shalt have taught me thy statutes.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p200"></a><b>172 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p200.1"></a>ת Speak shall my tongue of thy word; For all thy precepts are righteousness.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p201"></a><b>173 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p201.1"></a>ת Let thy hand be to succor me; For thy commandments I have chosen.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p202"></a><b>174 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p202.1"></a>ת I have longed for thy salvation, O Jehovah! And thy law <i>hath been</i> my delights.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p203"></a><b>175 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p203.1"></a>ת Live let my soul, and let it praise thee; And let thy judgments succor me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.i-p204"></a><b>176 </b><a name="xxxv.v.i-p204.1"></a>ת I have wandered like a lost sheep; Seek thy servant, for thy statutes I have not forgotten.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.ii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p2"></a>PSALM 120</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>To Jehovah in my distress I cried, And he answered me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>O Jehovah! deliver my soul from the lip of falsehood, From the tongue of deceit.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>What give thee, and what avail thee Shall the tongue of deceit?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>The arrows of a strong <i>man</i> sharpened, With coals of junipers.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Alas for me! that I have been a sojourner in Meseeh, <i>And</i> have dwelt among the tents of Kedar.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Long dwelt hath my soul with him who hateth peace.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>I [<i>am for</i>] peace; But when I speak, they [<i>are</i>] for war.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.iii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p2"></a>PSALM 121</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I will lift up my eyes to the mountains, Whence come shall my help.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>My help <i>cometh</i> from Jehovah, Who made heaven and earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>He will not suffer thy foot to stumble; Slumber not shall thy guardian.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Behold! slumber not nor sleep Shall the guardian of Israel.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Jehovah <i>is</i> thy guardian; Jehovah <i>is</i> <i>thy</i> defense on thy right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>By day the sun shall not smite thee, Nor the moon by night.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Jehovah shall keep thee from all evil; He shall keep thy soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Jehovah shall keep thy going out and thy coming in, From this time, and for ever.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.iv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p2"></a>PSALM 122</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I was glad when they said to me, “Into the house of Jehovah we will go.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>“Our feet shall be standing in thy gates, O Jerusalem!”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Jerusalem built as a city, compact in itself together.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Thither ascended the tribes, the tribes of God, For a testimony to Israel, To celebrate the name of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>For there have sat   				 <a name="fr_392"></a><a href="#fn_392"><font size="1">393</font></a>
  				 thrones for judgment, The thrones of the house of David.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p10"></a><b>6 </b>Pray ye for the peace of Jerusalem: Prosper may those who love thee!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p11"></a><b>7 </b>Peace be within thy bulwark! Prosperity within thy towers!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p12"></a><b>8 </b>For the sake of my brethren and my neighbors, I will say now, “Peace [<i>be</i>] within thee!“</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.iv-p13"></a><b>9 </b>For the sake of the house of Jehovah our God, I will seek good for thee.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.v"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.v-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.v-p2"></a>PSALM 123</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.v-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.v-p4"></a><b>1 </b>To thee will I lift up mine eyes, [<i>O thou</i>] who dwellest in the heavens!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.v-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Behold! as the eyes of servants look to the hand of their masters; As the eyes of a handmaid <i>look</i> to the hand of her mistress, So our eyes [<i>look</i>] to Jehovah our God, Until he have mercy upon us.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.v-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Have mercy upon us, O Jehovah! have mercy upon us; For we are exceedingly filled with reproach.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.v-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Exceedingly filled in itself is our soul With the mockery of the rich, With the contempt of the proud.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.vi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p2"></a>PSALM 124</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees. Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>“But for Jehovah who was on our side” — Say now may Israel:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>“But for Jehovah who was on our side, “When men rose up against us;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>“Then alive had they swallowed us up, “When kindled was their wrath against us;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>“Then the waters had overwhelmed us, “The torrent had gone over our soul:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>“Then had gone over our soul the proud waters.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Blessed <i>be</i> Jehovah, Who gave us not for a prey to their teeth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Our soul as a bird, hath been rescued   				 <a name="fr_393"></a><a href="#fn_393"><font size="1">394</font></a>
  				 from the snare of the fowlers; The snare hath been broken, and we have been delivered.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vi-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Our help <i>is</i> in the name of Jehovah, Who made heaven and earth.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.vii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p2"></a>PSALM 125</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>They who confide in Jehovah <i>are as</i> mount Zion, <i>Which</i> shall not be removed, <i>but</i> shall abide for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>As the mountains <i>are</i> about Jerusalem, So Jehovah <i>is</i> round about his people, From henceforth, and for ever.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>For rest not shall the scepter of the ungodly ones upon the lot of the just, Lest the just ones should put forth to iniquity their hands.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Do good, O Jehovah! to the good, And to <i>those who</i> are upright in their hearts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.vii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>But those who turn aside into their crooked paths, Jehovah shall make them walk with the workers of iniquity: <i>But there shall be</i> peace upon Israel.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.viii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p2"></a>PSALM 126</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>When bring back did Jehovah the captivity of Zion, We were like those that dream.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Now filled with laughter <i>shall</i> be our mouth, And our tongue with exultation: Now shall they say among the heathen, “Great things Jehovah hath done for them.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Great things Jehovah hath done for us, <i>Whereof</i> we have been made glad.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Bring back, O Jehovah! our captivity, As rivers in the South.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>They who sow in tears In exultation shall reap.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.viii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Going forth, he shall go and weep, Carrying the price of the seed: Returning he shall return with exultation, Bearing his sheaves.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.ix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p2"></a>PSALM 127</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees. Of Solomon</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Except Jehovah build the house, In vain they labor that build it; Except Jehovah keep the city, In vain watcheth the watchman.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Vain <i>is it</i> for you early to hasten to rise, To go late to rest, To eat the bread of sorrows: <i>For</i> thus will he give to his beloved one sleep.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Lo! the heritage of Jehovah are children: The reward <i>which he bestows</i> is the fruit of the womb.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p7"></a><b>4 </b>As arrows in the hand of a strong man, So <i>are</i> the sons of youth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.ix-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Blessed is the man who shall have filled his quiver with them; <i>For</i> they shall not be ashamed when they speak with their enemies in the gate.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.x"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.x-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.x-p2"></a>PSALM 128</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.x-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.x-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Blessed <i>is</i> the man who feareth Jehovah, Who walketh in his ways.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.x-p5"></a><b>2 </b>The labor of thy hands when thou shalt eat thou shalt be blessed, And it <i>shall be</i> well with thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.x-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Thy wife <i>shall be</i> as a vine fruitful on the sides of thy house: Thy children as plants of olives around thy table.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.x-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Lo! surely, thus blessed shall be the man who feareth Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.x-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Bless thee shall Jehovah from Zion; And thou shalt see the good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.x-p9"></a><b>6 </b>And thou shalt see thy children’s children, <i>And</i> peace upon Israel.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p2"></a>PSALM 129</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>“Often have they afflicted me from my youths” Say now let Israel:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>“Often have they afflicted me from my youth; “Yet they have not prevailed against me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>“Upon my back ploughed have the ploughers; “They have made long their furrows.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>“Jehovah, who is righteous, hath cut asunder the cords of the wicked.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Confounded and turned backward shall be all who hate Zion.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>They shall be as the grass of the housetops, Which before it cometh forth is withered:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>With which the mower hath not filled his hand, Nor his bosom he who gathereth handfuls.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Nor have they said who pass by, “The blessing of Jehovah <i>be</i> upon you, “We bless you in the name of Jehovah.”</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p2"></a>PSALM 130</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Out of the depths have I cried to thee, O Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>O Lord! hear my voice; Let thy ears be attentive to the voice of my prayers.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>If iniquities thou shouldest mark, O God! O Lord! who shall stand?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For with thee is forgiveness that thou mayest be feared.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>I have waited for Jehovah, waited hath my soul; And in his word have I hoped.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>My soul [<i>hath waited</i>] for the Lord Before the watchers of the morning, the watchers of the morning.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>But   				 <a name="fr_394"></a><a href="#fn_394"><font size="1">395</font></a>
  				 hope let Israel in Jehovah; For with Jehovah <i>there is</i> mercy, And with him there is plenteous redemption.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xii-p12"></a><b>8 </b>And he shall redeem Israel from all his iniquities.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xiii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xiii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xiii-p2"></a>PSALM 131</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xiii-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees. Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! my heart hath not been elated, Nor lifted up have been my eyes, Nor have I exercised myself in great matters, Or in things hidden from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>If I have not framed [<i>or set</i>] and quieted my soul, Like one that is weaned from his mother, —   				 <a name="fr_395"></a><a href="#fn_395"><font size="1">396</font></a>
  				 Like a child that is weaned is my soul upon me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiii-p7"></a><b>3 </b>Hope shall Israel in Jehovah From henceforth, and for ever.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xiv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p2"></a>PSALM 132</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Remember, O Jehovah! David With all his affliction:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Who sware to Jehovah, [<i>Who</i>] vowed to the Mighty One of Jacob:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p6"></a><b>3 </b>“If I shall enter into the tabernacle of my house, “If I shall go up upon the covering of my bed,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p7"></a><b>4 </b>“If I give sleep to my eyes, “To my eyelids slumber,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p8"></a><b>5 </b>“Until I find a place for Jehovah, “Habitations for the mighty God of Jacob,” —   				 <a name="fr_396"></a><a href="#fn_396"><font size="1">397</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p10"></a><b>6 </b>Lo! we heard of it at Ephratha; We found it in the fields of the wood.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p11"></a><b>7 </b>We will enter into his habitations, We will worship at his footstool.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p12"></a><b>8 </b>Arise, O Jehovah! into thy rest, Thou and the ark of thy strength.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p13"></a><b>9 </b>Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness, And let thy meek ones exult.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p14"></a><b>10 </b>For the sake of David thy servant Turn not away the face of thy Christ.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p15"></a><b>11 </b>Sworn hath Jehovah to David in truth, Nor will he turn from it: “Of the fruit of thy belly will I set upon thy throne.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p16"></a><b>12 </b>“If thy children shall keep my covenant, “And my testimonies, which I will teach them; “Also their children for ever shall sit upon thy throne.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p17"></a><b>13 </b>For chosen hath Jehovah Zion; He hath desired her for a habitation to himself.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p18"></a><b>14 </b>“This is my rest for ever; “Here will I dwell, because I have loved her.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p19"></a><b>15 </b>“Her provision blessing I will bless;” Her poor I will satisfy with bread.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p20"></a><b>16 </b>“And her priests I will clothe with salvation; “And her merciful ones with exultation shall exult.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p21"></a><b>17 </b>“There will I make to bud the horn of David: “I have prepared a lamp for my Christ.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xiv-p22"></a><b>18 </b>“His enemies will I clothe with shame, “And upon him flourish shall his crown.”</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xv"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xv-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xv-p2"></a>PSALM 133</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xv-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees. Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xv-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Behold! how good, and how becoming, That brethren should even dwell together!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xv-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Like the precious oil upon the head, Which descendeth   				 <a name="fr_397"></a><a href="#fn_397"><font size="1">398</font></a>
  				 upon the beard, the beard of Aaron, Which descendeth upon the skirt of his garments.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xv-p7"></a><b>3 </b>Like the dew of Hermon, Which descendeth upon the mountains of Zion: For there commanded hath Jehovah the blessing, Life for evermore.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xvi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xvi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xvi-p2"></a>PSALM 134</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xvi-p3"></a>A Song of Degrees</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Behold! bless ye Jehovah, All ye servants of Jehovah! Who stand in the house of Jehovah nightly.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Lift up your hands to the sanctuary, And bless ye Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>May Jehovah bless thee out of Zion, [<i>Even he</i>] who hath made heaven and earth.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xvii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p2"></a>PSALM 135</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p3"></a>Hallelujah</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Praise ye the name of Jehovah; Praise [<i>it</i>] O ye servants of Jehovah!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Who stand in the house of Jehovah, [<i>And ye who stand</i>] in the courts of the house of our God.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p6"></a><b>3 </b>Praise God; for good <i>is</i> Jehovah: Sing to his name; for it is pleasant:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For God hath chosen Jacob to himself, Israel for his own possession.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p8"></a><b>5 </b>For I know that great is Jehovah, And <i>that</i> our God is above all gods.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p9"></a><b>6 </b>All things which Jehovah pleaseth, lie doeth in the heavens and on the earth, In the sea and in all the deeps.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Causing the clouds to ascend from the end of the earth: The lightnings for the rain he maketh, Bringing forth the wind out of his secret places.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p11"></a><b>8 </b>He smote the first born of Egypt, From man even unto beast.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p12"></a><b>9 </b>He sent signs and wonders in the midst of thee, O Egypt! On Pharaoh and on all his servants.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p13"></a><b>10 </b>He smote great nations, And slew mighty kings.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p14"></a><b>11 </b>Sihon, king of the Amorites, And Og the king of Basham, And all the kingdoms of Canaan.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p15"></a><b>12 </b>And gave their land for an heritage, An heritage to Israel, his people.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p16"></a><b>13 </b>O Jehovah! thy name <i>is</i> for ever; O Jehovah! thy memorial <i>is</i> from generation to generation.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p17"></a><b>14 </b>For judge will Jehovah his people, And concerning his servants he will repent himself.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p18"></a><b>15 </b>The images of the nations <i>are</i> silver and gold, The work of the hands of man.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p19"></a><b>16 </b>A mouth have they, and they will not speak;   				 <a name="fr_398"></a><a href="#fn_398"><font size="1">399</font></a>
  				 Eyes have they, and they will not see.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p21"></a><b>17 </b>Ears have they, and they will not hear: Also, there is no breath in their mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p22"></a><b>18 </b>Like unto them are those who make them, <i>And</i> every one who trusteth in them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p23"></a><b>19 </b>O house of Israel! bless ye Jehovah; O house of Aaron! bless ye Jehovah;</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p24"></a><b>20 </b>O house of Levi! bless ye Jehovah; O ye who fear Jehovah! bless ye Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xvii-p25"></a><b>21 </b>Blessed <i>be</i> Jehovah out of Zion, Who dwelleth at Jerusalem. Hallelujah.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xviii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p2"></a>PSALM 136</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p3"></a><b>1 </b>Praise Jehovah, for <i>he is</i> good, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Praise the God of gods, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Praise the Lord of lords, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p6"></a><b>4 </b>Who hath done wonders great alone, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p7"></a><b>5 </b>Who hath made the heavens in wisdom, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p8"></a><b>6 </b>Who hath stretched out the earth above the waters, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p9"></a><b>7 </b>Who hath made the great lights, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p10"></a><b>8 </b>The sun for rule by day, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p11"></a><b>9 </b>The moon and stars for rule by night, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p12"></a><b>10 </b>Who smote the Egyptians in their first born, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p13"></a><b>11 </b>And brought out Israel from the midst of them, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p14"></a><b>12 </b>With a hand of strength and an arm stretched out, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p15"></a><b>13 </b>Who divided the Red Sea into divisions, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p16"></a><b>14 </b>And made Israel to pass through the midst of it, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p17"></a><b>15 </b>And cast Pharaoh and his host headlong into the Red Sea, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p18"></a><b>16 </b>And led his people through the wilderness, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p19"></a><b>17 </b>Who smote great kings, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p20"></a><b>18 </b>And slew renowned kings, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p21"></a><b>19 </b>Sihon, king of the Arnorites, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p22"></a><b>20 </b>And Og, the king of Bashan, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p23"></a><b>21 </b>And gave their land for an heritage, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p24"></a><b>22 </b>An heritage to Israel his servant, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p25"></a><b>23 </b>Who in our humiliation remembered us, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p26"></a><b>24 </b>And rescued us from our oppressors, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p27"></a><b>25 </b>Who giveth food to all flesh, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xviii-p28"></a><b>26 </b>Make acknowledgments to the God of heavens, For to everlasting <i>endureth</i> his mercy.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xix"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p2"></a>PSALM 137</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p3"></a><b>1 </b>By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down, Yea we wept when we remembered thee, O Zion!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p4"></a><b>2 </b>Upon the willows, in the midst thereof, We hanged our harps.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p5"></a><b>3 </b>Then they required of us, they who carried us away captive, the words of a song, And, when we were in suspense, mirth, [<i>Saying</i>] Sing us one of the songs of Zion.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p6"></a><b>4 </b>How shall we sing the song of Jehovah, In a strange land?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p7"></a><b>5 </b>If I shall forget thee, O Jerusalem! Forget let my right hand [<i>its cunning</i>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p8"></a><b>6 </b>Cleave let my tongue to my palate, If I do not remember thee, If I do not raise Jerusalem above my highest joy.   				 <a name="fr_399"></a><a href="#fn_399"><font size="1">400</font></a>
 </p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Remember, O Jehovah! the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem: ‘Who said, “Lay it bare — “Lay it bare, even to the foundations thereof.”</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p11"></a><b>8 </b>O daughter of Babylon laid waste! Happy he who shall repay thee The retribution with which thou hast retributed us!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xix-p12"></a><b>9 </b>Happy he who shall take And dash thy little ones against the stones.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xx"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p2"></a>PSALM 138</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p3"></a>Of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p4"></a><b>1 </b>I will celebrate thee with my whole heart; Before the gods! will sing psalms to thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p5"></a><b>2</b> I will worship <i>thee</i> towards the temple of thy holiness, And sing to thy name for thy mercy and for thy truth; For thou hast magnified above all <i>things</i> thy name by thy word.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p6"></a><b>3 </b>In the day <i>when</i>, I cried <i>to thee</i>, then thou heardest me, Thou didst abundantly minister to me strength in my soul.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p7"></a><b>4 </b>Celebrate thee, O Jehovah! let all the kings of the earth; For they have heard the words of thy mouth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p8"></a><b>5 </b>And let them sing in the ways of Jehovah, For great is the glory of Jehovah.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p9"></a><b>6 </b>For high <i>is</i> Jehovah; yet the lowly he will regard; And being high will know afar off:</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p10"></a><b>7 </b>If I shall walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive me; Against the wrath of my enemies thou wilt put forth thy hand, And save me shall thy right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xx-p11"></a><b>8 </b>Jehovah will perform in me <i>his work</i>, O Jehovah! thy mercy is from everlasting; The works of thy hands thou wilt not forsake.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xxi"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p2"></a>PSALM 139</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p4"></a><b>1 </b>O Jehovah! thou hast searched me and known <i>me</i></p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Thou hast known my down sitting and my uprising, Thou understandest my thought afar off.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p6"></a><b>3 </b>My path and my lying down thou besiegest, And with all my ways thou art acquainted.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p7"></a><b>4 </b>For there is not a word in my tongue [<i>But</i>] lo! O God! thou knowest it altogether.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p8"></a><b>5 </b>Behind and before thou hast shut me up, And hast laid upon me thy hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p9"></a><b>6 </b>Wonderful is <i>thy</i> knowledge above me; It is high, I cannot <i>attain</i> to it.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p10"></a><b>7 </b>Whither shall I go from thy Spirit? And whither from thy time shall I flee?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p11"></a><b>8 </b>If I ascend up into the heavens, there thou art; If I lie down   				 <a name="fr_400"></a><a href="#fn_400"><font size="1">401</font></a>
  				 in the sepulcher, behold! thou [<i>art there</i>.]</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p13"></a><b>9 </b>Should I take the wings of the morning, That I may dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea,</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p14"></a><b>10 </b>Even there thy hand shall lead me, And hold me shall thy right hand.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p15"></a><b>11 </b>If I should say: “At least the darkness shall cover me;  				”  				 “And the night shall be light for me;“</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p16"></a><b>12 </b>Even the darkness shall not hide from the And the night as the day shall shine, And the darkness as the light.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p17"></a><b>13 </b>For thou hast possessed my reins; Thou hast covered me in the womb of my mother.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p18"></a><b>14 </b>I will celebrate thee; for I have been fearfully and wonderfully made:   				 <a name="fr_401"></a><a href="#fn_401"><font size="1">402</font></a>
  				 Marvelous are thy works, And my soul shall know them full well.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p20"></a><b>15 </b>Not hidden is my strength from thee, Which thou hast made in secret: I was woven together in the lowest parts of the earth.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p21"></a><b>16 </b>My shapelessness see did thine eyes;   				 <a name="fr_402"></a><a href="#fn_402"><font size="1">403</font></a>
  				 In thy book all shall be written; They were formed <i>in many</i> days, And <i>there was</i> not one of them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p23"></a><b>17 </b>And towards me how precious are thy thoughts, O God! How great <i>are</i> the sums of them!</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p24"></a><b>18 </b>If I should count them; above the sand they shall be multiplied: I am awakened, and still I am with thee.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p25"></a><b>19 </b>If thou shalt slay, O God! the wicked, Then ye men of bloods depart from me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p26"></a><b>20 </b>Who have spoken of thee wickedly: Taken thy name falsely have thy adversaries.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p27"></a><b>21 </b>Thy haters, O Jehovah! shall not I hate? And with those that rise up against thee shall I not strive?</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p28"></a><b>22 </b>With perfect hatred I have hated them, As my enemies I have held them.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p29"></a><b>23 </b>Search me, O God! and know my heart: Examine me and know my thoughts.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxi-p30"></a><b>24 </b>And know whether the way of wickedness be in me, And lead me in the way of this life.</p>  <a name="xxxv.v.xxii"></a>  			 
 <p class="Normal"><a name="xxxv.v.xxii-p1"></a>  			 
 </p><p class="HDG-C-Gr-16-Pref14"><a name="xxxv.v.xxii-p2"></a>PSALM 140</p>  			 
 <p class="PoetryLast-DkBlu-11-Cent26"><a name="xxxv.v.xxii-p3"></a>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxii-p4"></a><b>1 </b>Deliver me, O Jehovah! from the evil man: From the man of injuries do thou preserve me.</p>  			 
 <p><a name="xxxv.v.xxii-p5"></a><b>2 </b>Who devise mischiefs in <i>their</i> heart; Daily do they congregate for wars.</p>
